尼娜看着其它二年级的孩子们跑出去。他们的父母来接他们了。但是，尼娜的妈妈很晚才下班。所以，尼娜要去儿童中心。
Nina watched the other second graders run outside. Their parents were picking them up. But Nina's mom worked late. So Nina was going to Kids Central.
尼娜走进体育馆。她想回家，在后院玩儿。窗户上一个大横幅写着 “课后活动和游戏，就在儿童中心！” 
Nina walked into the gym. She wished she could go home and play in her backyard. A big banner over the windows read "After-School Fun & Games @ Kids Central!"
尼娜没有看到认识的人。她很紧张。
“哦，我的名字在那儿。” 尼娜发现了自己的名签。她坐下来。
Nina didn't see anyone she knew. She felt nervous.
"Oh, there's my name." Nina spotted a name tag with her name on it. She sat down.
莉琪来到儿童中心，非常兴奋。但是，她的名签写错了。“莉莎贝尔？” 莉琪说，“我叫莉琪，不叫莉莎贝尔！” 
莉琪看着旁边的男生。“你是贾森吧？” 
Izzie was excited to be at Kids Central. But her name tag was wrong. "Isabel?" Izzie read. "I'm Izzie, not Isabel!"
Izzie looked at the boy next to her. "You must be Jason."
“欢迎大家！请找到自己的座位。” 雪莉老师说。
雪莉老师是儿童中心的老师。尼娜觉得她的笑容很好看。“今天我们要装饰名签。” 雪莉老师说。
"Welcome, everyone! Please find your seat," Miss Shelly called.
Miss Shelly was the Kids Central teacher. Nina thought she had a nice smile. "Today we're going to decorate name tags," Miss Shelly said.
一个高高的男生坐在尼娜旁边。他没有打招呼。他的名签上写着 “波比” 。
“看一下桌子上的杂志。剪出你喜欢的图片。” 雪莉老师说。
A tall boy sat down next to Nina. He didn't say hello. But his name tag said "BOBBY."
"Look through the magazines on your table. Cut out pictures of things you like," Miss Shelly said.
“举个例子。尼娜，你喜欢什么？” 雪莉老师问。
尼娜笑了。“我喜欢紫色，还喜欢我的雨靴。” 她害羞地回答。
“很好！贾森，你喜欢什么？” 雪莉老师等了等，“贾森？” 
"For example, Nina, what do you like?" Miss Shelly asked.
Nina smiled. "I like the color purple and I like my rain boots," she answered shyly.
"Nice! Jason, what do you like?" Miss Shelly waited. "Jason?"
莉琪提醒贾森。“他喜欢玩儿电子游戏。” 她说。
“贾森，我们不在儿童中心玩儿电子游戏。请收起来。” 雪莉老师严肃地说，“除了电子游戏，你还喜欢什么？” 
Izzie poked Jason's arm. "He likes video games," she said.
"Jason, we don't play video games at Kids Central. Please put that away." Miss Shelly sounded serious. "Besides video games, what do you like?"
贾森抬起头。“芝士汉堡。” 
“很好！开始剪吧！” 雪莉老师指了指杂志。
“请把那本杂志递给我。” 尼娜说。
“请把剪刀递给我。” 波比说。
Jason looked up. "Cheeseburgers."
"Great! Start cutting!" Miss Shelly pointed to the magazines.
"Please pass me that magazine," Nina said.
"Please pass me those scissors," Bobby said.
莉琪挥了挥手。“雪莉老师？我需要一个新名签。只有我奶奶才叫我莉莎贝尔。大家都叫我莉琪。” 
Izzie waved her hand in the air. "Miss Shelly? I need a new name tag. Only my grandma calls me Isabel. Everyone calls me Izzie."
“抱歉！你可以做一个新的。” 雪莉老师给了她一些硬纸片。“在上面打两个孔。” 莉琪打了孔。“然后写上你的名字。” 
"I'm sorry! You can make a new name tag." Miss Shelly handed her some stiff paper. "Punch two holes in the top." Izzie punched. "Then write down your name."
“现在把你们剪的图片拿出来。把它们粘在名签上。你们可以粘在前面或后面，或者两面都粘。” 
"Now take all the pictures you cut out. Glue them onto your name tag. You can glue them on the front, on the back, or on both sides."
“做好以后，选一条线，把它穿进孔里。看！你的名签就变成了一条项链！” 雪莉老师把她的名签戴在脖子上。“你还可以把它挂在房间的门把上。” 
"When you're done, choose a piece of yarn. Thread it through the holes on your tag. Ta-da! Your name tag becomes a necklace!" Miss Shelly tied her name tag around her neck. "You could also hang it on your bedroom doorknob."
“尼娜，你妈妈来了。” 雪莉老师说。
尼娜很惊讶。“活动已经结束了吗？” 
“对呀，该回家了。” 妈妈说。
“再见，雪莉老师！” 尼娜跑向妈妈，“看我的名签！” 
"Nina, your mom's here," Miss Shelly called.
Nina looked surprised. "Is Kids Central over already?"
"Yep. Time to go home," her mom said.
"Bye, Miss Shelly!" Nina ran to her mom. "Look at my name tag!"
需要准备：
• 硬纸片或纸板
• 剪刀
• 打孔器
• 记号笔
• 杂志或报纸
• 胶水
• 60厘米长的线
Things You'll Need:
• stiff paper or cardboard
• scissors
• a hole puncher
• markers
• magazines or newspapers
• glue
• yarn, cut into 60 cm pieces
自己试试吧：
1) 剪出一个长方形作名签。
2) 在名签最上方打两个孔。
3) 写上名字。
4) 在杂志或报纸上剪下喜欢的图片。
5) 把图片粘在名签上。
6) 把线穿过名签的孔。
7) 把名签戴在脖子上！
Do It Yourself:
1) Cut out a rectangle to be your name tag.
2) Punch two holes in the top of the name tag.
3) Write your name.
4) Cut out pictures of things that you like from a magazine or newspaper.
5) Glue the pictures onto your name tag.
6) Thread a piece of yarn through the holes on your tag.
7) Tie your name tag around your neck!
波比放学后去了体育馆。外面在下雨，所以，今天儿童中心在室内活动。他希望可以去外面玩儿，他还希望自己带了点心。他饿了。
Bobby walked into the gym after school. It was raining. So Kids Central was inside today. He wished they could go outside and play. He also wished he had brought a snack. He was hungry.
“今天大家看上去都很累。我们做点东西吃吧。” 雪莉老师说。
“耶！” 波比说。
“我妈妈累的时候会喝咖啡。” 尼娜说。
"You guys look tired today. Let's make something to eat," Miss Shelly said.
"Yeah!" Bobby said.
"My mom makes coffee when she's tired," Nina said.
雪莉老师大笑起来。“我们要做比咖啡更好的东西。我们要做我们自己的儿童中心能量棒。大家都过来吧。” 
Miss Shelly laughed. "We're going to make something better than coffee. We're going to make our very own Kids Central energy bars. Everyone, come here."
“太酷了。我们要自己做点心了！” 波比说。
“我们要把食材混合起来。黑板上有说明。第一步：把一罐炼乳和两汤匙的油倒进碗里，搅拌。” 雪莉老师念道。
"Cool. We're making our own snack!" Bobby said.
"We'll make the mixture all together. The instructions are on the board. Step 1: Empty one can of condensed milk and two tablespoons of oil into a bowl. Stir," Miss Shelly read.
尼娜拿起一个打开的罐头。“炼乳在这里。” 
“我准备油。” 贾森加了两汤匙的油。“搅拌！” 
Nina picked up an open can on the table. "Here is the condensed milk."
"I've got the oil." Jason added two tablespoons of oil. "Stir!"
“第二步：加两杯烤燕麦片，搅拌。” 尼娜拿起一袋烤燕麦片。“两杯是多少？” 
波比给她一个量杯。“装两次。” 
“一、二。好了！” 尼娜笑了，“真好玩儿。” 
"Step 2: Add two cups of toasted oats. Stir." Nina picked up a bag of toasted oats. "How much is two cups?"
Bobby handed her a measuring cup. "Fill this up twice."
"One. Two. There!" Nina grinned. "This is fun."
“第三步：加一杯膨化小麦，搅拌。” 贾森加了一杯膨化小麦。“真酷。这很简单。” 
“第四步：加半杯杏仁片。杏仁片在哪里呢，雪莉老师？” 莉琪问。
"Step 3: Add one cup of puffed wheat. Stir." Jason added one cup of puffed wheat. "Cool. That was easy."
"Step 4: Add half a cup of chopped nuts. Where are the chopped nuts, Miss Shelly?" Izzie asked.
“给你，莉琪，杏仁片在这里。” 雪莉老师给了她一袋杏仁。莉琪把杏仁加了进去。
“第五步：加点甜味。加入巧克力碎和葡萄干。” 尼娜念道。“哦，我最喜欢葡萄干了。” 
"Here are the sliced almonds, Izzie." Miss Shelly handed her the bag of nuts. Izzie added them to the mix.
"Step 5: Make it sweet. Add chocolate chips and raisins," Nina read. "Ooh, I love raisins."
“别忘了第六步：加一杯葵花籽。” 雪莉老师提醒大家。
“别忘了搅拌、搅拌、搅拌哦！” 莉琪说。
“我在搅拌、搅拌、搅拌！” 尼娜说。
"Don't forget step 6: Add one cup of sunflower seeds," Miss Shelly reminded them.
"And don't forget to stir, stir, stir!" Izzie said.
"I am stirring, stirring, stirring!" Nina said.
“铺在抹好油的烤盘上。要怎么给烤盘抹油呢，雪莉老师？” 波比问。
“在纸巾上倒一些油。” 她回答，“然后抹在烤盘上。” 雪莉老师给了他一张纸巾。
"Spread onto a greased baking pan. How do you grease the pan, Miss Shelly?" Bobby asked.
"Pour some oil onto a paper towel," she answered. "Then rub it around the bottom of the pan." Miss Shelly gave him a paper towel.
“现在，我们要这样压一压食材。” 雪莉老师用力压了压食材。“可以烤了！” 雪莉老师把烤盘放进烤箱里。
“用175摄氏度烤25分钟。” 波比说。
"Now we press the mixture down like this." Miss Shelly pressed her palms firmly on top of the mixture. "We're ready to bake!" Miss Shelly lifted the pan into the toaster oven.
"Bake for 25 minutes at 175 degrees Celsius," Bobby said.
“那这25分钟我们做什么呢？” 贾森问。
“我们踢足球吧。女生对男生！” 波比大喊。
“耶！男生赢了！” 贾森和波比很开心。
"What will we do for 25 minutes?" Jason asked.
"Let's play soccer. Girls versus boys!" Bobby shouted.
"Yeah! Boys win!" Jason and Bobby were happy.
“嗯……我闻到了香味儿！” 波比大喊。
“是我们的点心！” 雪莉老师说，“要做最后一步了。” 
“切成小条后品尝。” 波比念道，“那就是可以吃了！我觉得室内活动也挺不错的。” 
"Mmm . . . Something smells good!" Bobby cried.
"It's our snack!" Miss Shelly said. "It's ready for the final step."
"Cut into bars and enjoy," Bobby read. "That means eat! Maybe staying inside isn't so bad after all."
雪莉老师切了12个小条。每个人都吃了一个。
“哇。我们做的点心真好吃！” 莉琪说。
“对。现在我有力气了。” 波比说，“我们再去踢足球吧！” 
Miss Shelly cut 12 bars. Everyone took an energy bar.
"Wow. We made a really good snack!" Izzie said.
"Yeah. And now I have lots of energy," added Bobby. "Let's go play more soccer!"
需要准备：
• 一罐炼乳（400克）
• 两汤匙油
• 两杯烤燕麦片
• 一杯膨化小麦（或你喜欢的不加糖麦片）
• 半杯杏仁片
• 一杯巧克力碎
• 一杯水果干
• 一杯（剥壳的）葵花籽
Things You'll Need:
- 1 can of sweetened condensed milk (400 grams)
- 2 tablespoons oil
- 2 cups toasted oats
- 1 cup puffed wheat (or your favorite unsweetened cereal)
- ½ cup chopped nuts
- 1 cup chocolate chips
- 1 cup dried fruit
- 1 cup sunflower seeds (shelled)
自己试试吧：
1) 把一罐炼乳和两汤匙的油倒进碗里，搅拌。
2) 加烤燕麦片，搅拌。
3) 加膨化小麦或麦片，搅拌。
4) 加杏仁片，搅拌。
5) 加巧克力碎和水果干，搅拌。
6) 加葵花籽，搅拌。
7) 铺在抹好油的烤盘上（30 x 20厘米），压一压。
8) 放进预热到175摄氏度的烤箱里，烤25分钟。
9) 从烤箱里拿出来，放凉。
10)  切成小条。
11)  品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Mix condensed milk and oil in large bowl. Stir.
2) Add toasted oats. Stir.
3) Add puffed wheat or cereal. Stir.
4) Add chopped nuts. Stir.
5) Add chocolate chips and dried fruit. Stir.
6) Add sunflower seeds. Stir.
7) Spread in a greased baking pan (30 x 20 cm). Press down.
8) Place in preheated oven at 175˚C. Bake for 25 minutes.
9) Remove from oven. Let cool.
10) Cut into bars.
11) Enjoy!
贾森正在玩儿电子游戏。这时，有人拍了拍他的肩膀。
“贾森。” 雪莉老师说，“我说过在儿童中心不能玩儿电子游戏……” 
Jason was playing video game when someone tapped him on the shoulder.
"Jason," Miss Shelly said. "I've warned you about video games in Kids Central . . ."
“对不起，雪莉老师。” 贾森小声回答。他看到自己被大白鲨吃掉了。
“大家带塑料垃圾袋和报纸来了吗？” 雪莉老师问。
"Sorry, Miss Shelly," Jason mumbled. He looked down and saw himself get eaten by the shark.
"Did everyone bring in a plastic garbage bag and a newspaper?" Miss Shelly asked.
“带了。但这些是拿来做什么的呢？” 尼娜很好奇。
“这是一个秘密。” 雪莉老师说。她的双眼放光。“请大家从桌子上拿两只彩笔和一把尺子。放到袋子里，跟我出去吧！” 
"Yes. But what are they for?" Nina wanted to know.
"It's a secret," Miss Shelly said, her eyes twinkling. "Everyone, grab two paint pens and a ruler from the table. Toss them in your bags and follow me outside!"
雪莉老师带着学生们来到野餐桌旁。
“有这些野餐桌很好。但是，如果我们想坐在那棵树下，或者坐在没有野餐桌的公园里呢？” 
孩子们看着她。
Miss Shelly led the class to the picnic tables.
"We're lucky we have these tables. But what if we wanted to sit under that tree over there? Or in a park that doesn't have tables?"
The kids stared at her.
“地是湿的。” 雪莉老师暗示他们。
“我们就会变湿。” 波比说。
“我们需要垫子！” 莉琪马上回答。
“对！我们需要坐垫！” 雪莉老师说。
"The ground is all wet," Miss Shelly hinted.
"We'd get all wet," Bobby said.
"We'd need something to sit on!" Izzie burst out.
"Yes! We'd need something like a sit-upon!" Miss Shelly said.
“今天我们就要制作坐垫。除了报纸，把袋子里的所有东西都拿出来。首先，我们要把垃圾袋剪小一点。” 
"Today we're going to make sit-upons. Take everything out of your bag except for the newspaper. First we have to cut your garbage bags to make them smaller."
“让报纸滑到袋子底部。从报纸边缘开始量十厘米，然后剪下多余的部分。” 雪莉老师给每个人分剪刀。
"Let your newspaper slide all the way to the bottom of the bag. Measure about ten centimeters from the end of the newspaper. Then cut off the extra part." Miss Shelly handed out scissors.
“量一量。” 波比说。他把尺子放在袋子上。
“剪下来。” 尼娜剪短袋子。
“好了！” 莉琪拿起袋子说。
"Measure," Bobby said, placing a ruler on his bag.
"Cut," Nina said, cutting her bag.
"Done!" Izzie said, holding up her bag.
“现在像包礼物一样把开口折起来。然后用胶带粘上。小心，胶带很黏的！” 
"Now fold the loose side, like you're wrapping a present. Then tape with duct tape. Be careful. Duct tape is very sticky!"
贾森双臂交叉，看上去很不开心。
“贾森，你怎么了？” 雪莉老师问。
“我不喜欢做这个手工。” 他生气地说。
“为什么呢？” 雪莉老师皱了皱眉头。
Jason sat with his arms crossed, looking unhappy.
"What's the matter, Jason?" Miss Shelly asked.
"I don't like this craft," he said grumpily.
"Why not?" Miss Shelly frowned.
“我妈妈给了我一个粉红色的垃圾袋！我讨厌粉红色！” 贾森把袋子推开。
“哦，贾森。粉红色也很好呀。但是如果你想换一个……让我想想……有人想和贾森换袋子吗？” 
"My mom gave me a pink garbage bag! I hate pink!" Jason pushed his bag away from him.
"Oh, Jason. Pink is a great color. But if you want a different bag . . . Let's see . . . Does anyone want to trade bags with Jason?"
“我！” 莉琪跳了起来，“我喜欢粉红色！” 
“谢谢你，莉琪。你的袋子是什么颜色的？” 雪莉老师问。
“灰色。可以吗？” 莉琪看着贾森。
“灰色是我最喜欢的颜色。” 贾森咧嘴笑了。
"I do!" Izzie jumped up. "I love pink!"
"Thank you, Izzie. What color is your bag?" Miss Shelly asked.
"Gray. Is that okay?" Izzie looked at Jason.
"Gray is my favorite color." Jason grinned.
“问题解决了。现在我们要在坐垫上画画了！” 雪莉老师对孩子们说。“用彩笔装饰你的坐垫吧！一定要写上你的名字。这样就完成了！” 
"Problem solved. Now everyone is going to paint their sit-upons!" Miss Shelly turned to the kids. "Use your paint pens to decorate your sit-upon any way you'd like! Make sure to put your name on it. Then you're all done!"
“哇，贾森。你做得太酷了。” 莉琪说。贾森在他的坐垫上画了一只大白鲨。
“谢谢。好像还可以。如果是画在粉红色的袋子上就很奇怪了！” 他说。
"Wow, Jason. That's cool," Izzie said. Jason had drawn a great white shark on his sit-upon.
"Thanks. I guess it's okay. But it would have looked dumb on a pink bag!" he said.
需要准备：
-报纸
-塑料垃圾袋
-尺子
-剪刀
-胶带
-彩笔或者涂料
Things You'll Need:
- a newspaper
- a plastic garbage bag
- a ruler
- scissors
- duct tape
- paint pens or paint
自己试试吧：
1） 把报纸放在垃圾袋最底部。
2） 从报纸边缘开始量十厘米。
3） 剪下多余的部分。
4） 把剪短的一边折下来粘好。
5） 装饰坐垫。
6） 拿着坐垫坐在自己喜欢的地方！
Do It Yourself:
1) Put the newspaper in the bottom of your garbage bag.
2) Measure ten centimeters from the end of the newspaper.
3) Cut off the extra part.
4) Fold the cut side of the garbage bag and tape it down.
5) Decorate your sit-upon.
6) Sit on it anywhere you'd like!
莉琪和尼娜在荡秋千。她们是几个星期前在儿童中心认识的。莉琪喜欢尼娜。
“秋天是我最喜欢的季节。” 莉琪说。
“是啊，我也喜欢秋天。” 尼娜说。
Izzie and Nina were swinging high on the swings. They had just met at Kids Central a few weeks ago. But Izzie liked Nina.
"Fall is my favorite season," Izzie said.
"Yeah. I love fall too," Nina agreed.
“孩子们！来拿你们的坐垫。你们很快就要用到了！” 雪莉老师喊道。
儿童中心的活动时间到了。
“不知道今天我们要做什么。” 莉琪说。
"Girls! Come get your sit-upons. You'll need them soon!" Miss Shelly called.
It was time for the Kids Central activity of the day.
"I wonder what we're doing," Izzie said.
雪莉老师拿着一个棕色的纸袋。她穿着靴子。“我们要去树林里了！” 她说。
大家跟着雪莉老师走进了一条小路。小路通往树林。
Miss Shelly was holding a brown paper bag. She wore tall rubber boots. "Out to the woods we go!" she said.
Everyone followed Miss Shelly onto a path. The path went into the woods.
“到了。” 雪莉老师说，“这是我们今天的露营地。” 
“我们在这里做什么？” 莉琪问。
“我们可以随便放坐垫吗？” 波比问。
“当然可以。” 雪莉老师回答。
"Here we are," Miss Shelly said. "Our campground for the day."
"What are we doing here?" Izzie asked.
"Can we put our sit-upons anywhere?" Bobby asked.
"Sure," Miss Shelly answered.
雪莉老师把纸袋的东西倒到地上。“今天，我们要用火、棉花糖、巧克力和全麦饼干。有谁可以猜到我们要做什么吗？” 
“全麦饼干三明治！” 波比大喊，“我的最爱！” 
Miss Shelly emptied her shopping bag onto the ground. "For today's activity we'll use a fire, marshmallows, chocolate, and graham crackers. Can anyone guess what it is?"
"S'mores!" Bobby yelled. "My favorite!"
“一定很好吃！我们家去露营的时候就会做全麦饼干三明治。” 尼娜说。
“什么是全麦饼干三明治？” 莉琪问。
“什么是全麦饼干三明治？” 尼娜惊讶地又问了一次。
“莉琪，你今天要尝到好吃的啦！” 雪莉老师笑了。
"Yum! My family makes s'mores when we go camping," Nina said.
"What's a s'more?" Izzie asked.
"What's a s'more?" Nina repeated, shocked.
"You're in for a treat today, Izzie." Miss Shelly smiled.
“我要先生火。你们每个人找一根细细长长的树枝，然后清理一下。” 雪莉老师说。
“哦，这根不错！” 尼娜边说边清理一根长树枝。
"First I'll make the fire. You should each find a long, skinny stick. Brush off any dirt," Miss Shelly instructed.
"Oh, I found a perfect one!" Nina said, brushing off a long stick.
“我们用这个烤棉花糖。” 贾森告诉莉琪。
“对，把棉花糖插在树枝上。像这样。” 波比做给莉琪看。
"We use these to roast the marshmallows," Jason told Izzie.
"Yep. You put the marshmallow on the end of your stick. Like this." Bobby showed Izzie how to stab the marshmallow.
莉琪举起树枝。“好了。现在呢？” 
“现在我们来烤棉花糖吧！” 雪莉老师说，“小心地把树枝放在火的上方，而不是火里。” 
Izzie held up her stick. "Okay, now what?"
"Now let's roast these marshmallows!" Miss Shelly said. "Hold your stick carefully over the fire, but not in the fire."
“我喜欢黏糊糊的棉花糖。那样最好吃。” 尼娜说。
“才不是呢。烤焦、脆皮的才最好吃。” 波比说。
莉琪尖叫起来。“雪莉老师！我的棉花糖着火了！” 
"I like mine gooey and dripping. That's the best," Nina said.
"No way. Totally burnt and crispy on the outside is the best," Bobby said.
Izzie screamed. "Miss Shelly! My marshmallow is on fire!"
“别担心，莉琪。像吹生日蜡烛一样吹灭它就可以了。” 雪莉老师拿起莉琪的树枝，把火吹灭了。
“这就是全麦饼干三明治吗？” 莉琪拿着烤焦的棉花糖问。
"Don't worry, Izzie. Just blow it out, like a birthday candle." Miss Shelly calmly took Izzie's stick and blew out the small flame.
"So this is a s'more?" Izzie asked, holding up her burnt marshmallow.
“还不是。现在我们要拿两片全麦饼干。” 尼娜说。
“还有一块巧克力。” 贾森补充说。
“把巧克力放在一片全麦饼干上。再把棉花糖放在巧克力上。” 波比做给她看。
"Not yet. Now we take two graham crackers," Nina said.
"And a piece of chocolate," Jason added.
"Put your chocolate on one graham cracker. And put your marshmallow on top of the chocolate." Bobby showed her how.
“把另外一片全麦饼干放在上面，像三明治一样。然后压一下。” 尼娜压了压自己的三明治。融化的巧克力流了出来。莉琪和尼娜哈哈大笑。
“全麦饼干三明治真好吃！” 莉琪擦了擦嘴上的棉花糖。
"Then put your other graham cracker on top, like a sandwich. And squish it together." Nina squished her sandwich. Melted chocolate dripped out of one side. Izzie and Nina laughed.
"S'mores are so good!" Izzie wiped marshmallow off her lips.
“好吃吧？正适合在秋天吃。” 雪莉老师笑着说。
莉琪看了看四周，然后她看了看自己的新朋友尼娜。雪莉老师说得对。一切都太完美了。
"Aren't they? They're perfect for a fall day." Miss Shelly smiled.
Izzie looked around, then she looked at her new friend Nina. Miss Shelly was right. Everything was perfectly perfect.
需要准备：
-篝火（户外）或者煤气炉（室内）
-一袋棉花糖
-细细长长的树枝
-巧克力块
-一盒全麦饼干
Things You'll Need:
- a fire (outside) or a gas stove (inside)
- a bag of large marshmallows
- a long, skinny stick
- a chocolate bar
- a box of graham crackers
自己试试吧：
1） 叫大人帮忙生火或者点煤气炉。
2） 把棉花糖插在树枝上。
3） 在火上烤棉花糖。
4） 把一块巧克力放在全麦饼干上。
5） 把烤好的棉花糖放在巧克力上。
6） 把另外一片全麦饼干放在棉花糖上。
7） 把三明治压一压。
8） 品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Ask an adult to start a fire or light the stove.
2) Place a marshmallow on the end of the stick.
3) Roast the marshmallow over the fire.
4) Put a piece of chocolate on a graham cracker.
5) Put the roasted marshmallow on the chocolate.
6) Put another graham cracker on top of the marshmallow.
7) Squish the sandwich together.
8) Enjoy!
波比在打篮球。他假装自己是高中篮球队“老鹰” 里的一员。
雪莉老师在做活动准备。“希望活动会有趣。” 波比想。他还想继续打篮球。

Miss Shelly was getting ready to start an activity. "It'd better be fun," Bobby thought. He didn't want to stop playing basketball.
雪莉老师准备了一盒粉笔和一个球。她吹了吹哨子。“大家都过来吧！” 她喊道。
“我要和莉琪一队！” 尼娜大喊。

波比知道四方格游戏，他的姐姐们玩儿过。今天的活动一定很有趣。
"We're going to play a game. It's called Four Square," Miss Shelly said.
Bobby knew Four Square. His sisters played it. Kids Central was going to be fun today.
“谁玩儿过四方格游戏？” 雪莉老师问。
只有波比举手。“我一定最厉害！” 他想。

Only Bobby raised his hand. "I'm going to be the best!" he thought.

波比画了一个大方格，然后把它分成四个小方格。他写上数字1、2、3、4。
"Bobby, would you draw a Four Square board for us?" Miss Shelly asked. She held out the chalk.
Bobby drew a large square and then divided it into four smaller squares. He numbered them 1, 2, 3, 4.
“我一开始把球传给波比。” 雪莉老师说道，“球必须在我的方格里弹一次才能进入波比的方格。如果球碰到线，我就出局了。” 
"I start by passing the ball to Bobby," explained Miss Shelly. "The ball must bounce once in my square and then go into Bobby's. If the ball lands on any line, I am out.
“波比必须用手拍球，让球弹到另外一个方格里。如果他做不到，他就出局。 如果球弹到大方格外面，没有弹到其他方格里面，他也出局。如果他接住了球，他也出局。” 
"Bobby must hit the ball with his hands and bounce the ball to another square. If he doesn't, he is out. If the ball goes out of the big square without bouncing in any square, he is out. If he catches the ball, he is out.
“如果波比出局，他就走到1号方格。1号方格的人移到2号方格，以此类推。我们会玩儿五分钟。最后在4号方格的人就赢了！” 
"If Bobby is out, he will go to square 1. The person in square 1 will move to square 2, and so on. We will play for five minutes. Whoever is in square 4 at the end wins!
“波比，你在1号方格。莉琪，2号方格。贾森，3号方格。尼娜，4号方格。” 
“这不公平！” 波比大喊，“我会输的！” 
“这是随机安排的，波比。” 雪莉老师回答，“从4号方格开始。尼娜，给你！” 
"Bobby, you're in square 1. Izzie, square 2. Jason, 3. Nina, 4."
"That's not fair!" Bobby cried. "I'm going to lose!"
"It's random, Bobby," Miss Shelly replied. "Square 4 starts. Here you go, Nina!"
“准备好了吗？” 尼娜说。大家点点头。她把球弹给贾森。
贾森把球弹给莉琪。莉琪把球弹给波比。波比把球弹回给莉琪，但是莉琪没拍到！
"Ready?" Nina said. Everyone nodded. She bounced the ball to Jason.
Jason bounced the ball to Izzie. Izzie bounced the ball to Bobby. Bobby bounced the ball back to Izzie. But she missed!

尼娜把球弹给贾森。

Nina bounced the ball to Jason.

波比很着急。他需要让尼娜出局才能赢，但是，没有人把球弹给他！

需要准备：
-一片空地
-粉笔
-大的、有弹性的球
Things you'll need:
- an open space
- chalk
- a large, bouncy ball
游戏规则：
1. 当球进入你的方格时，你必须拍球，并让它弹到另外一个方格里。
2. 如果没有拍到球，你就出局了。
3. 如果接住了球，你就出局了。
4. 如果球碰到线，你就出局了。
5. 如果球弹到大方格外面，没有弹到其他方格里面，你就出局了。
6. 如果球在你的方格里弹了两次，你就出局了。
7. 出局的人移到1号方格，1号方格的人移到2号方格，以此类推。
8. 4号方格的人不移动，除非出局。
9. 最后在4号方格的人赢！
The Rules of Four Square:
1. When the ball enters your square, you must hit it and bounce it into another square.
2. If you miss the ball, you're out.
3. If you catch the ball, you're out.
4. If you bounce the ball on a line, you're out.
5. If you hit the ball out of the big square without bouncing it in any square first, you're out.
6. If the ball bounces twice in your square, you're out.
7. When you are out, you move to square 1. The person in square 1 moves to square 2, and so on.
8. The person in square 4 does not move unless he or she is out.
9. The person in square 4 at the end wins!
尼娜从背包里拿出她的围裙。雪莉老师让孩子们都带围裙来。

需要准备：
-切成两半的面包圈或切成厚片的面包
-披萨酱（或番茄酱）
-碎芝士
-切好的蔬菜或肉等配料
Things You'll Need:
- small (or regular) bagels sliced in half or thickly sliced bread
- pizza sauce (or tomato sauce)
- shredded cheese
- a topping such as chopped vegetables or meat
自己试试吧：
1) 请大人帮忙把面包圈切成两半。
2) 在面包圈上涂披萨酱。
3) 在酱上撒碎芝士。
4) 在芝士上面撒上你最喜欢的配料。
5) 放进烤箱，用180摄氏度烤5分钟。
6) 品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Ask an adult to slice the bagels in half.
2) Spread pizza sauce over each bagel half.
3) Sprinkle cheese on top of the sauce.
4) Sprinkle your favorite topping on the cheese.
5) Place in the toaster oven and bake at 180˚ C for 5 minutes.
6) Enjoy!

"My face is 17 centimeters long and 12 centimeters wide," Jason said.
"So your head is bigger. But I bet you can fit your head through this little index card." Miss Shelly held up her card.
“什么？不可能！” 贾森说。
“这不可能。” 波比说。
“雪莉老师一定可以。” 莉琪看着自己最喜欢的老师，笑着说。
"What? No way!" Jason said.
"Impossible," Bobby said.
"I bet Miss Shelly can do it," Izzie said. She smiled at her favorite teacher.
“我要给你们看一个小招数。” 雪莉老师说。
“是魔术吗？” 贾森问。
“不是魔术，是小招数。” 她回答。
"Well, I'll show you a trick," Miss Shelly said.
"A magic trick?" Jason asked.
"Not a magic trick. A real trick," she answered.
“第一步：把卡片上下对折。第二步：在卡片一边剪13刀。” 
每个人都小心地剪着。
“第三步：在另外一边剪13刀。” 
"Step 1: Fold your card in half from top to bottom. Step 2: Make 13 small cuts on one side of your card."
Everyone cut carefully.
"Step 3: Make 13 small cuts on the other side of your card.
“第四步：小心地打开卡片，沿着中间的折痕剪开。但是，不要剪开第一个和最后一个折痕。变成什么了？” 
贾森打开卡片。他的眼睛睁大了。“哇！真大。我的头可以穿过去！” 
"Step 4: Carefully unfold your card and cut along the fold. But do not cut the first edge or the last edge. What do you have?"
Jason unfolded his card. His eyes opened wide. "Wow! It's huge. And my head fits through it!"
“但它还是一个普通的卡片。” 雪莉老师把她的卡片合起来。
“这个招数真酷，雪莉老师。” 贾森说，“您可以教我们更多的招数吗？” 
"But it's still just a regular index card." Miss Shelly put her card back together.
"That's a cool trick, Miss Shelly," Jason said. "Will you teach us more like that?"
“当然了。但是现在你爸爸在等你了。” 她指了指门口。
“爸爸！” 贾森跳起来。“想看一个很酷的招数吗？我可以把头穿过卡片！” 
"Sure. But right now I think your dad's waiting for you." She pointed to the door.
"Dad!" Jason jumped up. "Want to see a cool trick? I can put my head through an index card!"
需要准备：
-8 x 13厘米的卡片
-剪刀
Things You'll Need:
- an index card or any 8 x 13 cm piece of paper
- scissors
自己试试吧：
1） 跟朋友说能让自己的头穿过小卡片。
2） 把卡片上下对折。
3） 在卡片一边剪13刀。小心不要剪断卡片。
4） 在另外一边剪13刀。小心不要剪断卡片。
5） 打开卡片，沿着折痕剪开。但是，不要剪开第一个和最后一个折痕。
6） 把头穿过卡片，让大家都吓一跳吧！
Do it Yourself:
1) Tell your friend that you can stick your head through an index card.
2) Fold the card in half from top to bottom.
3) Make 13 small cuts on one side of the card. Be careful not to cut through the card.
4) Make 13 small cuts on the other side of the card. Be careful not to cut through the card.
5) Unfold the card and cut along the fold. Do not cut the first edge or the last edge.
6) Amaze everyone by sticking your head through an index card!
莉琪看着窗外。外面又阴又冷。但没有下雪。两周后就是圣诞节。莉琪希望是一个白色圣诞节。她闭上眼睛，祈祷下雪。
Izzie looked out the window. It looked cold and gray outside. But there was no snow. Christmas was only two weeks away. Izzie hoped it would be a white Christmas. She closed her eyes and wished for snow.

“太好了。” 莉琪说。她喜欢做手工。雪莉老师准备的活动都很有趣。

"Oh good," said Izzie. She loved crafts. And Miss Shelly always had fun ideas.

"Is that a paper plate?" Jason asked.

“哦！” 尼娜和莉琪同时看到了天使。“是我的！” 她们同时伸手拿天使。
“尼娜，我真的很想要这个。” 莉琪说。
“我也是，莉琪。” 尼娜说。

“我们应该分享吗？” 尼娜问雪莉老师。

"Should we share it?" Nina asked, looking at Miss Shelly.
"You two girls are smart. I'm sure you'll figure something out," Miss Shelly said.
"Share it?" Izzie repeated. "How do you share an angel?"
“我们可以把它剪成两半。” 尼娜说。
莉琪很想哭。她可不想要半个天使。半个天使一点也不好看。她想要整个天使。
"I guess we could cut it in half," Nina said.
Izzie felt like crying. She didn't want half of the angel. Half of the angel would not be beautiful. She wanted the whole angel.
“没关系。” 莉琪小声说，“给尼娜吧。” 尼娜拿走天使的时候，她看着其他地方。
“谢谢你，莉琪。” 雪莉老师说，“你很棒。” 
"It's okay," Izzie said quietly. "Nina can have it." She looked away as Nina took the ornament.

莉琪看到尼娜的花环放在地板上晾干。花环看上去很不错。
“请让天下雪吧。” 莉琪小声地对天使说。
他们在等花环变干。雪莉老师拿出铃铛。他们一边摇铃铛一边唱圣诞歌。
Izzie saw Nina's wreath drying on the floor. It looked good.
"Please make it snow," Izzie whispered to the angel.
While their wreaths were drying, Miss Shelly brought out a bucket of jingle bells. They sang holiday songs and shook their bells.
很快就到了回家的时间。
“莉琪，花环真可爱！” 莉琪的妈妈说。她和尼娜的妈妈正拿着花环。
“莉琪，快来看！” 尼娜突然大喊。
Soon it was time to go home.

"Izzie, come look!" Nina suddenly shouted.
莉琪跑到窗边。她不敢相信自己的眼睛。

Izzie ran to the window. She couldn't believe it.
It was snowing! Her wish had come true. She looked at Nina's wreath and silently thanked the angel. Then she turned to Nina. "Let's go out and play!"

自己试试吧：

Do it Yourself:
1) Fold a paper plate in half.
2) Cut a half circle out of the middle of the plate.
3) Unfold the plate and paint it with your favorite holiday color.
4) Glue paper ornaments or holiday pictures on the wreath.
5) Add ribbons or other decorations.
6) Let the wreath dry on a flat surface.
7) Hang the wreath on a door for holiday cheer!
波比打开体育馆的门。贾森、尼娜和莉琪已经到了。雪莉老师正在发吸汗带。

"We are exercising," Miss Shelly answered.

"We're doing a different kind of exercise," she said. "Today we'll exercise our brains!"
孩子们互相看着对方。“大脑？我们今天要做数学题吗？” 尼娜皱着眉头问。波比叹了口气。

尼娜选了一张卡片看了看。她笑了。“我选波比。” 她说。
"Here, Nina," Miss Shelly said. "Pick a card and read the brain teaser to yourself. Then choose someone to answer it."
Nina took a card and read it silently. Then she grinned. "I choose Bobby," she said.
“太平洋的中间是什么？” 尼娜问。
“很简单，海水。” 波比回答。
尼娜哈哈大笑。“不对，是 ‘平’。太-平-洋，中间是 ‘平’。明白了吗？” 她对雪莉老师笑了笑。“真好玩儿。” 
"What's in the middle of the Pacific Ocean?" Nina asked.
"That's easy; seawater," Bobby answered.
Nina burst into giggles. "Nope. It's 'ping.' Pacific Ocean, 'Tai-ping-yang'; the middle of it is 'ping.' Get it?" She smiled at Miss Shelly. "This is fun."
“好了，波比，下一个是你。选一张卡片吧。” 雪莉老师说。
波比选了一张卡片看了看。“贾森！” 他说，“什么东西只会往上，不会往下？” 
"Okay, Bobby, you're next. Pick a card," Miss Shelly said.
Bobby took a card and read it. "Jason!" he said, turning to his friend. "What goes up but never comes down?"
贾森耸耸肩。“热气球？云？” 
“只能有一个答案！” 波比说。
“好吧，云。” 
“不，是年龄！” 波比在贾森面前挥了挥卡片。
Jason shrugged. "A hot air balloon? Clouds?"
"You can only have one answer!" Bobby said.
"Okay, clouds."
"Nope. Your age!" Bobby waved the card in front of Jason.
“轮到我了。” 贾森说。他从桶里选了一张卡。“这个问题不错。” 他对莉琪说，“什么东西在雨里不会变得更湿？” 
莉琪想了想。“雨伞？” 她说。
"My turn," Jason said, taking a card out of the bucket. "Aha! This is a good one." He turned to Izzie. "What doesn't get any wetter, even in the rain?"
Izzie thought for a moment. "An umbrella?" she said.
“不，是水！” 贾森开心地说。
“好吧，到我了。尼娜，天气越热，爬得越高的东西是什么？” 莉琪问。
"No. Water!" Jason said happily.
"Okay. Here I go. Nina, what goes higher when it's hotter?" Izzie asked.
“太阳当空照……” 尼娜开始轻轻地唱起歌来。“是太阳！” 她大喊。
“不，答案是温度计。” 莉琪说。
"The sun is high in the sky. . . ," Nina began to sing softly. "The sun!" she cried.
"No, the answer is a thermometer," Izzie said.
“雪莉老师，轮到您了！” 贾森说。
“好，开始了。” 雪莉老师选了一张卡片，闭上眼睛，转了一圈。当她停下来的时候，她正对着波比。
"Miss Shelly, now it's your turn!" Jason said.
"Okay. Here I go." Miss Shelly took a card, closed her eyes, and spun around in a circle. When she stopped, she was facing Bobby.
“波比。” 雪莉老师说，“什么布剪不断？” 
波比想了想。“什么布剪不断？” 他重复着。
"Bobby," Miss Shelly said. "What kind of cloth can not be cut?"
Bobby thought. "What kind of cloth(布) can not be cut?" he repeated to himself.
“抹布、拖布、瀑布！雪莉老师，答案是瀑布！” 波比说。
雪莉老师拍手笑了。“非常棒！” 她说，“你答对了。” 
"Rag(抹布), mop(拖布), waterfall(瀑布)! Miss Shelly, the answer is waterfall(瀑布)!" Bobby said.
Miss Shelly clapped her hands and laughed. "Well done!" she said. "You got it."
“这些脑筋急转弯很难。” 尼娜说，“我的头都疼了！” 
“雪莉老师，我可以把这些卡片带回家吗？” 波比问，“我要学会世上所有的脑筋急转弯！” 
"These were hard brain teasers," Nina said. "My head hurts!"
"Miss Shelly, can I take home the brain-teaser bucket?" Bobby asked. "I'm going to learn every brain teaser in the world!"
需要准备：
-脑筋急转弯
-卡片
-一个桶
Things You'll Need:
- brain teasers
- cards
- a bucket
自己试试吧：
1） 在网上或者书上找到脑筋急转弯。
2） 在卡片上写下二十个脑筋急转弯和答案，放在桶里。
3） 一个人从桶里选一张卡片，然后选一个人回答。
4） 有人选你时，试着猜出答案，锻炼大脑！
Do It Yourself:
1) Look up brain teasers for kids on the Internet or in a book.
2) Write about twenty brain teasers and their answers on cards and place them in a bucket.
3) Someone should choose a card from the bucket and then pick someone else to answer the brain teaser.
4) When someone chooses you, try to guess the correct answer, and exercise your brain!

1） 决定谁来摇绳子。
2） 摇绳子的两个人各拿住绳子的一边。
3） 跳的人站在绳子旁边，当绳子碰到地上时跳进去。
4） 边跳边唱你们最喜欢的歌！
Do It Yourself:
1) Decide who will be the turners.
2) Each turner holds one end of the rope.
3) The jumper stands on the side and jumps in when the rope is hitting the ground.
4) While the jumper is jumping, chant your favorite jump-rope rhyme!
“大家请注意，因为大雪，今天学校两点放学。” 广播里传出弗拉尼校长的声音，“希望大家能够安全回家。” 
"Attention, students and teachers. Because of heavy snow, we will close the school at two o'clock today," Ms. Folani's voice announced over the loudspeaker. "We want everyone to get home safely."
尼娜在二年级教室里想：“今天还会有儿童中心活动吗？” 
贾森在三年级教室里也在想同样的事。
In her second-grade room, Nina wondered, "Will we have Kids Central today?"
In his third-grade room, Jason wondered the same thing.
就在这时，雪莉老师从门口把头伸了进来。“今天儿童中心两点开始活动。大家一直待到父母来接你们，好吗？” 她说。
贾森点点头，波比竖起大拇指。
Just then Miss Shelly stuck her head in the door. "We'll start Kids Central at two today. You'll stay until your parents arrive to pick you up, okay?" she said.
Jason nodded. Bobby gave her a thumbs-up sign.
“尼娜、莉琪、波比，你们的妈妈刚刚打电话过来。她们四点到。” 雪莉老师说，“我们有足够的活动时间。你们带围裙来了吗？” 
“我爸爸呢？” 贾森问，“他什么时候来？” 
"Nina, Izzie, and Bobby, your moms just called. They will be here at four o'clock," Miss Shelly said. "That gives us just enough time for our activity. Did you all bring your aprons?"
"What about my dad?" Jason asked. "When is he coming?"
贾森的爸爸每个星期三都来接他。然后他们会一起去吃披萨。
“你爸爸还没有打电话过来。但是别担心，他一定会像平时一样五点到的。” 雪莉老师说。
Jason's dad always picked him up on Wednesdays. And they always went out for pizza afterward.
"I haven't gotten a call from your dad yet. But don't worry, I'm sure he'll come at five o'clock as usual," Miss Shelly said.
“今天我们要做雪花巧克力蛋糕。” 雪莉老师说。
“耶！巧克力蛋糕。” 莉琪说，“但什么是雪花巧克力蛋糕呢？” 
贾森没有听到雪莉老师的回答。他还在想自己的爸爸。为什么他还没有打电话来呢？
"Today we'll bake snow brownies," said Miss Shelly.
"Yay! Brownies," Izzie said. "But what's a snow brownie?"
Jason didn't hear Miss Shelly's answer. He was still thinking about his dad. Why hadn't he called?
“第一步：把烤箱预热到175摄氏度。贾森，你可以帮忙吗？” 雪莉老师问。
“什么？哦，好的。” 贾森在烤箱上设置了温度。
"Step 1: Preheat the oven to 175 degrees Celsius. Jason, would you do that?" Miss Shelly asked.
"What? Oh, okay." Jason set the temperature on the oven.
“第二步：在烤盘上抹油。雪莉老师，这次可以让我抹油吗？” 尼娜问。
“当然可以。给你油和纸巾。” 老师说，“谁要念第三步？” 
"Step 2: Grease a baking pan. Miss Shelly, can I grease the pan this time?" Nina asked.
"Of course. Here is some oil and a paper towel," the teacher said. "Who will read step 3?"
“我！第三步：把融化的黄油和糖混合起来。请给我糖。” 莉琪伸手拿糖。
“第四步。” 波比念道，“加入鸡蛋和香草香精。” 
"Me! Step 3: Beat the melted butter and sugar. Sugar, please." Izzie held out her hand for the sugar.
"Step 4," Bobby read. "Beat in eggs and vanilla."
“第五步：加入可可粉和面粉。你好呀，贾森！你可以把面粉倒进去吗？” 尼娜问。
“第六步：加入盐和发酵粉。” 莉琪加入盐和发酵粉。
"Step 5: Stir in cocoa powder and flour. Hellooo, Jason! Can you pour the flour?" Nina asked.
"Step 6: Stir in salt and baking powder." Izzie added the salt and baking powder.
“可以烤了！” 雪莉老师把烤盘放进烤箱。“等27分钟就可以了。” 
这段时间，孩子们量了一下窗户上的积雪。“这里是12厘米！” 莉琪大喊。
"We're ready to bake!" Miss Shelly lifted the pan into the oven. "These should be done in about 27 minutes."
While the brownies baked, the kids measured the snow that had collected on the windows. "12 centimeters here!" Izzie cried.
“现在该把它们变成雪花巧克力蛋糕了。” 雪莉老师说。
孩子们把纸做的雪花放在烤盘上方。雪莉老师在上面撒上糖粉。当孩子们把纸拿走时，蛋糕上就有了漂亮的雪花图案。
"Time to turn these into snow brownies," Miss Shelly called.
Each kid placed a paper snowflake over the baking pan. Miss Shelly shook powdered sugar on top. When the kids lifted the paper snowflakes, there was a pretty snow pattern.
五点多了。大家都走了以后，雪莉老师和贾森清理桌子，洗了碗。他们又一起看了一本书。六点的时候，体育馆的门开了。
“好香啊。” 一个男人说。
Five o'clock came and went. After everyone left, Miss Shelly and Jason cleaned the tables and washed the dishes. Then they read a book together. Finally, at six o'clock, the gym door opened.
"What is that delicious smell?" a man asked.
“爸爸！” 贾森跳起来，跑向爸爸。
“对不起，我来晚了。我在开会，不能用手机。” 他的爸爸说，“准备好回家了吗？今天雪太大，我们不能去吃披萨了。” 
“没关系。我们可以吃巧克力蛋糕！” 贾森说。
"Dad!" Jason jumped up and ran to his father.
"Sorry I'm late. I was in a meeting and couldn't use my phone," his dad said. "Ready to go home? I'm afraid it's too snowy for pizza."
"That's okay. We can have brownies for dinner!" Jason said.
需要准备：
-油和纸巾
-半杯黄油
-一杯糖
-两个鸡蛋
-一茶匙香草香精
-三分之一杯无糖可可粉
-半杯面粉
-四分之一茶匙盐
-四分之一茶匙发酵粉
-糖粉
-纸雪花
Things You'll Need:
- oil and a paper towel
- 1/2 cup butter
- 1 cup sugar
- 2 eggs
- 1 teaspoon vanilla
- 1/3 cup unsweetened cocoa powder
- 1/2 cup flour
- 1/4 teaspoon salt
- 1/4 teaspoon baking powder
- powdered sugar
- a paper snowflake
自己试试吧：
1) 把烤箱预热到175摄氏度。
2) 在20 x 20厘米的烤盘上抹油。
3) 把融化的黄油和糖混合起来。
4) 加入鸡蛋和香草香精。
5) 加入可可粉和面粉。
6) 加入盐和发酵粉。
7) 把面糊倒到抹完油的烤盘上。
8) 烤25到30分钟。
9) 如果你想要的话，可以在烤盘上方放纸雪花，撒上糖粉。然后移开纸雪花。
10)  切成四方形。
11)  品尝美食！
Do it Yourself:
1) Preheat oven to 175˚C.
2) Grease a 20 x 20 cm pan.
3) Beat melted butter and sugar.
4) Beat in eggs and vanilla.
5) Stir in cocoa and flour.
6) Stir in salt and baking powder.
7) Pour batter into greased pan.
8) Bake for 25 to 30 minutes.
9) If you'd like, place a paper snowflake over the pan and sift powdered sugar over it. Remove the paper snowflake when you're done.
10) Cut into squares.
11) Enjoy!
莉琪躺在雪地上。她和尼娜在做雪天使。雪莉老师正在准备儿童中心的活动。天空很晴朗。莉琪看到一只红色的小鸟停在树枝上。“唧唧唧。” 她对小鸟叫。
Izzie lay on her back in the snow. She and Nina were making snow angels while Miss Shelly set up the Kids Central activity. The sky was clear and blue. Izzie saw a red bird land on a tree branch. "Tweet, tweet, tweet," she called to it.
“尼娜，鸟儿是不是吃蚯蚓和昆虫？” 莉琪问。
“是呀。” 尼娜回答。
“那下雪时它们吃什么呢？” 
女生们想了一会儿。她们决定去问问雪莉老师。
"Nina, don't birds eat worms and bugs?" Izzie asked.
"Yes. I think so," Nina answered.
"Then what do they eat when there is snow on the ground?"
The girls thought about this. They decided to ask Miss Shelly.
“你们一定是知道我心里想什么了。” 雪莉老师说，“我刚好要问你们同样的问题。” 
“真的吗？” 莉琪问。雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。贾森和波比停止打雪仗，走了过来。
"You girls must have read my mind," Miss Shelly said. "I was just going to ask you that question."
"You were?" Izzie said. Miss Shelly blew her whistle. Jason and Bobby stopped their snowball fight and came over.
“鸟儿一般吃蚯蚓、昆虫和莓果。但是，这些在冬天很难找到。” 雪莉老师说。
“冬天太冷了。还有很多雪！” 莉琪说。
"Birds usually eat worms, bugs, and berries. But these things are hard to find in winter, right?" Miss Shelly said.
"It's too cold. And there's so much snow!" Izzie said.
“人们可以在外面放喂食器来帮助鸟儿。今天我们要在操场上为鸟儿做喂食器。” 雪莉老师说。
“太酷了！” 莉琪说，“要怎么做呢？” 
"People can help birds by putting out feeders. Today we'll make bird feeders for the birds here on the playground," Miss Shelly said.
"Cool!" Izzie said. "How do we make them?"
“首先，在那边的松树下找一颗松果。” 雪莉老师指了指操场旁边的一排树。
几分钟后，孩子们就带着松果跑了回来。“我的最大！” 波比大喊。
"First find a pinecone by those pine trees over there." Miss Shelly pointed to a row of trees on the edge of the playground.
Minutes later the kids came running back with their pinecones. "Mine's the biggest!" Bobby shouted.
“接下来，选一条扭扭棒。把一边绑在你的松果上。” 雪莉老师说。
“请给我绿色的。” 莉琪说。
“请给我蓝色的。” 贾森说。
"Next choose a pipe cleaner. Tie one end around the stem of your pinecone," Miss Shelly said.
"Green please," Izzie said.
"Blue please," Jason said.
“我要用紫色的。” 尼娜说。
“当然了。” 波比说。
“你什么意思？” 尼娜问。
“没什么，紫色小姐。” 波比咧嘴笑了。
"I'm going to use a purple one," Nina said.
"Of course you are," said Bobby.
"What does that mean?" Nina asked.
"Nothing, Miss Purple." Bobby grinned.
“现在我们用它粘满花生酱。” 雪莉老师说。
“哇！好黏呀！” 莉琪大喊。
“没错！我们要让松果变黏，这样就可以让鸟食粘到上面。接下来，我们用它粘满鸟食。” 雪莉老师说。
"Now we roll the pinecones in peanut butter," Miss Shelly said.
"Whoa! It's so sticky!" Izzie cried.
"Exactly! We need the pinecones to be sticky so seeds will stick to them. Next we roll them in birdseed," Miss Shelly said.
“看上去很漂亮！” 莉琪拿起她的松果说。松果上粘满了不同颜色的鸟食。
“我的也是！” 尼娜说。
“我希望那只红色的小鸟会吃它。” 莉琪说。
"It looks pretty!" Izzie said, holding up her pinecone. It was covered with different-colored seeds.
"So does mine!" Nina said.
"I hope that red bird eats from it," Izzie said.
“我们把喂食器挂起来看看吧。” 雪莉老师说，“我们挂在哪一棵树上呢？” 
“那棵。” 莉琪指着刚才红色小鸟停过的树。
"Well, let's hang up your bird feeders and find out," Miss Shelly said. "Which tree should we hang them on?"
"That one." Izzie pointed to the tree where she had seen the red bird earlier.
雪莉老师用梯子爬到树上。“请把你们的喂食器给我。” 她说。
雪莉老师把喂食器绑在不同的树枝上。莉琪觉得它们看上去就像圣诞树上的装饰。
Miss Shelly carried a ladder over to the tree and climbed up. "Pass me your bird feeders please," she said.
Miss Shelly tied all the bird feeders onto separate branches. Izzie thought they looked like ornaments on a Christmas tree.
“现在我们坐下来边等边看。” 雪莉老师说。他们回到野餐桌旁坐下。雪莉老师给大家倒热可可。大家看着树。
“它来了！” 莉琪开心地小声说。
"Now we sit, wait, and watch," Miss Shelly said. They sat back down at the picnic table. Miss Shelly poured everyone hot cocoa. They all watched the tree.
"There it is!" Izzie whispered happily.
莉琪指着树上的一只红鸟。它跳到一根树枝上。然后飞下来啄莉琪的松果。
“我要叫你樱桃。” 她说。小鸟飞上了天空。“再见，樱桃！快点回来哦。” 
Izzie pointed to a red bird in the tree. It hopped on a branch. Then it flew down to peck at Izzie's pinecone.
"I'm going to name you Cherry," she said. The bird took off into the sky. "Good-bye, Cherry! Come back soon."
需要准备：
-一颗松果
-一条扭扭棒或一条粗线
-花生酱
-鸟食
Things You'll Need:
- a pinecone
- a pipe cleaner or a piece of thick string
- peanut butter
- birdseed
自己试试吧：
1) 找一颗松果。
2) 把扭扭棒或者线的一边绑在松果上。
3) 把松果放进花生酱里，让它粘满花生酱。
4) 把松果放进鸟食里，让它粘满鸟食。
5) 把松果喂食器挂在你喜欢的树上，等着小鸟来吧！
Do It Yourself:
1) Find a pinecone.
2) Tie one end of a pipe cleaner or piece of string onto the stem of the pinecone.
3) Roll the pinecone in peanut butter until it is fully covered.
4) Roll the pinecone in the birdseed until it is fully covered.
5) Hang the pinecone bird feeder on your favorite tree and watch for birds!
尼娜在去儿童中心的路上看到了莉琪。“这是我今天在书展上买的书，叫《关于水果》。我喜欢水果！” 
“我也喜欢水果！” 莉琪说。
Nina saw Izzie on her way to Kids Central. "This is the book I got at the book fair today. It's called All About Fruit. I love fruit!"
"I love fruit too!" Izzie said.
雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。“女生们，该把书收起来了。” 
“但这是关于水果的书，水果是我们最喜欢的食物！” 尼娜说。
Miss Shelly blew her whistle. "Girls, time to put the book away."
"But this is a book about fruit, and fruit is our favourite food!" Nina said.
雪莉老师笑了。“太好了。因为今天我们的活动是水果野餐。但是，我们要先准备水果大餐。” 
“水果野餐？耶！” 莉琪说。
“什么是水果大餐？听上去很好吃！” 尼娜说。
Miss Shelly laughed. "Perfect. Because today we are going on a fruit picnic! But first we have to make our fruit feast."
"A fruit picnic? Yay!" Izzie said.
"What's a fruit feast? It sounds yummy!" Nina said.
“贾森，请你读一读菜单。” 雪莉老师指了指钉在树上的纸。
“水果串和猕猴桃奶油三明治。” 贾森念道。
“首先，我们要做水果串。” 雪莉老师说。
"Jason, please read the menu." Miss Shelly pointed to a piece of paper tacked onto a tree.
"Fruit kebabs and kiwi-and-cream sandwiches," Jason read.
"First we'll make the fruit kebabs," Miss Shelly told them.
“什么是串？” 波比问。
“串就是插在竹签上的食物。” 雪莉老师说，“我们要把四块水果串在竹签上。” 
“葡萄、哈密瓜、香蕉、苹果！” 莉琪把水果插在竹签上。
"What's a kebab?" Bobby asked.
"A kebab is food on a skewer," Miss Shelly said. "So poke a skewer through four pieces of fruit."
"Grape, melon, banana, apple!" Izzie put her fruit on a skewer.
“哈密瓜、苹果、香蕉、葡萄！” 贾森说。
“葡萄、葡萄、葡萄、葡萄。” 波比说，“这样可以吗？” 
“你喜欢就好，波比，这是你的水果串！做好以后，把水果串放到塑料盒里。” 雪莉老师说。
"Melon, apple, banana, grape!" Jason said.
"Grape, grape, grape, grape," Bobby said. "Is that okay?"
"Whatever you want is fine, Bobby. It's your fruit kebab! When you're finished, put your kebab in a container," Miss Shelly said.
“现在，我们要做猕猴桃奶油三明治。” 雪莉老师说。
“拿两片面包。每片都涂奶油。” 莉琪念道。
"Now we'll make the kiwi-and-cream sandwiches," Miss Shelly said.
"Take two slices of bread. Spread whipped cream on one side of each slice," Izzie read.
“然后在其中一片面包上放猕猴桃。” 波比念道。
“把另外一片面包盖上去，完成三明治。快看！我做好了。” 尼娜拿起她的三明治。
"Then place some kiwi on one slice of bread," Bobby read.
"Place the other slice of bread on top to complete your sandwich. Ta-da! I'm done." Nina held up her sandwich.
“现在我们准备野餐篮。” 雪莉老师拿起一个篮子，“把你们的三明治放到袋子里。然后放到塑料盒里。” 
“出发！” 雪莉老师说。孩子们跟着她穿过树林。
"Now we prepare the picnic basket." Miss Shelly held up a basket. "Put your sandwich in a bag. Then put it in your container."
"Off we go!" Miss Shelly said. The kids followed her onto the path through the woods.
他们在一片草地停下。“我们在这里做过全麦饼干三明治！” 尼娜说。
“对。我们也要在这里野餐。你们觉得怎么样？” 雪莉老师问。
“好呀！” 波比说。
They stopped at a grassy area. "We made s'mores here!" Nina said.
"Yes, and this is where we'll have our picnic too. What do you think?" Miss Shelly answered.
"Great!" Bobby said.
“早知道就带雨伞了。” 尼娜说。
大家看着她。“为什么？” 雪莉老师问。
尼娜伸出手掌。“因为我刚刚感觉到下雨了！” 
"Maybe we should have brought umbrellas," Nina said.
Everyone looked at her. "Why?" Miss Shelly asked.
Nina held out her palm. "Because I just felt a raindrop!"
“快！把食物放回篮子里。” 雪莉老师说。雨更大了。“别忘了你们的坐垫！” 
“不好了！我的书！” 尼娜跑回去拿书。
"Quick! Put the food back in the basket," Miss Shelly said as it began to rain harder. "Don't forget your sit-upon!"
"Oh no! My book!" Nina ran back for her book.
“好险，我们跑回来了。” 雪莉老师停下来喘气。
“雨停了。看，太阳出来了！” 尼娜说。
“最近的天气真是的。” 雪莉老师叹了口气。接着她笑了。“我们在这里野餐，怎么样？” 
"Whew, we made it." Miss Shelly stopped to catch her breath.
"The rain stopped. Look, the sun is coming out!" Nina said.
"Oh, this weather." Miss Shelly sighed. Then she smiled. "Why don't we have our picnic here?"
莉琪笑了。“如果又开始下雨，我们就能跑进室内。” 她把坐垫放在地上。
“哪里都可以，快开始吃吧。” 尼娜说，“然后我们又可以看关于水果的书了！” 
Izzie grinned. "If it starts to rain again, we can run back inside." She plopped her sit-upon down on the blacktop.
"Anywhere is fine. Let's eat already," Nina said. "And then we can read my fruit book again!"
需要准备：
-竹签
-各种水果块
-切下边缘的面包片
-奶油
-切片的猕猴桃
Things you'll need:
- wooden skewers
- a variety of fruit chunks
- sliced bread with crusts cut off
- whipped cream
- sliced kiwi
自己试试吧：
做水果串：
1) 把水果块串在竹签上。
做猕猴桃奶油三明治：
1) 在两片面包上涂奶油。
2) 在一片面包上放猕猴桃。
3) 把另一片面包盖在上面。
4) 把三明治和水果串装好去野餐，或者在家里品尝美食！
Do it Yourself:
For the fruit kebabs:
1) Poke a skewer through chunks of fruit.

For the kiwi-and-cream sandwiches:
1) Spread whipped cream on two slices of bread.
2) Place some kiwi on one slice of bread.
3) Place the other slice of bread on top.
4) Pack your sandwich and fruit kebab for a picnic or enjoy at home!
波比在去儿童中心的路上遇到了弗拉尼校长。
“你好，波比。” 她说，“我那天在超市遇到了你妈妈。她很开朗，也很亲切。母亲节，你有什么特别的计划吗？” 
Bobby met Ms. Folani in the hallway on his way to Kids Central.
"Hello, Bobby," she said. "I saw your mom the other day at the grocery store. She is so cheerful and nice. Do you have anything special planned for Mother's Day?"
波比咽了一口口水。“哦。母亲节……是什么时候？” 
弗拉尼校长哈哈大笑。“是下个星期天，波比！你有12天的时间。你一定能想出好礼物！” 
Bobby swallowed. "Oh. Mother's Day . . . When is that?"
Ms. Folani laughed. "It's next Sunday, Bobby! You have 12 days. I'm sure you'll think of something sweet!"
“也许我们在儿童中心会制作一些母亲节礼物。” 波比边开门边想。
雪莉老师正在做准备。波比问贾森他的母亲节计划。
"Maybe we'll make something for Mother's Day in Kids Central," Bobby thought as he opened the gym door.
While Miss Shelly was setting up the tables, Bobby asked Jason what he was doing for his mom on Mother's Day.
“我和爸爸会为她做一个蛋糕。” 贾森说，“怎么了？你要做什么呢？” 
雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。“把你们的东西收起来，然后过来吧。” 她说。
"My dad and I are going to bake her a cake," Jason said. "Why? What are you doing?"
Miss Shelly blew her whistle. "Please put away your things and come over," she called.
雪莉老师把纸杯分给大家。“今天我们要把这些纸杯变成花盆。” 雪莉老师说。
“我们要怎么把它们变成花盆呢？” 莉琪很好奇。
Miss Shelly passed out paper cups. "Today we are going to turn these paper cups into flowerpots," said Miss Shelly.
"How do we turn them into flowerpots?" Izzie wanted to know.
“我们在里面种下花种！” 雪莉老师说。
“我们种什么花呢？” 波比问。妈妈们都喜欢花。也许这可以成为一个礼物。
"By planting flower seeds in them!" said Miss Shelly.
"What kind of flower seeds are we planting?" Bobby asked. Moms always like flowers. Maybe this could be his present.
雪莉老师举起一个袋子。“金盏花。” 她说。她给大家看一张图。“金盏花有绿叶和黄花。” 
Miss Shelly held up a bag. "Marigolds," she said. Then she showed them a picture. "Marigolds are small plants with green leaves and yellow flowers."
“给我妈妈刚好，你不觉得吗？” 波比小声对贾森说。
“应该吧。送她个电子游戏怎么样？” 贾森说。
“贾森，妈妈们喜欢巧克力，不喜欢电子游戏。” 莉琪说。
"Those would be perfect for my mom, don't you think?" Bobby whispered to Jason.
"I guess so. How about getting her a video game?" Jason said.
"Jason, moms like chocolate, not video games," Izzie said.
雪莉老师用铅笔敲敲桌子。“首先，用铅笔在纸杯底下穿一个孔。这样，在我们浇水的时候，多余的水可以流出来。” 
Miss Shelly tapped the table with her pencil. "First use your pencil to poke a hole in the bottom of your paper cup. That way when we water the plants, the extra water can drain out."
“接着，我们在杯子里装土。大家去那边装土吧。” 雪莉老师指着地上的箱子。
“然后我们用手指挖个小洞，把种子放进去，对吗？” 莉琪说。她和妈妈一起种过花。
"Next fill the cup with soil. Please go and get some soil over there." Miss Shelly pointed to a box on the floor.
"Then we dig a little hole with our fingers and put the seeds in, right?" Izzie said. She had planted flowers with her mom before.
“是的！” 雪莉老师说。她给每个孩子几个种子。“然后我们给它们水和阳光，等它们长大！” 
"Exactly!" Miss Shelly said. She gave each kid a few seeds. "After that we give them water and sun. And we wait for them to grow!"
“等它们长大？” 波比紧张地想。他忘记种子需要时间长大了。
“雪莉老师？” 波比问，“金盏花在母亲节之前会开花吗？” 
"Wait for them to grow?" Bobby thought nervously. He had forgotten that it took a long time for seeds to turn into plants.
"Miss Shelly?" Bobby asked. "Will our marigolds bloom by Mother's Day?"
“不会。需要一两个月才能长大呢。” 雪莉老师回答。
“不好了……” 波比开始担心。现在，他没有东西可以在母亲节给妈妈了。
"I'm afraid not. It takes a month or two for them to grow," Miss Shelly answered.
"Oh no . . ." Bobby started to worry. Now he had nothing to give his mom for Mother's Day.
“我知道了！你在下个星期天先把花盆给你妈妈。等花开了，就好像又过了一次母亲节！” 尼娜说。
波比笑了。真是个好主意！就这样好了。
"I know! You could give the pot to her next Sunday anyway. And then when the flowers bloom, it will be like Mother's Day all over again!" Nina said.
Bobby smiled. What a great idea! That's just what he'd do.
需要准备：
-一个纸杯
-水
-种花用的土
-金盏花种子或其他花的种子
-削尖的铅笔
Things you'll need:
- a paper cup
- water
- potting soil
- marigold seeds or other flower seeds
- a sharp pencil
自己试试吧：
1) 用铅笔在纸杯底下穿一个孔。
2) 把纸杯装满土。
3) 用手指挖1到2厘米的洞。
4) 在洞里放几个种子。
5) 用土盖住洞。
6) 浇一点水。
7) 放在阳光充足的地方。
8) 土看上去比较干的时候需要浇水。
9) 一到两个月后就开花了！
Do It Yourself:
1) Poke a hole in the bottom of the cup with a pencil.
2) Fill the cup with potting soil.
3) Dig a 1–2 cm hole with your finger.
4) Put a few seeds in the hole.
5) Cover the hole with dirt.
6) Water the seeds lightly.
7) Place in a sunny spot and wait.
8) Water whenever the soil looks dry.
9) Your plant will bloom in a month or two!
“我看到了各种各样的动物。” 莉琪对尼娜说，“青蛙们很不错。我喜欢青蛙。但我最喜欢的是火烈鸟。” 
莉琪上周六跟家人去了动物园。现在她一直在讲关于动物园的事。
"I saw all kinds of animals," Izzie said to Nina. "The frogs were great. I love frogs. But my favorite was the flamingo."
Izzie had gone to the zoo on Saturday with her family. Now it was all she could talk about.
雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。“女生们！要开始了。” 她说。孩子们都过来了。雪莉老师正戴着一个黑面具，上面有彩色的装饰片和羽毛。
“哇。雪莉老师，您为什么戴面具？” 莉琪问。
Miss Shelly blew her whistle. "Girls! Time to start," she said. The kids gathered around the table. Miss Shelly was wearing a black mask with colorful sequins and feathers.
"Wow. Why are you wearing that, Miss Shelly?" Izzie asked.
“因为今天我们要做面具。可以做这样的派对面具，或者特工面具，或者怪物面具……” 雪莉老师说。
“哦，我要做特工面具。” 波比说。
“我要做超级特工面具。” 贾森说。
"Because today we'll make masks—party masks, like this one. Or secret-agent masks or monster masks . . . ," Miss Shelly said.
"Oh, I'm going to make a secret-agent mask," Bobby said.
"Mine's going to be a super secret-agent mask," Jason said.
“我要做派对面具！” 尼娜说，“你呢，莉琪？我们一起做派对面具吧！” 
莉琪想了想。“好吧。” 
“这里是没有装饰过的面具。” 雪莉老师说。
"I'm going to make a party mask!" Nina said. "What about you, Izzie? Let's make party masks together!"
Izzie thought for a moment. "Okay. I guess so."
"Here is a plain mask," Miss Shelly said.
“装饰品在桌子上。你可以用自己喜欢的东西。把装饰品粘在向外的一面就可以了。” 雪莉老师说。
莉琪看了看桌子。
"The rest of the decorations are on the table. You can use anything you like. Just glue the pieces to the front of the mask," Miss Shelly said.
Izzie looked at the table.
有蝴蝶结、布料、扣子和羽毛。莉琪看到两根粉红色的羽毛。突然，她有了个好主意。
“尼娜。” 她说，“我不跟你做派对面具了。” 
“为什么呢？” 尼娜看上去很伤心。
There were ribbons, fabric, buttons, and feathers. Izzie saw two pink feathers poking out of the pile. Suddenly she got a great idea.
"Nina," she said. "I'm not going to make a party mask with you."
"Why not?" Nina looked hurt.
“因为我要做一个火烈鸟面具！” 莉琪大喊。
“动物面具真是个好主意！” 雪莉老师说。
尼娜看了看自己的面具。她已经把不同颜色的装饰片粘到面具的一角了。
"Because I'm going to make a flamingo mask!" Izzie cried.
"An animal mask. What a cool idea!" Miss Shelly said.
Nina looked down at her mask. She had already begun to glue different-colored sequins to one corner.
“火烈鸟是粉红色的。但它们的嘴是黑色和白色的。而且还突出来。我需要做一个嘴巴。” 莉琪说。她拿了一把装饰片。
“好吧。” 尼娜皱着眉说，“但不要拿走所有的装饰片。” 
"Flamingos are pink. But their beaks are black and white. And they stick out too. I need to make a beak," Izzie said, grabbing a handful of sequins.
"Fine," Nina said, frowning. "But don't take all the sequins."
莉琪用一张纸板折成嘴。她把它粘到面具上。然后，她用粉红色的羽毛装饰剩下的部分。最后，她用黑色和白色的装饰片装饰嘴。
Izzie folded a piece of cardboard into a beak. She glued it to her mask. Then she decorated the rest of the mask with pink feathers. Finally she covered the beak with black and white sequins.
“嘎、嘎。” 莉琪戴上面具，单脚站着。“我是火烈鸟！” 
“我是瓢虫！” 尼娜也戴上她的面具，“我也想做动物。” 她害羞地说。
"Squawk, squawk." Izzie put on her mask and stood on one leg. "I'm a flamingo!"
"And I'm a ladybug!" Nina put on her mask too. "I wanted to be an animal too," she said shyly.
“可以告诉我你四月十九号晚上在哪里吗？” 一个戴着灰色面具和墨镜的男生突然问。
“是的。我们还想知道你的真名，瓢虫小姐。” 另一个戴着蓝色面具和墨镜的男生问。
"Can you tell me where you were on the night of April 19th?" a boy in a gray mask and sunglasses suddenly asked.
"Yes, and we'd like to know your real name, Miss Ladybug," said another boy, in a blue mask and sunglasses.
“啊！” 女生们尖叫起来。
雪莉老师哈哈大笑。“男生们，面具真不错。” 她说。她也戴上自己的面具。“现在没人认得出我们了！” 
体育馆的门开了，弗拉尼校长走了进来。
"Ah!" the girls shrieked.
Miss Shelly laughed. "Great masks, boys," she said. She put on her mask too. "Now no one will recognize us!"
The gym door opened, and Ms. Folani walked in.
校长看上去很困惑。“你们是谁？儿童中心的孩子们都去哪儿了？” 
“外星人在动物园绑架了儿童中心的孩子们。我们特工正在这里调查。” 贾森严肃地说。
The principal looked confused. "Who are you? I thought the Kids Central kids were in here today."
"Aliens kidnapped the Kids Central kids at the zoo. We secret agents are here to investigate," Jason said seriously.
“瓢虫和火烈鸟可能和这件事有关。” 波比补充说。尼娜和莉琪偷笑着。
“哦！” 弗拉尼校长接着说，“如果有新发现，请一定要告诉我。儿童中心的孩子们对我们来说很重要。” 
"The ladybug and the flamingo may be part of the crime," Bobby added. Nina and Izzie giggled behind their masks.
"Oh!" Ms. Folani exclaimed. "Well, please let me know what you find out. Those kids from Kids Central are very important to us."
需要准备：
-一个还没装饰的面具（从手工艺品店买或者自己做）
-羽毛、装饰片、水彩、记号笔、布料和其他你想要用来装饰的东西
-胶水
Things you'll need:
- a basic mask (from a craft store or make your own)
- feathers, sequins, paint, markers, fabric, and anything else you want to decorate your mask with
- glue
自己试试吧：
1) 决定要做什么面具。
2) 设计，装饰面具。
3) 戴上面具，看别人能不能认出你！
Do it Yourself:
1) Decide what kind of mask you want to make.
2) Design and decorate your mask.
3) Put on your mask and see if people can recognize you!
“太热了。” 贾森说。他在体育馆里用笔记本扇风。
“是啊，我不停流汗。可我只是站在这里。” 波比说。
雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。
"It is so hot," Jason said. He fanned himself with his notebook in the gym.
"I know. I'm sweating. And I'm just standing here," Bobby said.
Miss Shelly blew her whistle.
她的脚边放了一个大冷藏箱。“今天我买了草莓、香蕉、桃子、牛奶和冰淇淋。我们要做一个冰凉的甜品。” 她说。
There was a large cooler by her feet. "Today I brought strawberries, bananas, peaches, milk, and ice cream. We're going to make an ice-cold treat," she said.
“奶昔！” 莉琪边跳边喊。
“太好了。” 波比握着拳说。
“嗯……我喜欢桃子奶昔。” 尼娜说。
贾森看着冷藏箱里的冰淇淋。
"Milk shakes!" Izzie cried, jumping up and down.
"Yes," Bobby said, pumping his fist.
"Mmm . . . I like peach milk shakes," Nina said.
Jason stared at the ice cream in the cooler.
“奶昔很容易做。” 雪莉老师说，“我们只需要把食材放进搅拌机，然后……” 
“搅拌、搅拌、搅拌！” 莉琪说。
尼娜念出第一步。“把草莓放进搅拌机。” 
"Milk shakes are easy to make," Miss Shelly explained. "All we do is put the ingredients into the blender and—"
"Blend, blend, blend!" finished Izzie.
Nina read the first step. "Put strawberries into the blender."
“然后放进一根香蕉。” 波比说。
“和一杯桃子。” 贾森说。
“接下来，放一杯半香草冰淇淋。一定很好吃。” 莉琪说。她把冰淇淋舀到量杯里。
"Then add one ripe banana," Bobby said.
"And one cup of peaches," Jason said.
"Next add one and a half cups of vanilla ice cream. Yum," Izzie said. She scooped ice cream into the measuring cup.
“然后放一杯半冰块。” 尼娜说，“哦，冷藏箱真凉。” 
“然后加半杯牛奶。” 莉琪小心地倒下去，“哇！已经完成了。” 
"Then we put in one and a half cups of ice cubes," Nina said. "Ooh, it's cold in the cooler!"
"And then add half a cup of milk," Izzie said, pouring carefully. "Wow! We're done already."
“快要完成了。” 雪莉老师纠正她说，“贾森，你可以把搅拌机的盖子盖上，启动机器吗？” 
贾森盖上盖子，启动机器。搅拌机的刀片旋转着，发出很大的声音。 
"Almost done," Miss Shelly corrected. "Jason, will you put the lid on the blender and turn it on for us?"
Jason put the lid on the blender and turned it on. The blender hummed and buzzed as the blades spun around.
孩子们听到冰块搅碎，撞到玻璃的声音。接着，声音变小了。
“奶昔做好了。” 雪莉老师说。
The kids heard the ice cubes crack and bang against the glass. Then the sound became softer.
"I think our milk shakes are ready," Miss Shelly said.
她给尼娜、波比和莉琪倒满了冰凉的奶昔。到贾森时，贾森突然把他的手盖在杯子上。
“不要！” 他大喊。
She filled Nina, Bobby, and Izzie's glasses with ice-cold milk shakes. When she reached for Jason's, he suddenly put his hands over the glass.
"No!" he cried.
“贾森，怎么了？你不想喝奶昔吗？” 雪莉老师问。
“不要。” 他摇摇头，又说了一次。
大家都看着贾森。
"Jason, what's the matter? Don't you want to try the milk shake?" Miss Shelly asked.
"No," he said again, shaking his head.
Everyone looked at Jason.
“为什么不喝呢？” 波比问。
“对啊，真的很好喝。” 莉琪说完喝了一口。
“其实我不喜欢牛奶。” 贾森的眼睛往下看，“我也不喜欢冰淇淋。我就是这么奇怪。” 
"Why not?" Bobby asked.
"Yeah, it's really good," Izzie said, taking a sip of hers.
"Well, actually I don't like milk." Jason looked down. "And I don't like ice cream either. I'm weird."
“你不奇怪。” 波比笑着说，“嗯……你是有点儿奇怪，但不是因为这个。” 
“我很奇怪。小孩子应该喜欢牛奶。小孩子应该喜欢冰淇淋。” 贾森说。
"You're not weird." Bobby grinned. "Well, you are weird, but not because of that."
"I am weird. Kids are supposed to like milk. Kids are supposed to love ice cream," Jason said.
“小孩子不需要喜欢什么。” 雪莉老师说，“做水果冰沙也很容易。我们只需要用果汁代替牛奶和冰淇淋。” 
她在冷藏箱里找了找。“哦！这里正好有芒果汁！” 
"Kids don't have to like anything," Miss Shelly said. "And it's so easy to make a fruit smoothie. We'll just use juice instead of milk and ice cream."
She dug through the cooler. "Aha! Here's some mango juice!"
大家一起把草莓、香蕉、桃子、冰块和果汁倒进搅拌机。不到一分钟，贾森的水果冰沙就做好了。
“谢谢大家。” 他尝了一口，“嗯！冰沙很好吃！” 
Everyone helped put strawberries, banana, peaches, ice cubes, and juice into the blender. Jason's fruit smoothie was done in a minute.
"Thanks, guys." He took a sip. "Mmm! Smoothies are great!"
需要准备：
-一杯草莓
-一根香蕉
-一杯桃子
-一杯半香草冰淇淋
-一杯半冰块
-半杯牛奶
-（也可以用一杯芒果汁和两杯冰块代替冰淇淋、冰块和牛奶）
-搅拌机
Things you'll need:
- 1 cup strawberries
- 1 ripe banana
- 1 cup peaches
- 1 ½ cups vanilla ice cream
- 1 ½ cups ice cubes
- 1/2 cup milk
- (for nondairy, replace ice cream, ice, and milk with 1 cup mango juice and 2 cups ice)
- a blender
自己试试吧：
1) 把草莓放进搅拌机。
2) 加入香蕉。
3) 加入桃子。
4) 加入香草冰淇淋。（如果做冰沙，就用芒果汁代替。）
5) 加入冰块。
6) 加入牛奶。（如果做冰沙，就跳过这一步）
7) 搅拌到均匀。
8) 品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Put strawberries in a blender.
2) Add the banana.
3) Add peaches.
4) Add vanilla ice cream. (Add mango juice instead if you're making a smoothie.)
5) Add ice cubes.
6) Add milk. (Skip this step if you're making a smoothie.)
7) Blend until smooth.
8) Enjoy!
“今天我们要把旧蜡笔变成彩虹蜡烛。” 雪莉老师说。她拿起一个彩色的蜡烛。

Nina looked into her bag of old crayons. She wasn't sure she wanted her purple crayons in a rainbow candle

"First let's see what colors we have," said Miss Shelly. The kids took out their crayons.
"We've got red, orange, yellow, blue, green, and . . . lots of purple from Nina!" Miss Shelly said. "Perfect for rainbow candles."
尼娜举起手。“雪莉老师，我可以做个紫色的蜡烛吗？我不想要彩虹蜡烛。”

Nina raised her hand. "Miss Shelly, can I make a purple candle? I don't want a rainbow candle."
Miss Shelly paused. "Well, we're all going to share crayons. If you only want purple, it may be a short candle. Is that okay?"
尼娜点点头。“是的，只要是紫色就行。”

Nina nodded. "Uh-huh. As long as it's purple."
"Okay. First we need to peel the paper off the crayons," Miss Shelly said. "There shouldn't be any paper in our candles."
孩子们做好之后，雪莉老师点起电炉的火。“现在我们要让蜡笔融化。一次一个颜色。我们要把它们放在锅里融化。” 她说，“请放红色的蜡笔。”

孩子们把红色蜡笔放进锅里。
“哦，它们开始融化了！” 贾森说。
“小心。锅很烫！” 雪莉老师提醒说。
The kids dropped handfuls of red crayons into the pot.
"Ooh, they're melting!" Jason said.
"Be careful. The pot is very hot!" Miss Shelly warned.
“现在我们把蜡倒进玻璃罐里。像这样小心地把烛芯放在罐子中间。我来倒蜡。不要把烛芯放开！” 雪莉老师说。
"Now we pour the wax into your glass jars. Carefully hold the wick in the center of your jar like this. I'll pour the wax. Do not let go of your wick!" Miss Shelly said.
她倒了一层红色的蜡到莉琪、贾森和波比的罐子底下。然后她又倒了橙色、黄色、绿色和蓝色的蜡。
尼娜看着。她的罐子还是空的。
She poured a layer of red wax into the bottom of Izzie's jar, Jason's jar, and then Bobby's jar. She did the same for orange, yellow, green, and blue wax.
Nina just watched. Her jar was empty.
“好了。最后一层。” 雪莉老师说。
尼娜跳起来，拿起她的罐子。紫色终于准备好了！雪莉老师给每个人都倒了一些紫色的蜡。“雪莉老师，我的蜡烛太短了。” 尼娜皱着眉说。
"Here we go. The last layer," Miss Shelly said.
Nina jumped up and held out her jar. Finally they were ready for purple! Miss Shelly poured everyone some purple wax. "Miss Shelly, my candle is too short." Nina said, frowning.
“尼娜，我刚才告诉过你了。” 雪莉老师说。
“我知道。但我不知道它会是这个样子！” 尼娜说。她伤心地看着她的短蜡烛。
“我还有一些红色的蜡笔。” 波比说。
"Nina, I warned you about that," Miss Shelly said.
"I know. But I didn't think it was going to look like this!" Nina said. She looked sadly at her short candle with its long, droopy wick.
"I've still got some red crayons," Bobby said.
“贾森有蓝色的蜡笔。红色和蓝色混合起来是紫色。我们可以做更多紫色的蜡。” 波比看着雪莉老师。
尼娜对波比笑了笑。“谢谢你。” 她说。有时候波比还挺亲切的。
"And Jason has blue crayons. Red and blue make purple. We can make more purple wax." Bobby looked at Miss Shelly.
Nina smiled at Bobby. "Thanks," she said. Sometimes he was nice.
孩子们把红色和蓝色的蜡笔一起放进锅里。
“我觉得这样就可以了。你觉得呢？” 雪莉老师问尼娜。
尼娜的蜡烛没有彩虹蜡烛那么高。但已经快要装满罐子了。“是的，好多了。” 尼娜说。
They melted the red and blue crayons together in the pot.
"I think that will do. Don't you?" Miss Shelly asked Nina.
Nina's candle wasn't as tall as the rainbow candles. But now it almost reached the top of her jar. "Yeah. It's better," she said.
之后雪莉老师剪断大家的烛芯。然后，她点亮蜡烛，关上灯。大家的蜡烛都在黑暗中发着光。
“我们的蜡烛看上去真不错！” 贾森说。
Later Miss Shelly trimmed everyone's wicks. Then she lit the candles and turned off the lights. Everyone's candles flickered brightly in the dark.
"Our candles look awesome!" Jason said.
“你的彩虹蜡烛真漂亮。” 尼娜对莉琪说。
“谢谢。你的紫色蜡烛也很漂亮。” 莉琪说。
在烛光中，尼娜看着儿童中心的老师和朋友们。她和他们在一起很幸福！
"Your rainbow candle is really pretty," Nina told Izzie.
"Thanks. Your purple one is too," Izzie said.
Nina looked at her Kids Central friends and teacher in the glowing lights. She was so happy with them!
需要准备：
-烛芯
-剪刀
-铅笔
-断掉的蜡笔
-双层锅
-玻璃罐
Things you'll need:
- a candlewick
- scissors
- a pencil
- broken crayon pieces
- a double boiler
- a glass jar
自己试试吧：
1) 把烛芯剪得比玻璃罐的高度长20厘米。
2) 把烛芯绑在铅笔上。
3) 把蜡笔上的纸撕下来。
4) 在双层锅的下层装水煮沸。在上层的锅里融化蜡笔，一次一种颜色。如果没有双层锅，可以把一个罐子放在一锅沸水里。
5) 请大人帮你把蜡倒进玻璃罐里，你拿着烛芯。
6) 等蜡烛变硬变凉。
7) 把烛芯剪成1厘米。
8) 在大人的帮助下点蜡烛，关灯！
Do it Yourself:
1) Cut the wick about 20cm longer than the height of your jar.
2) Tie the wick to a pencil.
3) Peel the paper off old or broken crayons.
4) Boil water in the bottom pot of a double boiler. Melt the crayons, one color at a time, in the top pot of the double boiler. If you don't have a double boiler, you can place a can in a pot of boiling water.
5) Ask an adult to help you pour the melted crayon wax into a glass jar while you hold the wick over the jar.
6) Let the candle harden and cool.
7) Cut the wicks to 1 cm.
8) With an adult's help, light your candle and turn off the lights!
“太棒了！” 贾森看到雪莉老师后说。雪莉老师戴着厨师帽。这意味着他们今天要煮东西。他马上关掉游戏，围上围裙。
“我们要做什么？” 尼娜问。
"Cool!" Jason said when he spotted Miss Shelly. She was wearing her chef's hat. That meant they were cooking today. He turned off his video game right away and put on his apron.
"What are we making?" Nina asked.
“一顿为特别的客人准备的特别晚餐。” 雪莉老师说。
“客人？” 贾森说。
“什么客人？” 莉琪问，“他们是谁？” 
"A special meal," Miss Shelly said, "for very special dinner guests."
"Dinner guests?" Jason said.
"What dinner guests?" Izzie asked. "Who are they?"
“我们开始吧。这样才能在他们来的时候准备好。” 雪莉老师说。她拿起一张菜单。“波比，我们今晚要吃什么呢？” 
“番茄酱意大利面。” 波比念道。
"Let's get started so dinner will be ready when they get here," Miss Shelly said. She held up a menu. "Bobby, what are we having for dinner tonight?"
"Spaghetti with tomato sauce," Bobby read.
“首先，我们要做酱。贾森，我们该做什么呢？” 雪莉老师问。
贾森已经读好了说明。他拿了一个量杯。“我们用锅加热橄榄油。” 
"First we need to make the sauce. Jason, what do we do?" Miss Shelly asked.
Jason had already read the directions. He was reaching for a measuring cup. "We heat olive oil in a pot."
“然后，加入切碎的蒜头。” 莉琪念道，“一个大大的蒜头？” 她想象一个大头盯着她看。
“蒜头不是一个头，是这个。” 贾森拿起一个蒜头。
“贾森说得对。” 雪莉老师给莉琪一些切碎的蒜头。
"Next we add a head of garlic, chopped," Izzie read. "A big garlic?" She imagined a giant head staring at her.
"Garlic is not a head; it's this." Jason held one up.
"Jason's right." Miss Shelly handed Izzie some chopped garlic.
“炒三分钟。” 尼娜念道，“我来设闹钟！” 
“现在加入番茄。” 波比把两罐番茄倒进锅里。
"Cook the garlic in oil for three minutes," Nina read. "I'll set the timer!"
"Now we add the tomatoes." Bobby emptied two cans of tomatoes into the pot.
“加入辣椒粉。” 贾森说。他撒了一点辣椒粉。“这样酱就会变辣。” 
“你怎么会知道这么多？” 莉琪问。
“因为我喜欢做饭。我还经常帮爸爸妈妈做饭。” 贾森说。
"Add red pepper flakes," Jason said, sprinkling in the pepper. "This makes the sauce spicy."
"Since when do you know so much about cooking?" Izzie asked.
"I like it. And I've been helping my mom and dad cook," he said.
“用小火煮一个小时。” 尼娜念道，“一个小时？” 
“是的，需要煮很长时间。这样很好。” 雪莉老师说，“因为我们需要为客人做准备。我们要清理，摆好桌子，还要煮意大利面。” 
"Cook over low heat for one hour," Nina read. "One hour?"
"Yep. It has to cook for a long time. And that's good," said Miss Shelly. "Because we have to get ready for our guests. We need to clean up, set the table, and cook the spaghetti."
“谁要整理滑板和球？” 雪莉老师问。
“我！” 波比和贾森同时说。
“谁要摆桌子？” 雪莉老师问。

The kids cleaned and set the table for dinner. The gym looked like a real restaurant. Now it was time to cook the spaghetti.

雪莉老师还是没有说。
"It's boiling!" Nina said.
"Add the spaghetti. Cook for eleven minutes," Bobby read.
"The table looks nice," Jason said. "But who are our guests?"
Miss Shelly still wouldn't tell.
“该沥干意大利面了。” 雪莉老师说。
“现在我们把意大利面和酱放到大碗里混合起来。” 她说，“然后等待。” 
有人敲门。“请进！” 雪莉老师说。
"Time to drain the spaghetti," Miss Shelly said.
"Now we mix the spaghetti and the sauce in a big bowl," she said, "and wait."
There was a knock on the door. "Come in!" Miss Shelly called.
是爸爸妈妈们！
“爸爸、妈妈。” 贾森惊讶地说，“你们就是特别的客人！” 
“听说你们都是出色的厨师。” 贾森的妈妈说，“意大利面闻起来真香。” 
It was everyone's parents!
"Mom. Dad," Jason said, surprised. "You're our special guests!"
"We heard you kids are excellent chefs," Jason's mom said. "This spaghetti smells delicious."
“吃起来也一定很香。” 雪莉老师说，“孩子们忙了一下午。” 
“雪莉老师总能找到超级棒的食谱。她还告诉我们怎么煮。” 贾森补充说，“我觉得这很有趣。” 
"I bet it tastes delicious too," Miss Shelly said. "These kids have been working hard all afternoon."
"But Miss Shelly always finds great recipes. And she shows us what to do," Jason added. "I think it's fun."
需要准备：
-四分之三杯橄榄油
-一整个蒜头去皮，切碎
-两罐切块的番茄（每罐约800克）
-一又二分之一茶匙的辣椒粉
-一些盐
-意大利面（约450克）
Things you'll need:
- 3/4 cup olive oil
- 1 head of garlic, peeled and chopped
- 2 cans (about 800 grams each) of diced tomatoes
- 1 ½ teaspoons red-pepper flakes
- a pinch of salt
- spaghetti (about 450 grams)
自己试试吧：
1) 油放在锅里，在炉子上加热。
2) 加一整块切碎的蒜头。
3) 蒜头在油里炒三分钟。
4) 加番茄。
5) 加辣椒粉。
6) 小火煮一个小时。
7) 水里加一些盐，煮沸。
8) 加意大利面，煮十一分钟。
9) 沥干意大利面，和酱混合。足够四个人吃。
10) 品尝美食！
Do it Yourself:
1) Heat oil in a pot on a stove.
2) Add a head of garlic, chopped.
3) Cook the garlic in oil for about three minutes.
4) Add tomatoes.
5) Add red-pepper flakes.
6) Cook over low heat for one hour.
7) Boil water with a pinch of salt.
8) Add spaghetti and cook for eleven minutes.
9) Drain spaghetti and mix it with the sauce. This makes four large portions.
10) Enjoy!
莉琪在体育馆里蹦蹦跳跳。她假装自己是宠物青蛙呱呱。“呱、呱。” 她叫着。
这是学期结束的前一天。也意味着这是儿童中心结束的前一天。
Izzie was jumping around the gym. She was pretending to be her pet frog, Gurpy. "Gurp. Gurp," she called.
It was the second-to-last day of school. That meant it was also the second-to-last day of Kids Central.

波比从口袋里拿出一张脏纸巾。“我这里有一张纸！我刚刚用它擦过鼻涕。” 
"Attention, frogs and race-car drivers," Miss Shelly called. "We are ready to make today's craft—tissue-paper flowers."
Bobby pulled a dirty tissue out of his pocket. "I've got a tissue right here! I just blew my nose on it."
“不是那种纸，波比。” 雪莉老师说，“我们要用干净的包装纸。” 她指着桌子上的彩纸说。
“呱。我是说，好的。” 莉琪说。尼娜咯咯笑。
"Not that kind of tissue, Bobby," Miss Shelly said. "We're going to use clean wrapping tissue." She pointed to the colored tissue paper on the table.
"Gurp. I mean, great," Izzie said. Nina giggled.
“你们今天真淘气。” 雪莉老师摇摇头说，“好了，我们来做花吧。首先，在纸张的一边折三厘米。然后翻过来。” 
"You kids are too silly today," Miss Shelly said, shaking her head. "Okay, let's make our flowers. First fold one end of your tissue paper about three centimeters. Then flip the tissue over."
“接下来在同一边再折三厘米。然后翻过来再折。一直把整张纸折完。” 
"Next take the same edge you folded before, and fold it three centimeters the other way. Then flip it back over and fold again. Keep repeating this until you have folded the entire tissue."
“现在把扭扭棒的一端绑在纸张中间。” 雪莉老师说，“然后小心地把纸张打开……这样就变成一朵好看的花了！” 
“真简单。” 莉琪说。她在做一朵绿色的花。
"Now wrap one end of your pipe cleaner around the middle of your folded tissue," Miss Shelly said. "Then carefully pull apart the folds and . . . you’ve got a pretty flower!"
"This is easy," Izzie said. She was making a green flower.

需要准备：
-切成21厘米方块的彩色包装纸
-扭扭棒
Things you'll need:
- colored wrapping tissue paper, cut into 21 cm squares
- pipe cleaners
自己试试吧：
1) 在纸的一边折三厘米。
2) 把纸翻面，在同一边再折三厘米。
3) 不停翻面折纸，直到整张纸折完。
4) 把扭扭棒绑在纸张中间。
5) 小心拉开纸张，变成一朵美丽的花。（也可以继续做更多花。把所有的花连在一起，做成王冠。）
6) 把花送给特别的人！
Do it Yourself:
1) Fold one edge of the tissue paper over 3 cm.
2) Flip the tissue over and fold the same edge the other way 3 cm.
3) Keep flipping and folding until the whole tissue is folded.
4) Wrap one end of a pipe cleaner around the middle of the tissue.
5) Carefully unfold and pull apart the tissue into a beautiful flower. (Or continue making more flowers. Tie the ends of the pipe cleaner together to make a crown.)
6) Give your flower to someone special!

需要准备：
-一幅大地图
-可洗颜料
-托盘或者可以放颜料的其他容器
-擦脚的湿毛巾
-闪粉（可选）
Things you'll need:
- a large map
- washable paint
- a tray or something else to put the paint in
- a wet towel for wiping off your feet
- glitter (optional)
自己试试吧：
1) 在地图中选择旅游过的地方。可以是国家，也可以是大洲。
2) 找一张或画一张你所选择的地方的地图
3) 列出你在地图中去过的地方。
4) 把颜料倒进托盘里。
5) 光脚踩进托盘，再踩到地图上。 从你的家乡踩到你去过的地方。
6) 还可以在你最喜欢的地方洒上闪粉。
7) 挂在墙上。每次去旅行后就增加一条脚印！
Do It Yourself:
1) Pick an area of the world you've traveled around. It can be your country or your continent.
2) Find or draw a large map of this area.
3) Make a list of all the places you've been on the map.
4) Pour paint into a large tray.
5) With your bare feet, step into the paint and then step onto the map. Create a path of footprints from your hometown to all the places you've been.
6) If you like, sprinkle glitter over the place you like best.
7) Hang the map on a wall and add a new path every time you take a trip!

需要准备：
-一张23x60厘米的卡纸
-几张23x30厘米的卡纸
-订书机
-胶水
-贴纸、笔、记号笔
Things You'll Need:
-23x60 cm piece of construction paper
-several pieces of 23x30 cm construction paper
-a stapler
-glue
-stickers, pens, or markers
自己试试吧：
1) 对折23x60厘米的卡纸，做成封皮。
2) 在封皮里放至少六张23x30厘米的卡纸。
3) 把折的一边订起来。
4) 在封面上写年份和学校名。
5) 一页记录一个月，可以贴上图片或完成的作业。
6) 用你的创意装饰最后一页！
Do it Yourself:
1) Fold a 23x60 cm piece of construction paper in half to make the front and back cover of your book.
2) Place at least six 23x30 cm pieces of construction paper inside the folded cover.
3) Staple the folded side of your cover.
4) Write the year and the name of your school on the front of your book.
5) Create a page for each month. You can glue photos or school projects.
6) Decorate the last page with something creative!

“上周的雷雨天让一所小学烧毁了。孩子们几乎失去了他们所有的东西！书、铅笔……现在他们需要很多帮助。” 雪莉老师说。

贾森从口袋里拿出一个新的橡皮擦。“给您。” 他说，“这是我们的第一个捐赠物。”

“现在围上围裙！我们要做苹果酱松饼。” 雪莉老师说，“首先，我们需要把干食材混合起来。波比，让伊坦看看我们是怎么做的吧。” 
“一杯半面粉。” 波比念出黑板上的内容。
"Now put on your aprons! We're making applesauce muffins," Miss Shelly said. "First we need to mix the dry ingredients. Bobby, show Ethan how we do it."
"One and a half cups flour," Bobby read from the easel.

需要准备：
-一杯半面粉
-一茶匙发酵粉
-半茶匙小苏打
-半茶匙盐
-二又二分之一茶匙肉桂
-85克融化的黄油
-三分之二杯红糖
-两个鸡蛋
-一杯半苹果酱
-一个松饼烤盘
-烘焙纸杯
Things You'll Need:
-1 ½ cups flour
-1 teaspoon baking powder
-1/2 teaspoon baking soda
-1/2 teaspoon salt
-2 ½ teaspoons cinnamon
-85 grams butter, melted
-2/3 cup brown sugar
-2 eggs
-1 ½ cups applesauce
-a muffin pan
-paper baking cups
自己试试吧：
1) 预热烤箱到190摄氏度。
2) 在大碗里混合面粉、小苏打、盐和肉桂。
3) 在另一个碗里混合黄油和糖。
4) 在黄油和糖里加入鸡蛋，搅拌。
5) 在黄油、糖和鸡蛋里加入苹果酱，搅拌。
6) 轻轻地把干食材和湿食材搅拌在一起。注意不要过度搅拌。
7) 把纸杯放进松饼烤盘里。
8) 把面糊倒到纸杯四分之三的地方。
9) 烤20分钟。
10) 品尝美食！
Do it Yourself!
1) Preheat the oven to 190˚C.
2) Mix the flour, baking soda, salt, and cinnamon in a large bowl.
3) Mix the butter and sugar in a separate bowl.
4) Add the egg to the butter and sugar. Stir.
5) Add the applesauce to the butter, sugar, and egg. Stir.
6) Gently mix the dry ingredients with the wet ingredients. Be careful not to over mix.
7) Line a muffin pan with paper baking cups.
8) Fill the baking cups 3/4 full with batter.
9) Bake for 20 minutes.
10) Enjoy!
