下一个是尼娜。雪莉老师小心地把尼娜的蜡纸放在熨烫板上。她盖上一张旧布开始熨。“你和莉琪没事吧？” 她小声问。
尼娜的眼睛里充满了泪水。她摇摇头。
Nina was next. Miss Shelly carefully placed Nina's wax paper on the ironing board. She covered it with a rag and started to iron. "Is everything okay between you and Izzie?" she asked softly.
Nina's eyes filled with tears. She shook her head.
“怎么了？” 雪莉老师问。
“莉琪今天对我很不友好。我不知道为什么！” 尼娜说。
“你和伊坦关系很好。可能她觉得被忽视了。” 雪莉老师说。
"What's going on?" Miss Shelly asked.
"Izzie's being really mean today. I don't know why!" Nina said.
"You and Ethan are getting along well. Maybe she feels left out," Miss Shelly suggested.
“但是，莉琪是我最好的朋友！” 尼娜说。
“她可能需要时间来适应伊坦。” 雪莉老师说。她把叶子给尼娜。“给你。你的叶子很好看。过几分钟，我们要把它们剪下来。” 
"But Izzie is my best friend!" Nina said.
"She probably needs time to get used to Ethan," Miss Shelly said. She handed Nina her leaves. "Here you go. Your leaves look great. In a few minutes, we'll cut them out."
“沿着叶子的形状剪下来。” 雪莉老师说。
贾森和莉琪剪了圆形。波比和伊坦沿着叶子的形状剪下来。尼娜剪了正方形。她还在想雪莉老师的话。莉琪嫉妒伊坦吗？
"Cut around the edges of your waxed leaves," Miss Shelly said.
Jason and Izzie cut circles. Bobby and Ethan cut around the shape of the leaves. Nina cut squares. She was still thinking about what Miss Shelly had said. Was Izzie jealous of Ethan?
“现在在下面打一个孔。然后用一条长线把叶子穿起来。最后在线的两边打结。” 雪莉老师说。
“现在可以挂起来了吗？” 尼娜问。
"Now punch a hole near the stems. Then thread a long piece of string through each leaf. And finally tie knots on each end of the string," Miss Shelly said.
"Can we hang them up now?" Nina asked.
“莉琪，把你的挂在我的上面吧！” 尼娜说。
莉琪跳起来。“你的彩色叶子好像也很不错。” 她笑着说。尼娜对自己最好的朋友笑了笑。她喜欢交新朋友。但她也不想失去自己的老朋友。
"Izzie, hang yours above mine!" Nina said.
Izzie jumped up. "Your colored ones actually don't look that bad," she said, grinning. Nina smiled at her best friend. She liked making new friends. But she didn't want to lose her old ones.
需要准备：
-秋叶
-一卷蜡纸，剪成几片
-熨斗和熨烫板
-旧布
-打孔器
-剪刀
-线
Things You'll Need:
-autumn leaves
-a roll of wax paper, cut into pieces
-an iron and ironing board
-rags
-a hole puncher
-scissors
-string
自己试试吧：
1) 捡四片秋叶。
2) 把两张蜡纸剪成25x30厘米大小。
3) 把叶子放在其中一张蜡纸上。把另外一张蜡纸盖在上面。
4) 加热熨斗。把旧布放在熨烫板上。
5) 把蜡纸放在旧布上。把另外一块旧布盖在上面。
6) 用熨斗熨到蜡融化，蜡纸变透明。
7) 变凉后剪出叶子。
8) 在下面打孔。
9) 把线穿过孔。
10) 挂起来！
Do it Yourself:
1) Collect four autumn leaves.
2) Cut two pieces of wax paper into 25x30 cm pieces.
3) Place your leaves on one piece of wax paper. Put the other piece on top.
4) Heat an iron to high. Place a rag on an ironing board.
5) Place your wax papers on top of the rag. Cover with another rag.
6) Iron until wax melts and the wax paper turns clear.
7) Allow to cool. Then cut out the leaves.
8) Punch holes near the stems of your leaves.
9) Thread a long string through the holes.
10) Hang up!
波比走进体育馆的时候，雪莉老师刚好吹起了哨子。“排队！” 她说，“我们要去外面。” 她拿着一袋棒球。
“今天一定很有趣！” 波比想。
Bobby walked into the gym just as Miss Shelly blew her whistle. "Line up!" she said. "We're going outside." She was carrying a bag of baseballs.
"Today is going to be fun!" Bobby thought.
波比看到一个击球座。“我们要玩儿童棒球吗？” 他问。
“哦，我玩儿不好儿童棒球。” 莉琪说。
“我们要进行儿童棒球全垒打比赛。” 雪莉老师说。
Bobby saw a batting tee on the blacktop. "Are we playing T-ball?" he asked.
"Oh, I'm terrible at T-ball," Izzie said.
"We're having a T-ball Home Run Derby," Miss Shelly said.
“太好了！” 波比和伊坦很开心。
“什么是全垒打比赛？” 尼娜问。
“是棒球赛季里最棒的一个环节！” 波比说，“选手们比赛，看谁获得最多全垒打。” 
"All right!" Bobby and Ethan were happy.
"What's a home run derby?" Nina asked.
"It's the best part of baseball season!" Bobby said. "It's when the players have a home run contest."
“每个人可以击球三次。” 雪莉老师说，“球必须过那条蓝线才算是全垒打。” 她指了指地上的一条蓝线。
“获得最多全垒打的人赢。” 波比补充说。
"You each get three tries to hit the ball," Miss Shelly explained. "The ball must go past that blue line to be a home run." She pointed to a line on the blacktop.
"The person who hits the most home runs wins," Bobby added.
“谁想先来？” 雪莉老师问，“波比？” 
“一般最差的人先打。” 波比说。
“我先来吧。” 尼娜说，“我应该是最差的。” 
雪莉老师皱了皱眉。“波比，这里没有最好也没有最差。” 
"Who wants to go first?" Miss Shelly asked. "Bobby?"
"Usually the worst person goes first," Bobby said.
"I'll go," Nina offered. "I'm probably the worst."
Miss Shelly frowned. "There's no best or worst here, Bobby."
雪莉老师把球放在击球座上。“准备好就可以开始了！” 她说。
尼娜拿起球棒打了一下，没打中！她又打了一次，又没打中。最后一次，她还是没打中。
Miss Shelly set the ball on the tee. "Whenever you're ready!" she called.
Nina gripped the bat and swung. She missed! She swung again. Another miss! On her last try, she missed again.
“你是零分！” 波比说。
“波比，这样不好。” 雪莉老师责备他。
“下一个是我。” 贾森说，“我打得也不太好。” 他走到击球座旁边。第三次打时，他击中了！
"Your score is zero!" Bobby said.
"Bobby, that's not nice," Miss Shelly scolded.
"I'll go next," Jason said. "I'm not very good either." He stepped up to the tee. On his third try, he hit the ball!
“全垒打！” 贾森边跳边叫。
“不对。” 波比说，“在到达蓝线前球就碰地了。” 他本来要说 “你也是零分” ，但是，雪莉老师看了他一眼。
"Home run!" Jason cried, jumping up and down.
"No," Bobby said. "It bounced before it reached the blue line." He was about to say, "You got a zero too." But Miss Shelly was giving him a look.
“轮到我了。” 莉琪说。第一次她打到了击球座。第二次她没打中。最后一次她打出了全垒打。
“耶！莉琪！” 尼娜欢呼。
"My turn," Izzie said. First she hit the tee. Then she missed. Finally she hit a home run.
"Yeah, Izzie!" Nina cheered.
下一个是伊坦。他第一次就打了全垒打！“太好了。” 他点点头说。第二次，他又打了全垒打！“耶！” 他为最后一击做准备。全垒打！“呵！呵呵！你能赢我吗！” 他对波比说。
Ethan was next. He hit a home run on his first try! "All right!" he said, nodding. On his second try, he hit another home run! "Yeah!" He got ready for his last try. Home run! "Ha-ha! Beat that!" he said to Bobby.
“别担心，我会赢的。” 波比接过球棒说。他深吸了一口气。他想赢伊坦。他很喜欢全垒打比赛。他一定要赢！
"Don't worry. I will," Bobby said, taking the bat. He took a deep breath. He did not want to let Ethan beat him. The Home Run Derby was his favorite major league baseball event. He had to win!
呼！呼！呼！波比很容易就打了三次全垒打。“哈！” 他说，“现在呢，雪莉老师？” 
“现在我们要有一个决胜赛。你和伊坦每人可以再打两次。” 她说。
Whack! Whack! Whack! Bobby easily hit three home runs. "Ha!" he said. "Now what, Miss Shelly?"
"Now we have a tiebreaker. You and Ethan each get two more tries," she said.
伊坦先打，他把球打得很高。球在蓝线附近落下，但是没有超过蓝线。呼！他又打了一次。全垒打！“不错。” 他咧嘴笑着说。他把球棒给波比。
波比拿起球棒挥打。全垒打！
Ethan went first. He hit the ball way up in the air. It landed close to the blue line, but not past it. Then whack! He hit the ball again. A home run! "Not bad," he said, grinning. He passed the bat to Bobby.
Bobby gripped the bat and swung. Home run!
波比又打了一次。全垒打！“我是全垒打比赛冠军！” 他欢呼。
“你很厉害。” 伊坦说。他伸出手。
男生们握了握手。“你也不错。” 波比说。
Bobby swung again. Home run! "I'm the Home Run Derby champion!" he cheered.
"You're pretty good," Ethan said. He stuck out his hand.
The boys shook hands. "You're not so bad either," Bobby said.
需要准备：
-击球座
-棒球或垒球
-球棒
Things You'll Need:
-a batting tee
-a baseball or a softball
-a baseball bat
自己试试吧：
1) 聚集三个以上的朋友。
2) 画一条全垒打的线。
3) 把球放在击球座上。
4) 轮流打球，每个人一轮可以打三次。
5) 获得最多全垒打的人赢！
Do It Yourself:
1) Gather three or more friends.
2) Draw a line marking the home-run area.
3) Set the ball on the tee.
4) Take turns hitting the ball. Each player gets three hits per turn.
5) The player who hits the most home runs wins!
莉琪今天过得并不好。平时她很喜欢体育课。但是，今天她连足球都不想玩儿。平时她喜欢老师大声读书给他们听。但是，今天她只希望老师快点读完。
Izzie was having a bad day. Normally she loved gym. But today she didn't even feel like playing kickball. And normally she loved it when her teacher read aloud to them. But today she kept wondering when the book would be over.
“莉琪，我们今天要做巧克力饼干！” 尼娜大喊。
莉琪笑了。“我喜欢饼干。” 她说。也许巧克力饼干可以让她糟糕的一天变成开心的一天。
"Izzie! We're making chocolate chip cookies today!" Nina shouted.
Izzie smiled. "I love cookies," she said. Maybe chocolate chip cookies would turn her bad day into a good day.
“我也喜欢。” 雪莉老师说，“热乎乎的手工饼干很好吃。围上围裙开始准备吧！” 食材已经放在了桌子上。
"Me too," Miss Shelly said. "Nothing beats warm, homemade cookies. Put on your aprons and get ready to bake!" The ingredients were ready on the table.
“第一步：把一杯红糖和半杯白糖混合起来。” 贾森念道。
“第二步：加入切好的黄油，搅拌。” 伊坦说。他把糖和黄油搅拌起来。
"Step 1: Mix one cup brown sugar and half a cup white sugar," Jason read.
"Step 2: Add chopped butter and mix well," Ethan said. He stirred the sugar and butter together.
“第三步：加两个鸡蛋。” 莉琪说。她打了鸡蛋。
“第四步：加一茶匙的香草香精。” 波比说。
“搅拌、搅拌、搅拌！” 尼娜提醒伊坦。
"Step 3: Add two eggs," Izzie said, cracking an egg.
"Step 4: Add one teaspoon of vanilla," Bobby said.
"And stir, stir, stir!" Nina reminded Ethan.
“现在，在另一个碗里混合干食材。然后我们要一点一点地把干食材加进湿食材里。” 雪莉老师说。
“二又四分之一杯面粉。” 波比念道。
“一茶匙小苏打。” 贾森说。
"Now mix the dry ingredients in a different bowl. Then we'll add them into the wet ingredients little by little," Miss Shelly said.
"Two and a quarter cups of flour," Bobby read.
"One teaspoon baking soda," Jason said.
“一茶匙盐。” 尼娜说。
“还有巧克力碎！” 莉琪去拿巧克力碎。突然，她感到头晕。她坐下来，发现自己的头有点疼。
"One teaspoon salt," Nina said.
"And chocolate chips!" Izzie reached for the bag of chocolate chips. Suddenly she felt dizzy. She sat down and realized she had a headache.
“雪莉老师，我头疼。” 莉琪说。
“不好了。” 雪莉老师很担心，“尼娜，铺一些垫子让莉琪躺下。男生们，把干食材混合进去。” 
尼娜去柜子里拿出几块垫子。
"Miss Shelly? My head hurts," Izzie said.
"Oh no." Miss Shelly sounded concerned. "Nina, set up some mats for Izzie to lie down on. Boys, mix in the dry ingredients."
Nina went to the closet and pulled out some gym mats.
男生们准备好了食材。“把饼干面团放到烤盘上。哦！有人预热烤箱了吗？” 雪莉老师突然问。
“我预热了。” 贾森咧嘴笑着说。
The boys were ready to bake. "Drop spoonfuls of cookie dough on the baking tray. Oh! Did someone remember to preheat the toaster oven?" Miss Shelly suddenly asked.
"I did." Jason grinned.
“谢谢。” 雪莉老师松了一口气。“希望饼干烤好时，莉琪也会好起来。” 她说。尼娜回来了。“她还好吗？” 雪莉老师小声问。
尼娜点点头。“她躺下来了。应该已经睡着了！” 
"Thanks." Miss Shelly looked relieved. "I hope Izzie feels better by the time the cookies are done," she said. Then Nina came back to the table. "Is she all right?" Miss Shelly asked quietly.
Nina nodded. "She's lying down. I think she fell asleep already!"
“用190度烤十分钟。” 波比念道，“对吗，雪莉老师？” 
“对！190度，十分钟。” 雪莉老师说。她叹了口气。“我们开始清理吧。” 
"Bake for ten minutes at 190 degrees," Bobby read. "Right, Miss Shelly?"
"Yes! 190 degrees. Ten minutes," Miss Shelly said. She let out a sigh. "Let's clean up, everyone."
“好香啊。” 波比说，“我可以吃一个吗？” 
“先等一下。” 贾森说。
“先把饼干放凉。” 雪莉老师说。
“雪莉老师，莉琪可能想吃饼干。” 尼娜说。
"They smell good," Bobby said. "Can I eat one?"
"We have to let them cool first," Jason said.
"Put them on the cooling rack," Miss Shelly said.
"Miss Shelly, maybe Izzie would like a cookie," Nina said.
“你说得对。你去叫醒她问问吧。” 雪莉老师说。
“我们一起去！把饼干带给她。” 伊坦说。
“莉琪，你感觉好一点了吗？” 尼娜问。
"You're right. Go wake her up and ask," Miss Shelly said.
"We'll all go! And we'll bring her some cookies," Ethan said.
"Hey, Izzie. Are you feeling better?" Nina asked.
莉琪坐起来，打了个哈欠。“嗯，我可能只是需要休息一下。” 
“我们带了饼干给你。” 贾森说。
“谢谢！对不起，我没怎么帮忙。” 莉琪咬了一口饼干，“嗯！烤得真棒！” 她笑了。糟糕的一天终于结束了。
Izzie sat up and yawned. "Yeah. I think I just needed a nap."
"We brought you cookies," Jason said.
"Thanks! Sorry I didn't help more." Izzie bit into a cookie. "Mmm! Good job, bakers!" She smiled. Her bad day was finally over.
需要准备：
-一杯红糖
-半杯白糖
-225克切好的黄油
-两个鸡蛋
-一茶匙香草香精
-二又四分之一杯面粉
-一茶匙小苏打
-一茶匙盐
-350克巧克力碎
Things You'll Need:
-1 cup brown sugar
-1/2 cup white sugar
-225 grams butter, chopped
-2 eggs
-1 teaspoon vanilla
-2 ¼ cups flour
-1 teaspoon baking soda
-1 teaspoon salt
-350 grams chocolate chips
自己试试吧：
1) 烤箱预热到190摄氏度。
2) 混合黄油和糖。
3) 加入两个鸡蛋。
4) 加入香草香精，搅拌。
5) 在另外一个碗里，混合面粉、小苏打、盐和巧克力碎。
6) 混合干食材和湿食材。
7) 把饼干面团放到烤盘上。
8) 烤十分钟。
9) 品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Preheat oven to 190˚C.
2) Mix the butter and sugar.
3) Add two eggs.
4) Add vanilla and mix well.
5) In a separate bowl, mix the flour, baking soda, salt, and chocolate chips.
6) Mix the dry ingredients with the wet ingredients.
7) Drop spoonfuls of cookie dough onto a baking tray.
8) Bake for 10 minutes.
9) Enjoy!
贾森一整天都在玩儿电子游戏。他忙着要把游戏升级到第五级。
现在，他一边走向儿童中心，一边打龙。他正在打第四级的最后一战……咚！他撞到了尼娜。
Jason hadn't put down his video game all day. He was too busy trying to reach level five of his game.
Right now he was battling dragons on the way to Kids Central. He was about to reach the final battle of level four when . . . Smack! He walked right into Nina.
“走路时小心点！” 尼娜大喊。
“对不起，尼娜，我正要……” 贾森说。
"Watch where you're going!" she cried.
"Sorry, Nina. I'm trying to finish . . ." he said.
“把电子游戏收起来吧。” 雪莉老师提醒贾森，“今天的活动需要一本英文词典！” 
波比抱怨，“词典？为什么？” 
"It's time to put the video game away," Miss Shelly reminded Jason. "For today's activity, you'll need an English dictionary!"
Bobby groaned. "A dictionary? Why?"
雪莉老师拿起一张厚纸，上面写着她的英文名字。“我们要做英文名字诗书签。” 
贾森把游戏机放进背包。“什么是英文名字诗？” 
Miss Shelly held up a thick piece of paper with her name on it. "We're making name poem bookmarks."
Jason tucked his game into his backpack. "What's a name poem?"
“是用你英文名里的字母写的诗。” 雪莉老师解释说，“比如说，我的英文名叫Marie。第一行就是第一个字母开头，第二行是第二个字母开头。每一行都要写出你的特点。” 
"It's a poem that uses the letters in your name," Miss Shelly explained. "My first name is Marie. So the first word in my poem will begin with the first letter. The next line will begin with the second letter. Every line should describe you."
“Magical（有魔法的）。” 伊坦说。
“什么，伊坦？” 雪莉老师问。
“您的诗的第一行。” 他说，“因为您像有魔法一样，让各种事情变得有趣。” 
"Magical," Ethan said.
"What's that, Ethan?" Miss Shelly asked.
"That could be the first word in your poem," he said. "Because like magic, you make things fun."
“为什么要用英文词典？” 尼娜问。
“你想不出来的时候，可以查词典。” 雪莉老师给大家发了一张空白的书签，“把名字诗写在这上面，就可以用它作书签了。” 
"What are the dictionaries for?" asked Nina.
"Dictionaries help when you can't think of a word." Miss Shelly handed out blank bookmarks. "Write your name poem on it, then you can use it as a bookmark."
贾森在纸上写下自己的英文名字Jason。字母J不容易作诗。“Jolly（欢乐的）？” 他想，“感觉像圣诞老人。” 接下来是字母A。他叹了口气。他写诗实在很糟糕。“Awful（糟糕）！英文的‘糟糕’是A开头的。” 
Jason scribbled his name on a piece of paper. J wasn't the easiest letter to start with. "Jolly?" he thought. "Sounds too much like Santa Claus." Next was A. He sighed. He was awful at writing poems. "Awful! 'Awful' begins with A!"
他看着字母S，打了个哈欠。“Sleepy（困的）！” 他想。这个比较简单。然后是字母O。贾森打开字典看字母O的第一页。大部分词他都不知道。他看了所有字母O开头的单词。
He stared at the S and yawned. "Sleepy!" he thought. That was easy. Then there was O. Jason opened the dictionary to the first page of Oo. There were mostly words he didn't know. He looked through all the letter O words.
他觉得“Odd（奇怪的）” 是唯一一个可以用的单词。
大家都写好后，雪莉老师让伊坦读一读他的诗。“我的英文名是Ethan， Excellent surfer（很棒的冲浪手）、Totally cool（非常酷）、Helpful（会帮助人）、Adventurous（爱冒险的）、New（新的）。” 他说，“因为我是新同学。” 
He decided that "odd" was the only O word that might work.
When everyone was finished, Miss Shelly called on Ethan to read his poem. "Excellent surfer, Totally cool, Helpful, Adventurous, and New," he read, "because I'm a new student."
下一个是贾森。“Jumpy（紧张的）、Awful（糟糕的）、Sleepy（困的）、Odd（奇怪的）、Nut（怪人）。” 他说。
“怪人？” 莉琪不太理解。
“我看到‘nut’这个单词的意思是奇怪或者很蠢的人。” 他说。
Jason was next. "Jumpy, Awful, Sleepy, Odd, Nut," he read.
"Nut?" Izzie asked, confused.
"I saw that 'nut' can mean a strange or silly person," he said.
“贾森，这些说的是你吗？” 雪莉老师问，“这些也可以，但是我可以想到更好的。” 
“对，比如说J可以是 ‘Jigsaw puzzle wizard (七巧板天才)’！” 波比说，“你玩儿七巧板很厉害。” 
"Jason, are you sure those words describe you?" Miss Shelly asked. "They're not bad words, but I could think of nicer words."
"Yeah, like J for 'Jigsaw puzzle wizard!'" Bobby said. "You're great at puzzles."
“ ‘A’可以是 ‘awesome’（很棒的）。” 尼娜说。
“ ‘S’可以是 ‘super’（超级的）。” 莉琪补充说，“或者 ‘sweet’（亲切的）。” 
“ ‘O’可以是 ‘only’（唯一的）。因为你是唯一一个把游戏打到第四级的人！” 伊坦说。
"And A for 'awesome,'" Nina said.
"S for 'super,'" Izzie added. "Or 'sweet.'"
"O for the 'only' person who can reach level four in the video game!" Ethan said.
贾森笑了，“你们都好厉害！” 他写下新诗。
“但留着‘怪人’吧。” 波比笑着说，“因为有时你确实很奇怪。” 
Jason smiled. "You guys are good at this!" He began writing his new poem.
"But keep N for 'nut,'" Bobby said, grinning, "because you can be pretty strange."
需要准备：
-剪刀
-一张纸或者纸板
-打孔器
-蝴蝶结或者线
-字典
-笔或者记号笔
Things You'll Need:
-scissors
-a piece of paper or cardboard
-a hole puncher
-ribbon or string
-a dictionary
-pens or markers
自己试试吧：
1) 把一张纸或者纸板剪成书签的形状。
2) 在一端打一个孔。
3) 穿过孔绑一个短蝴蝶结。
4) 用你英文名里的字母写一首诗。
5) 把诗分享给朋友和家人！
Do it Yourself:
1) Cut a piece of paper or cardboard into the shape of a bookmark.
2) Punch a hole at one end.
3) Tie a short piece of ribbon through the hole.
4) Write a name poem using the letters in your name.
5) Share your name poem with your friends or family!
“星期六在苹果园好玩儿吗？” 尼娜问莉琪。她们正要去儿童中心。

"Did you have fun at the apple orchard on Saturday?" Nina asked Izzie. They were on their way to Kids Central.
"It was so fun!" Izzie said. "We picked all kinds of apples. Green, yellow, red . . . And we put them in cute wooden barrels."
女生们走进体育馆。“哦！就像那种木桶！” 莉琪指着桌子上的一个小木桶说。木桶里装满了苹果。

The girls walked into the gym. "Oh! Just like those!" Izzie pointed to a small barrel on the table. It was filled with apples.

“首先，把苹果切成两半。然后放在纸巾上，让它变干。伊坦，你可以帮忙分纸巾吗？” 雪莉老师问。
莉琪看了看颜料罐。“我们要用什么颜色？” 
"First cut the apple in half. Then press it onto a paper towel to dry it off. Ethan, would you please pass the paper towels around?" Miss Shelly asked.
Izzie glanced at the jars of paint. "What colors are we using?"
“基本的颜色我们都有。” 雪莉老师说，“如果你想要更多的颜色，就把它们混合起来！准备好了吗？”

"I want to make the perfect green," Izzie thought.
雪莉老师把纸盘分给大家。“把你的苹果在颜料里压一下。然后用力压在袋子上。” 她说，“压几秒，压出一个完整的苹果！” 
Miss Shelly passed out paper plates for the paint. "Press your apple into the paint. Then press it firmly onto the fabric," she said. "Hold it down for a few seconds. You want to make sure the whole stamp stamps!"
莉琪把蓝色的颜料倒进纸盘里。然后她加了一点黄色，搅拌了一下。接着她加了一点白色。这就是她喜欢的绿色。她把苹果放进颜料里，盖了印。
Izzie poured blue paint onto her plate. Then she added some yellow and mixed. Next she added a little white. That's her favorite green color. She dipped her apple in the paint and stamped.
她压着苹果。突然，她的手滑了一下！“不好！” 她大喊。
“哈哈。看上去像一颗流星。” 伊坦说。

She was pressing and pressing when her hand slipped! "Oh no!" she cried.
"Ha-ha! It looks like a shooting star," Ethan said.
"A shooting apple!" Bobby said.
“雪莉老师，莉琪做了一个很酷的流苹果！” 尼娜说。
“一点都不酷。” 莉琪说，“太丑了！”

"Miss Shelly, Izzie made a cool shooting apple!" Nina said.
"It doesn't look cool," moaned Izzie. "It looks dumb!"
"Well, I think it looks cool!" said Nina. "I'm going to make one too!"
“你的苹果印很有艺术感。” 雪莉老师说。
“谢谢。” 莉琪说，“但是，现在我要盖一个普通的印了。” 她又盖了一次。这次很完美。“看！” 莉琪拿起袋子，上面有一个流苹果和一个普通的苹果。
"I think your apple stamp looks very artistic," said Miss Shelly.
"Thanks," Izzie said. "But I'm going to make a regular stamp now." She stamped her bag again. This time it was perfect. "Ta-da!" Izzie held up her bag with one shooting apple and one regular apple.
莉琪还装饰了苹果。然后她在袋子下面写上自己的名字。她想让大家知道，这是她做的有艺术感的袋子。
Next Izzie decorated the apple. Then she wrote her name at the bottom of the bag. She wanted everyone to know this was her very artistic lunch bag.
大家坐在地毯上吃苹果。
“哈哈！这个苹果的形状很奇怪。” 贾森说。
“这个形状不奇怪。” 莉琪说。她看了看雪莉老师，笑了。“这个形状很有艺术感。” 
Later everyone sat on the rug munching apples.
"Ha! This apple is a funny shape," Jason cried.
"It's not a funny shape," Izzie said. She looked at Miss Shelly and smiled. "It's artistic."

-苹果
-刀

-纸盘
-颜料
-需要装饰的布袋（或者卡纸）
-胶水
-珠子和扣子
-记号笔
Things You'll Need:
-apples
-a knife
-paper towels
-paper plates
-paint
-cloth bag (or construction paper) to decorate
-glue
-beads and buttons
-markers
自己试试吧：
1) 把苹果切成两半。
2) 把苹果的切面放在纸巾上弄干。
3) 把颜料倒进纸盘。
4) 用苹果放进颜料里。
5) 把苹果压在布或者卡纸上。
6) 多印几个，或者用珠子、扣子或记号笔装饰！
Do it Yourself:
1) Cut an apple in half.
2) Press the apple, cut-side down, onto a paper towel to dry it.
3) Pour paint onto a paper plate.
4) Dip the apple into paint.
5) Press the apple onto the cloth or paper.
6) Add more stamps or decorate with beads, buttons, or markers!
今天是星期五。波比很兴奋。他非常期待周末。星期天，他要和爸爸一起去看足球比赛。
It was Friday. Bobby was very excited. He couldn't wait for the weekend. He was going to see a football game with his dad on Sunday.
“我带了瓶子。” 他走进儿童中心说。
“很好。” 雪莉老师说，“我们开始做糖和酵母气球吧。” 
“我不知道那是什么，但是听起来很酷！” 波比说。
"I brought my bottle," he said as he walked into Kids Central.
"Great," Miss Shelly said. "Let's start to make a sugar and yeast balloon."
"Whatever that is, it sounds cool!" Bobby said.
“糖能给我们能量。我们要给酵母一些糖。” 雪莉老师说，“会发生什么呢？气球会膨胀吗？” 雪莉老师吹了吹气球。“还是不会？” 她给气球放气。
"You know sugar gives you energy. We're going to give yeast some sugar," Miss Shelly said. "What will happen? Will the balloons blow up?" Miss Shelly blew air into a balloon. "Or not?" She let out all the air.
“酵母会让面包膨胀。” 贾森说，“所以我觉得它会把气球吹起来。” 
“糖和酵母怎么会把气球吹起来呢？” 波比问。他摇摇头。“我觉得不会。”  
"Yeast makes bread rise," Jason said. "So I think it will make our balloons blow up."
"How can sugar and yeast blow up a balloon?" Bobby asked. He shook his head. "I don't think it will work."
“那我们试试吧。” 雪莉老师说，“把一汤匙糖放进瓶子里。我拿热水过来。” 
波比小心地把糖放进瓶子里。他马上举起手。“雪莉老师，我准备好了！” 
"Let's try and find out," Miss Shelly said. "Drop one tablespoon of sugar into your bottle. I'll come around with warm water."
Bobby carefully put the sugar into his bottle. He shot his arm up in the air. "I'm ready for water, Miss Shelly!"
雪莉老师把温水倒进他的瓶子里。“现在摇一摇！” 她说。波比用力摇了摇。
“好了，波比。加酵母，把气球套在瓶口，然后轻轻摇一摇！” 
Miss Shelly poured warm water into his bottle. "Now shake!" she said. Bobby shook as hard as he could.
"That's good enough, Bobby. Next add the yeast. Then put the balloon on. Gently shake it up!"
波比把一袋酵母倒进瓶子里。他把蓝色气球套在瓶口。然后他又轻轻地摇了摇瓶子。“什么都没发生。” 他抱怨道。
“要有耐心。” 雪莉老师说，“我们去外面边玩儿边等吧。” 
Bobby emptied the packet of yeast into the bottle. He put a blue balloon on the top of the bottle. Then he shook the bottle again, gently. "Nothing's happening," he complained.
"Be patient," Miss Shelly said. "Let's go outside while we wait."
“哦！” 大家一回来，莉琪就尖叫道，“我的气球变大了！” 大家跑到莉琪的座位。
波比跑到自己的座位。“我的也变大了！” 
"Oh!" Izzie shrieked when they got back. "My balloon is getting bigger!" Everyone ran to Izzie's bottle on the table.
Bobby dashed to his seat. "Mine's growing too!"
“太奇怪了。” 贾森看着气球说。
“为什么会变大？” 尼娜问，“是谁把它吹大的？” 
"That is so weird," Jason said, examining his own balloon.
"How is it getting bigger?" Nina asked. "Who's blowing it up? "
“是糖和酵母。酵母其实是活着的，但它平时处在一个安静的睡眠状态。当和水、糖混合时，它又活跃起来。” 雪莉老师解释说。
"The sugar and the yeast are doing it. Yeast is actually alive. But it's in a quiet, sleeping stage in the packet. When mixed with water and sugar, it becomes active again," Miss Shelly explained.
“当酵母吃了糖，它会产生气体，跑到气球里。有了气体，气球就被吹大了，就像我们吹气球时一样！理解了吗？” 雪莉老师问。
"When yeast eats sugar, it creates gas that fills the balloon. The balloon gets bigger to make room for the gas. Just like it gets bigger when we blow into it! Does that make sense?" Miss Shelly asked.
一个高高的男人走进了体育馆。“大家在做什么？” 他问。
“爸爸！快看！” 波比大喊，“我们把酵母、糖和水装在瓶子里混合起来。产生的气体把气球吹大了！” 
A tall man entered the gym. "What's going on in here?" he asked.
"Dad! Look at this!" Bobby shouted. "We mixed yeast, sugar, and water in a bottle. That created gas that blew up this balloon!"
“听上去很有意思。” 波比的爸爸说。
“再过几个小时，你们会看到酵母没有了糖会发生什么。” 雪莉老师说。
“什么？还有事情会发生？” 波比问。
"That sounds interesting," Bobby's dad said.
"And in a few hours, you'll see what happens when the yeast runs out of sugar to eat," Miss Shelly said.
"What? You mean there's more?" Bobby asked.
“把气球带回家，我们在家里观察吧。” 他爸爸说。
波比很兴奋。他可以和爸爸一起看足球和气球。这个周末一定很棒！
"Take your balloon home, and we'll watch it there," his dad said.
Bobby was thrilled. He'd get to watch football and his balloon with his dad. It was going to be a great weekend!
需要准备：
-空的500毫升塑料瓶
-一汤匙的糖
-四分之一杯温水
-一袋干酵母（二又四分之一茶匙）
-一个气球
Things You'll Need:
-an empty 500 ml plastic bottle
-1 tablespoon sugar
-1/4 cup very warm water
-1 packet dry yeast (2 ¼ teaspoons)
-a balloon
自己试试吧：
1) 糖和温水混合后摇一摇。
2) 加入一袋干酵母。
3) 把气球套在瓶口。
4) 轻轻摇瓶子。
5) 等等看会发生什么！
Do It Yourself:
1) Mix the sugar and warm water in a bottle. Shake.
2) Add one packet of dry yeast.
3) Put the balloon over the open end of the bottle.
4) Shake the bottle gently.
5) Watch and wait to see what happens!
今天是感恩节放假的前一天。尼娜很感谢，因为老师没有布置作业！
Today was the last day of school before Thanksgiving vacation. And Nina was already feeling thankful because her teacher hadn't given the class any homework!
儿童中心里，莉琪戴着一个印第安头饰。这是她在美术课上做的。“我感谢印第安人让我们吃到玉米。我喜欢玉米。” 她蹦蹦跳跳，“哦！我还感谢漂亮的花！”

"Take one piece of paper and fold it in half. Open it back up, and arrange your flowers on the inside. Make sure the flowers don't touch each other. Then fold it shut again."
“真可爱，像一本小小的花书。” 尼娜说。

"Cute. It's like a little flower book," Nina said.

Nina followed Miss Shelly's directions exactly.

需要准备：
-小朵的鲜花
-几张薄纸
-厚厚的、带硬皮封面的书
-空白的卡片
-胶水
-小的颜料刷
Things You'll Need
-small, freshly picked flowers
-pieces of thin paper
-a very heavy, hardcover book
-blank cards
-glue
-a small paintbrush
自己试试吧：
1) 准备一些花，确认花瓣是干的。
2) 把一张纸对折。
3) 打开纸，把花平放在里面。
4) 合上纸。
5) 把花放在一本厚厚的、有硬皮封面的书里。
6) 几个星期后，小心拿出压好的干花。
7) 把花粘在空白的卡片上。
8) 为特别的人做一张漂亮的卡片！
Do It Yourself:
1) Prepare some flowers. Make sure the petals are not wet.
2) Fold a piece of paper in half.
3) Open the paper and lay the flowers flat inside.
4) Fold the paper shut again.
5) Place the flowers in a thick, hardcover book.
6) After a few weeks, carefully remove your dried, pressed flowers.
7) Glue them onto a blank card.
8) Create a beautiful card for someone special!
伊坦正走向儿童中心。他想象着海边。突然，有人拍了拍他的肩膀。“啊！” 他吓了一跳，转过身去。
Ethan walked down the hallway towards Kids Central. He was daydreaming about the beach. Suddenly someone tapped him on the shoulder. "Ah!" He turned around, startled.
“呃，我只是想说你好！” 波比说。他用手指转着篮球。
伊坦叹了口气。“我很想念放学后去冲浪的日子。我也很想念海边我最喜欢的墨西哥卷饼店。” 
"Yikes. I was just saying hello!" Bobby said. He twirled a basketball on his finger.
Ethan sighed. "I miss going surfing after school. And I miss eating at my favorite taco stand on the beach."
“今天可能是你的幸运日。” 波比说，“雪莉老师围着围裙呢。” 
“我们要做什么？” 贾森问。他看着桌上的食材。
"Today might be your lucky day," Bobby said. "Miss Shelly has her apron on."
"What are we making?" Jason asked. He looked at all the ingredients on the table.
“墨西哥卷饼！” 雪莉老师说。
伊坦的眼睛睁大了。“您记得我说想做墨西哥卷饼！” 
“你可以在旁边帮我。” 雪莉老师说。
"Tacos!" Miss Shelly said.
Ethan's eyes grew big. "You remembered my idea to make tacos!"
"You can stand aside and help me," she said.
“我不知道怎么做。” 伊坦说，“我只知道怎么吃！” 大家哈哈大笑。
“什么是墨西哥卷饼？” 尼娜问。
"I don't know how to make them," Ethan said. "I just know how to eat them!" Everyone laughed.
"What's a taco?" Nina asked.
雪莉老师拿起一个墨西哥卷饼。“墨西哥卷饼长这样， 是一个硬硬的玉米壳。你可以在里面放不同的东西。” 
“比如说？” 尼娜问。
雪莉老师看着伊坦。
Miss Shelly picked one up. "A taco looks like this, it is a hard corn shell. You fill it with many different things."
"Like what?" asked Nina.
Miss Shelly looked at Ethan.
“嗯，肉。” 他说，“豆、米饭、生菜。” 
“没错！” 雪莉老师说，“我们今天准备了碎牛肉、黑豆、米饭、生菜、芝士和莎莎酱。” 
"Um, meat," he began. "Beans, rice, lettuce."
"Exactly!" Miss Shelly said. "Our fillings for today are ground beef, black beans, rice, lettuce, cheese, and salsa."
“选你想要的食材。把食材扔进饼壳里，就可以了！” 雪莉老师说。
“扔进饼壳里？” 波比重复说，“是不是说我们可以把饼壳扔起来呢？像披萨一样？” 他笑着问雪莉老师。
"Pick which ingredients you want. Toss them in your shell, and you're finished!" Miss Shelly said.
"Toss them in the shell?" Bobby repeated. "Does that mean we throw the shell in the air? Like a pizza?" He grinned at Miss Shelly.
“不是。” 雪莉老师皱着眉说，“不可以把东西扔起来。” 她对伊坦说：“你要先来吗？让大家看看怎么做墨西哥卷饼！” 
“当然了！” 伊坦拿起一个饼壳。
"No," Miss Shelly said with a frown. "It does not mean we throw anything in the air." She turned to Ethan. "Would you like to go first? Show everyone how to make a taco!"
"Sure!" Ethan picked up a taco shell.
“先放米饭，然后放肉。这样饼壳才不会变软。” 伊坦沿着桌子走，“然后加生菜。我不加莎莎酱，因为我不喜欢番茄！” 
"First I put rice in. Then I put the meat on top of the rice. That way it doesn't make the shell soggy." Ethan moved down the table. "Then I add lettuce. Then I skip the salsa, because I don't like tomatoes!"
他撒了一点芝士。“好了！” 
“看上去挺简单的。下一个我来！” 尼娜说。她放了豆、米饭和莎莎酱。
He sprinkled some cheese on top. "Done!"
"That looks easy. I'll go next!" Nina said. She filled her taco with beans, rice, and salsa.
大家做好后，拿着盘子坐到地毯上。
“哦！” 莉琪大叫，“这个墨西哥卷饼软软的，我弄得乱七八糟！” 她的饼壳碎成两块。
When everyone was finished, they carried their plates to the rug.
"Uh-oh," Izzie cried. "These are super sloppy tacos. I just made a mess!" Her taco shell had broken in half. There was a big blob of meat on her plate. There was even more salsa on her shirt.
盘子上掉了一大块肉。连她的衣服上都有莎莎酱。尼娜咯咯笑。
“我说过不要把肉放在最下面！” 伊坦笑着说。接着，大家都笑了起来，包括莉琪。
“墨西哥卷饼真好吃。虽然吃起来很麻烦。” 莉琪说。
Nina began to giggle.
"I warned you about putting meat on the bottom!" Ethan said, laughing. Then everyone was laughing, even Izzie.
"The taco is really good. Even if it is messy," Izzie said.
大家都准备回家了。“谢谢你做墨西哥卷饼的建议。” 雪莉老师对伊坦说，“这次非常成功。” 
“我还有其他好想法。” 伊坦说，“下次我们去海边玩儿，怎么样？” 
Soon it was time to go home. "Thanks for the idea of making tacos," Miss Shelly said to Ethan. "They were a big hit."
"I have other great ideas too," Ethan said. "How about next time we take a trip to the beach?"
需要准备：
-墨西哥卷饼壳
-450克煮熟的碎牛肉（用番茄酱、辣椒粉、洋葱、蒜、孜然和盐腌制）
-一杯切好的生菜
-一杯切好的芝士
-一瓶莎莎酱
-两杯煮好的米饭
-一罐黑豆（425克）
Things You'll Need:
-taco shells
-450 grams cooked ground beef (seasoned with tomato paste, chili powder, onion, garlic, cumin, and salt)
-1 cup shredded lettuce
-1 cup shredded cheese
-one jar of salsa
-2 cups cooked rice
-one can of black beans (425 grams)

1) 把喜欢的食材放进饼壳。
2) 品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Fill a taco shell with your choice of ingredients.
2) Enjoy!
莉琪不敢相信自己的眼睛。地上有很多呼啦圈。有大呼啦圈、小呼啦圈、彩色的呼啦圈。
Izzie could not believe her eyes. On the floor of the gym were hula hoops. Big hula hoops. Small hula hoops. Colorful hula hoops.
“雪莉老师！您怎么知道？” 莉琪大声说。
“你好，莉琪。知道什么？” 雪莉老师问。
“我喜欢呼啦圈！” 莉琪说，“上个星期的生日，我收到了一个。” 
"Miss Shelly! How did you know?" Izzie burst out.
"Hi, Izzie. How did I know what?" Miss Shelly looked puzzled.
"I love hula hoops!" Izzie said. "I got one for my birthday last week."
“是吗？那太好了。今天你会学到一些呼啦圈游戏。” 雪莉老师说。
“游戏？” 莉琪皱了皱眉，“我只是喜欢转呼啦圈。” 
"I didn't know. That's great. Today you'll learn some hula hoop games," Miss Shelly said.
"Games?" Izzie frowned. "I like to just twirl it around my hips."
“穿上外套，拿一个呼啦圈。” 雪莉老师说。
莉琪拿了一个有绿色和粉色条纹的呼啦圈。
"Put on your coats and grab a hoop," Miss Shelly said.
Izzie grabbed a hoop with green and pink stripes.
“天很阴。” 尼娜搓着手说。
“放下呼啦圈。” 雪莉老师说，“手拉手围成一个圈。” 
莉琪叹了口气。什么时候才能转呼啦圈呢？
"The sky is so gray," Nina said, rubbing her hands.
"Put down your hoops," Miss Shelly said. "Join hands and make a circle."
Izzie sighed. When would they get to hula hoop?
“第一个活动，我们要一起合作。” 雪莉老师说，“我可以站在这里吗？” 她走到莉琪和贾森中间。她拉起贾森的手。在拉莉琪的手之前，她在手臂上挂了个呼啦圈。
"For the first activity, we have to work as a team," Miss Shelly said. "Can I join here?" She stepped into the circle between Izzie and Jason. She joined hands with Jason. Before she took Izzie's hand, she put her arm through a hula hoop.
“我们要传递呼啦圈。但是，不能放手。” 雪莉老师说。
“什么？那要怎么传递？” 莉琪问。
雪莉老师笑了。“你会知道的。” 
"We're going to pass the hula hoop around the circle. But we can't let go of each other's hands," Miss Shelly said.
"What? How will we pass it?" Izzie asked.
Miss Shelly smiled. "You'll figure it out."
雪莉老师低下肩膀。呼啦圈滑到莉琪的左臂。莉琪把头穿过去。然后她扭动身体穿过去。她把腿伸出去，呼啦圈到了她的右臂！“我成功了！” 她尖叫道，“尼娜，到你了！” 
Miss Shelly lowered her shoulder. The hula hoop slipped down to Izzie's left arm. Izzie put her head through it. Then she wriggled the rest of her body through. She stepped out of it and it was on her right arm! "I did it!" she squealed. "Nina, your turn!"
尼娜也跟莉琪一样穿了过去。很快，呼啦圈就到了波比的手臂上。波比传给伊坦。伊坦传给贾森。贾森传给雪莉老师。呼啦圈传了一圈！
“我们成功了！” 贾森大喊。大家都欢呼起来。
Nina did what Izzie did. Soon the hoop was around Bobby's arm. Bobby moved it to Ethan. Ethan moved it to Jason, and Jason moved it to Miss Shelly. It made a full circle!
"We did it!" Jason cried. Everyone cheered.
“大家是怎么做到的？” 雪莉老师问。
波比大声说：“我得看尼娜的动作。如果她弯下身，我也得弯下身。” 
"How did you make it?" Miss Shelly asked.
Bobby spoke up. "I had to watch whenever Nina moved. If she bent down, I had to bend down too."
莉琪点点头。“最难的部分就是不能放手。我们什么时候可以转呼啦圈呢？” 她问。
“快了。” 雪莉老师说，“在地上滚呼啦圈，然后在它停下来的地方转呼啦圈！” 
Izzie nodded. "The hardest part was not letting go of each other's hands. Now when do we get to hula hoop?" she asked.
"Very soon," Miss Shelly said. "Roll your hula hoop on the blacktop. Wherever it lands, start hula hooping!"
莉琪脱下外套，颤抖着。她的呼啦圈在地上滚，她跟着它跑。当呼啦圈停下来时，她转起呼啦圈。呼啦圈转呀转，真有意思！她好像在一个呼啦圈的乐园里！
Izzie took off her jacket and shivered. Her hoop was rolling on the ground, and she ran after it. When it stopped, she started to spin it. The hula hoop flew around and around. It was so much fun! She was in hula hooping heaven!!
她看着尼娜。她也在转呼啦圈。男生们的呼啦圈却一直掉下来。莉琪觉得，她可以一直转下去。她看了看天空。天在变黑。突然，有个湿湿的东西落到她的脸上。
She looked at Nina. She was hula hooping too. The boys kept dropping theirs though. Izzie felt like she could hula hoop forever. She looked up at the sky. It was getting dark. Suddenly something wet landed on her face.
“是雪花！” 尼娜大喊。下雪了！
“我从来没见过雪！” 伊坦说。
“耶！” 莉琪大喊。她很喜欢雪。“呼啦圈真好玩儿！在雪里转呼啦圈更好玩儿！” 
"Snowflakes!" Nina cried. It was starting to snow!
"I've never seen real snow!" Ethan said.
"Hooray!" Izzie cried. Snow was her favorite thing about winter. "Hooray for hula hoops! Hooray for hula hooping in the snow!"

-大呼啦圈
-一群朋友
Things You'll Need:
-a large hula hoop
-a group of friends
自己试试吧：
1) 让一个人把呼啦圈放在肩膀上。
2) 手拉手站成圆圈。
3) 在圆圈里传递呼啦圈。不能放手！
4) 大家一起合作，开心玩儿游戏吧！
Do It Yourself
1) Have someone put a hula hoop around his or her shoulder.
2) Stand in a circle and hold hands.
3) Pass the hula hoop around the circle. Do not let go of each other's hands!
4) Use teamwork and have fun!
伊坦不敢相信外面这么冷。在休息时间，他穿了毛衣和外套，围了围巾，戴了帽子和手套。但他还是很冷！
“今天在外面活动！穿厚一点。” 雪莉老师在伊坦走进门时说。
Ethan couldn't believe how cold it was outside. At recess he wore a sweater, coat, scarf, hat, and mittens. But he was still cold!
"Today's activity is outside! Bundle up," Miss Shelly said as Ethan walked in the door.
“外面？” 伊坦问，“但是太冷了！” 
“很好玩儿的。” 波比说，“你会习惯的。” 
伊坦不想在外面活动。但他还是拉上了外套拉链。
"Outside?" Ethan asked. "But it's freezing!"
"It's fun," Bobby said. "You'll get used to it."
Ethan didn't want to have activities outside. But he zipped up his coat anyway.
昨晚下雪了，现在地上都是雪。伊坦穿着新靴子小心地走着。他不习惯在雪地里走。他害怕滑倒。
The ground was covered in snow from the snowstorm last night. Ethan walked carefully in his brand-new boots. He wasn't used to walking in the snow. He was afraid he'd slip.
“我们在外面做什么？” 伊坦问。
“有很多在雪里玩儿的方法！” 尼娜说。
“今天我们要玩儿雪地拔河的游戏。” 雪莉老师说。
"What are we doing out here?" Ethan asked.
"There are so many ways to play in the snow!" Nina said.
"Today we're playing snowy tug-of-war," said their teacher.
“贾森和伊坦，你们一队。” 雪莉老师说，“波比、尼娜、莉琪，你们一队。你们一起选个队名和代表颜色。” 
波比叹了口气。“我为什么在女生队？” 
"Jason and Ethan, you're a team," Miss Shelly instructed. "Bobby, Nina, and Izzie, you're a team. Together choose a team name and a team color."
Bobby groaned. "Why am I on the girls' team?"
“你拔河厉害吗？” 伊坦问贾森。
贾森摇摇头。“我很糟糕。” 他说。
“那我们就是糟糕队。” 伊坦说。

"Are you good at tug-of-war?" Ethan asked Jason.
Jason shook his head. "I stink," he said.
"Great. Let's be the Stinkers," Ethan said.
"Ha-ha! Okay. And our team color will be green," said Jason.
“给你们看看紫雏菊队的力量！” 莉琪大喊。
“给你们看看绿糟糕队的力量！” 贾森回答。
波比摇摇头。“真不敢相信我们的队叫紫雏菊队。” 
"Get ready to lose to the Purple Daisies," Izzie cried.

Bobby shook his head. "I can't believe our team is called the Purple Daisies."
“紫雏菊队，在雪里画一条线。” 雪莉老师给尼娜一瓶紫色的液体。
“这是什么？” 尼娜问。
“雪地颜料，是食物色素和水的混合物。” 她说。
"Purple Daisies, draw your team line in the snow." Miss Shelly handed Nina a bottle filled with purple liquid.
"What's this?" Nina asked.
"Snow paint, which is food coloring mixed with water," she said.
“线要画在哪里呢？” 波比问。
雪莉老师拿起一个卷尺。“两条线隔两米，每条线两米长。” 她说。
伊坦和尼娜在雪里画了线。
"Where do the team lines go?" Bobby asked.
Miss Shelly held up a tape measure. "They should be two meters apart and two meters long," she said.
Ethan and Nina drew their lines in the snow.
“这是绳子的中心。” 雪莉老师指着绳子上绑着的小旗，“先把小旗拉到自己的线的队伍赢。另外一个规则是不能摔倒！如果有人摔倒，那个队伍就输！” 
"This is the center of the rope." Miss Shelly pointed to a flag tied to the rope. "The first team to pull the flag over their line wins. The other rule is that no one can fall down! If anyone does, the team loses!"
伊坦看了看自己的靴子。“不能摔倒？” 他担心地想。
“排好队，准备好！” 雪莉老师喊道。
“最强的人在后面。” 波比说。
Ethan looked down at his boots. "No one can fall?" he thought, worried.
"Line up and get ready!" Miss Shelly called.
"The strongest person goes in the back," Bobby said.
“我们可以的！” 伊坦小声对贾森说。
雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。“开始！” 
伊坦马上感觉到一股很强的拉力。伊坦和贾森跌跌撞撞地往前。“哦，不。” 伊坦说。
"We can do it!" Ethan whispered to Jason.
Miss Shelly blew her whistle. "Go!"
Right away Ethan felt a strong tug. Ethan and Jason stumbled forward. "Oh, no," Ethan said.
伊坦把靴子插进雪里。他紧闭着眼睛，用力拉。他和贾森慢慢往后。小旗在往他们这边移动！他更用力拉。但这时，紫雏菊队也用力地拉了一下！
Ethan dug his boots into the snow. He squeezed his eyes shut and pulled hard. He and Jason stepped back. They were moving the flag toward their team line! He tugged harder. But then the Purple Daisies gave a huge tug!
伊坦脚一滑，摔倒在雪里。
“紫雏菊队赢了！绿糟糕队输了！” 莉琪大喊。
伊坦哈哈大笑。摔倒在雪里其实没那么糟糕，还很有意思！他站起来大喊：“再玩儿一次吧！” 
Ethan slipped and landed on his back in the snow.
"Purple Daisies win! Green Stinkers lose!" Izzie shouted.
Ethan laughed. Falling in the snow wasn't bad. It was fun! He stood up and yelled, "Let's play again!"
需要准备：
-一条长长的粗绳子
-一块布（用来作小旗）或者一条彩色的带子
-食物色素
-水
-空塑料瓶
Things You'll Need:
-a long, thick rope
-a piece of cloth (to use as the flag) or a piece of colored tape
-food coloring
-water
-empty plastic bottles
自己试试吧：
1) 把布或带子绑在绳子中间。
2) 把食物色素和水混合在瓶子里，做成雪地颜料。
3) 用雪地颜料在雪地里画出两个队的线。
4) 开始时，让小旗在两条线中间。
5) 一个人说 “开始” 以后，两个队开始拉。
6) 先把小旗拉到自己的线内的队伍获胜。
7) 如果有人摔倒，那个人所在的队就输。
8) 玩儿到大家都累得爬不起来吧！
Do It Yourself:
1) Tie the cloth or tape around the center of the rope.
2) Mix the food coloring and water in a bottle to make snow paint.
3) Draw two team lines in the snow using the snow paint.
4) Start with the flag in the middle of the two team lines.
5) When someone says "Go," the two teams start pulling.
6) The first team to pull the flag over its line wins.
7) If anyone falls down, his or her team loses.
8) Play until you get so tired that you all fall down!
贾森看着窗外的雨。儿童中心今天在室内活动。外面太湿了。

“贾森，你来开始吧。” 雪莉老师说。
“沥干一包豆腐。” 贾森念道，“放进搅拌机。” 
“什么是沥干豆腐？” 莉琪问。
“就是把水倒掉。” 贾森回答。
"Jason, start us off," Miss Shelly said.
"Drain one package of tofu," Jason read. "Put it in the blender."
"What does drain the tofu mean?" Izzie asked.
"It means dump out the water," Jason answered.
“加一根香蕉。” 莉琪念道。
“加可可粉。” 伊坦把可可粉放到搅拌机里。
“加糖。” 尼娜说。
“搅拌。” 波比说，“可以让我按按钮吗？” 
"Add one ripe banana," Izzie read next.
"Add cocoa powder." Ethan put the cocoa in the blender.
"And sugar," said Nina.
"Blend until smooth," Bobby said. "Can I hit the blend button?"
搅拌机发出轰轰声。一开始很吵，后来安静了下来。
“我们该怎么办？” 波比问，“搅拌机是开着的，但是没有在搅拌！布丁不动了。” 
The blender buzzed and hummed. It was very noisy at first, but then it got quiet.
"What do we do?" Bobby asked. "The blender's on, but it's not blending! The pudding stopped moving."
“关掉后用这个刮一刮。” 雪莉老师给他一把勺子，“然后再搅拌。” 
波比按照老师的话做了。当他重新按按钮时，布丁转了起来。
"Turn it off and scrape it with this." Miss Shelly handed him a spoon. "Then blend again."
Bobby followed the instructions. When he turned the blender back on, the pudding swirled around.
“我觉得可以了！” 贾森说。
“关掉搅拌机。每个人拿一个纸杯。把布丁倒进纸杯。我们要把布丁放进冰箱半个小时。” 雪莉老师说。
"I think it's done!" Jason called.
"Turn off the blender. Each of you, take a paper cup. Pour the pudding into the cup. We have to refrigerate the pudding for about thirty minutes," Miss Shelly said.
雪莉老师把托盘放到冰箱里。孩子们在体育馆里打篮球。很快就到回家时间了。弗拉尼校长的头从门口伸进来。
“冰箱里有贴着你们名字的东西。” 她说。
Miss Shelly carried the tray to the refrigerator. The kids played basketball in the gym. Soon it was almost time to go home. Ms. Folani, the principal, stuck her head in the door. .
"These had your name on them in the refrigerator," she said.
“我们的布丁！” 莉琪大喊。
大家坐下来，各拿了一杯。“嗯。” 贾森边吃边说，“真好吃。” 
“闻起来很奇怪。” 波比说。他闻了闻杯子。
"Our pudding!" Izzie cried.
Everyone gathered at the table and grabbed a cup. "Mmm," Jason said with a mouthful of pudding. "This is good."
"It smells funny," Bobby said. He sniffed his cup.
“尝一尝嘛。” 贾森转了转眼睛说，“很好吃的。” 
波比尝了一口。“这不是巧克力布丁的味道吗！” 他说。
“因为这就是巧克力布丁，傻瓜。” 贾森说。
"Just try it," Jason said, rolling his eyes. "It tastes good."
Bobby spooned some pudding into his mouth. "Wait, this tastes like chocolate pudding!" he said.
"That's because it is chocolate pudding, dummy," Jason said.
贾森对雪莉老师说：“谢谢。” 
雪莉老师笑了。“不用谢，贾森。” 
“谢谢您让我尝豆腐。” 波比说，“豆腐没那么难吃。” 
Jason turned to Miss Shelly. "Thanks."
Miss Shelly smiled. "You're welcome, Jason."
"Thanks for making me try tofu," Bobby said. "It's not so bad."
需要准备：
-一包豆腐（约450克）
-一根香蕉
-三分之一杯不加糖的可可粉
-半杯糖
-搅拌机
-几个小杯子
Things You'll Need:
-1 package of tofu (about 340 grams)
-1 banana
-1/3 cup unsweetened cocoa powder
-1/2 cup sugar
-a blender
-small cups
自己试试吧：
1) 沥干豆腐。
2) 把豆腐、香蕉、可可粉和糖放进搅拌机。
3) 搅拌。
4) 倒进六个小杯里。
5) 放进冰箱至少三十分钟。
6) 品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Drain the tofu.
2) Put the tofu, banana, cocoa, and sugar in the blender.
3) Blend.
4) Pour into six small cups.
5) Put in the refrigerator for at least thirty minutes.
6) Enjoy!
尼娜来到儿童中心。大家都在转呼啦圈。“我们今天又转呼啦圈吗？” 尼娜兴奋地问，“莉琪在哪里？” 
Nina arrived at Kids Central. Everyone was hula hooping. "Are we having another hula hoop day?" Nina asked excitedly. "Where's Izzie?"
“莉琪不太舒服。她今天在家。” 雪莉老师告诉尼娜，“我们还要用呼啦圈，但是，是另一种方法。” 
"Izzie wasn't feeling well. So she stayed home from school today," Miss Shelly told Nina. "And we are using hula hoops again, but in a different way."
尼娜脱下背包，坐在波比和伊坦中间。她看着贾森笑了笑。
Nina took off her backpack and sat down between Bobby and Ethan. She smiled at Jason.
“快要到圣诞节了。有谁家里已经做了装饰？” 雪莉老师问。
“我们在前院放了圣诞灯饰。” 尼娜说。
"It's almost holiday season. Did any of you decorate your houses yet?" Miss Shelly asked.
"We put Christmas lights in our front yard," Nina said.
“我们在烛台上放了蜡烛。” 贾森说。
“我们摆好了圣诞树，用灯装饰！” 伊坦说。
“灯和蜡烛都很漂亮。我最喜欢的装饰是用灯做的花环。” 雪莉老师说。
"We put candles in our menorah," Jason said.
"We put up a Christmas tree with lights!" Ethan said.
"Lights and candles are pretty. My favorite decoration is a wreath of lights," Miss Shelly said.
她给大家看一张发光的花环的照片。花环是用灯做的！
“哦！我希望这里也有一个那样的花环。” 尼娜小声说。
“我们马上就会有了。” 雪莉老师说。
She showed them a photo of a bright, white wreath. It was made of lights!
"Oh! I wish we had a wreath like that in here," Nina whispered.
"We will have one soon." Miss Shelly said.
雪莉老师推出一个呼啦圈。尼娜从来没有看过这么大的呼啦圈。“哇！莉琪不在真是太可惜了！” 尼娜说。
“这会成为我们的花环吗？” 波比问。
“对！我们要把灯缠在上面。” 雪莉老师说。
Miss Shelly rolled out a hula hoop. It was the biggest hula hoop Nina had ever seen. "Whoa! Too bad Izzie isn't here to see this!" Nina said.
"Is that going to be our wreath?" Bobby asked.
"Yes! We'll wrap lights around it," Miss Shelly said.
雪莉老师打开一个盒子，拿出一条灯串。“用胶带把一端贴在呼啦圈上。剩下的缠在呼啦圈上。做好以后，连上另一条灯串，继续缠！” 
Miss Shelly opened a box and pulled out a string of lights. "Tape one end to the hula hoop. Wrap the rest of the string around the hoop. When you're done, connect it to another string and keep going!"
大家努力把灯串缠到呼啦圈上。终于，所有盒子里的灯串都用完了。
“我都看不到呼啦圈了！” 尼娜说。
“我们给花环插电吧。” 雪莉老师说。
Everyone worked hard wrapping lights around the hoop. Finally the boxes of lights were empty.
"I can't even see the hula hoop anymore!" Nina said.
"Let's plug in our wreath," Miss Shelly said.
“哇！” 孩子们欢呼起来。
“在太空一定也能看到！” 波比说。
“这里怎么关灯了？” 弗拉尼校长把头伸进来，“没事吧？” 
"Wow!" The kids all cried together.
"I bet you can see it from outer space!" Bobby said.
"Why are the lights out in here?" Ms. Folani stuck her head in the door. "Is everything okay?"
她看到了花环。“真漂亮！这是你们做的吗？” 她问。
“是的。” 尼娜开心地说。雪莉老师看上去也很开心。
“我知道该把这个花环放在哪里！” 弗拉尼校长说。
Then Ms. Folani noticed the wreath. "That's beautiful! Is this the work of Kids Central?" she asked.
"Yep." Nina nodded happily. Miss Shelly looked proud too.
"I know a great spot for that wreath!" Ms. Folani said.
“放在我们学校前面！怎么样？” 校长看着尼娜、波比、伊坦和贾森。
伊坦咧嘴笑了。“太好了！” 
“真棒。” 贾森说。
"On the front of our school! What do you think?" The principal looked at Nina, Bobby, Ethan, and Jason.
Ethan grinned. "Great!"
"Wonderful," Jason said.
“你们是不是少了一个人？” 弗拉尼校长问。
“莉琪今天生病在家。” 尼娜说，“但她一定也会同意的。” 
孩子们把花环抬到校门口。
"Aren't you missing somebody?" Ms. Folani asked.
"Izzie stayed home sick today," Nina said. "But I bet she would say it's a good idea too."
The kids carried the wreath out the front door.
雪莉老师插了电。雪地上反射出温暖的灯光。尼娜想快点给莉琪看看这个大花环。
Miss Shelly plugged it in. The warm glow of the lights reflected off the snowy ground. Nina couldn't wait to show the wreath to Izzie.
需要准备：
-呼啦圈
-几条长灯串
-强力胶带
-电源延长线
Things You'll Need:
-a hula hoop
-several long strings of lights
-duct tape
-an extension cord
自己试试吧：
1) 用胶带把灯串的一端贴在呼啦圈上。
2) 把灯串缠在呼啦圈上。
3) 连上另一条灯串，继续缠绕。
4) 把花环连接到一个电源延长线上。
5) 挂起来，接上电源，观赏美丽的花环！
Do It Youself:
1) Tape one end of a string of lights to the hula hoop.
2) Wrap the string around the hula hoop.
3) Plug in a new string. Start again.
4) Attach an extension cord to your hula hoop wreath.
5) Hang it up, plug it in, and enjoy!
今天是寒假前的最后一天。孩子们互相交换礼物，和对方说再见。
波比走向儿童中心。
It was the last day of school before winter vacation. Kids were exchanging presents and saying good-bye.
Bobby was heading toward Kids Central.
“真不敢相信今天是学校的最后一天。” 贾森说。
“今天不是学校的最后一天。” 波比说，“学校的最后一天在六月。” 
“是今年学校的最后一天！” 贾森说。
"Can you believe it's the last day of school?" Jason asked.
"It's not the last day of school," Bobby said. "The last day of school is in June."
"It's the last school day of this year!" Jason said.
雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。“要过新年了，大家兴奋吗？” 她问，“而且要放假了。” 
“当然了。但是我们今天要做什么？” 贾森说，“今天是今年儿童中心活动的最后一天！” 
Miss Shelly blew her whistle. "Is everyone excited for the new year?" she asked. "And it's vacation."
"Yes, but what are we doing today?" Jason said. "It's the last day of Kids Central for the year!"
“我们要玩儿一个游戏，叫环绕世界。” 雪莉老师拿起塑料垫。每个垫上有一个英文字母。
“太好了！我喜欢环绕世界！” 波比欢呼。
"We're going to play a basketball game called Around the World." Miss Shelly held up plastic place mats. Each one had a letter written on it.
"Yes! I love Around the World!" Bobby cheered.
“这些字母是儿童中心Kids Central的英文拼写。” 雪莉老师说。她把塑料垫放在地上，摆成了半圆形。“先从字母K开始投篮。如果球进了，就移到字母I。谁最靠近字母L，谁就赢！” 
"These letters spell Kids Central," Miss Shelly said. She put the place mats on the floor around the basketball net. They made a big U-shape. "You'll start at K and shoot the basketball. If it goes in, you'll move to I. Whoever makes it closest to L wins!"
“我先来！” 莉琪边说边跑到字母K的位置。雪莉老师给她球，大家排好了队。莉琪投了第一个球。“成功了！” 她欢呼道。
"I'll go first!" Izzie said, rushing to letter K. Miss Shelly tossed her the ball. Everyone lined up, and Izzie took her first shot. "I made it!" she cheered.
每个人都投了两次。现在，他们站在字母D的位置。莉琪又成功了。波比不敢相信莉琪这么厉害。今年，她的篮球进步很大！尼娜没投进。伊坦和贾森投进了。现在轮到波比。
Everyone made their first two shots. Now they were standing at letter D. Izzie made her shot. Bobby couldn't believe how well she was doing. She had gotten good at basketball this year! Nina missed her shot. Ethan and Jason made theirs. Now it was Bobby's turn.
投篮很容易，但是波比很紧张。这是他今年的最后一场比赛！他把球投出去。球碰到篮板，进了。
“移到字母S！” 雪莉老师说。
It was an easy shot, but Bobby felt nervous today. It was his last game of 2011! He shot. The ball hit the backboard and went in.
"On to S!" Miss Shelly said.
字母E就在篮球架前面。莉琪、伊坦、贾森和波比都投进了。
在字母N，贾森没有投进。他抱怨说：“我差点就环绕世界了！” 接着他笑了。“但是，对我来说已经很不错了。” 
E was right in front of the net. Izzie, Ethan, Jason, and Bobby all made their shots.
At N, Jason missed. He groaned. "I almost made it around the world!" Then he smiled. "But I did pretty well for me."
莉琪、伊坦和波比继续投篮。他们都在字母T和R投进了。到了字母A，伊坦没有投进。“什么？” 他大喊，“怎么回事？” 他和尼娜和贾森一起坐在地上。
Izzie, Ethan, and Bobby moved on. They all made T and R. At A, Ethan missed! "What?" he cried. "How did that happen?" He joined Nina and Jason on the floor.
尼娜说：“莉琪加油！” 
“你可以的，波比！” 贾森鼓着掌说。
莉琪对波比笑了笑。“来了！” 她说。她投出球。“耶！” 进球时她大声欢呼起来。
Nina cheered. "Good luck, Izzie!"
"You can do it, Bobby!" Jason said, clapping.
Izzie smiled at Bobby. "Here we go!" she said. She shot. "Whoo!" She cheered when the ball went in.
波比拍着球。他不能输给一个三年级的女生。他投出球……球进了！
“今年的环绕世界冠军是莉琪和波比！” 雪莉老师宣布说，“你们两个都很棒！” 
Bobby bounced the ball. He couldn't get beaten by a third-grade girl. He shot, and . . . the ball went in!
"The Around the World champions this year are Izzie and Bobby!" Miss Shelly announced. "Nice job, you two!"
“谢谢。” 莉琪笑了。
“比赛很精彩。” 伊坦对他们俩说。
莉琪对波比说：“你要小心哦！很快，你就会有一个篮球对手了。” 
"Thanks." Izzie was beaming.
"Good game," Ethan called to both of them.
Izzie turned to Bobby. "You'd better watch out! You'll have a basketball rival soon."
“我知道！” 波比说。这一整个假期，他都要练习篮球了。他要在明年打败莉琪！
"I know!" Bobby said. He was going to practice all vacation long. He wanted to beat Izzie next year!
需要准备：
-放在篮球架附近的字母（或者用来写字母的粉笔）
-篮球
-篮球架
Things You'll Need:
-letters to place around the net (or chalk to write the letters)
-a basketball
-a basketball net
自己试试吧：
1) 在篮球架前把字母摆成半圆形。（如果在室外，也可以用粉笔写。）
2) 从第一个字母开始轮流投球。
3) 如果球进了，就移到下一个字母。如果没进，就出局。
4) 最靠近最后一个字母的人赢。
5) 如果平手，平手的人可以再玩儿一次。这次从最后一个字母开始，移到第一个字母。
Do It Yourself:
1) Place letters around the net in a half circle. (Or write with chalk if you're outside.)
2) Take turns shooting from the first letter.
3) If you make your shot, move to the next letter. If you miss, you're out.
4) The person who makes it closest to the last letter wins.
5) If there is a tie, the winners can play again. This time start at the last letter and move back to the first letter.
放学后，伊坦在走廊看到贾森和波比。

"Yum! I've never made cupcakes," Izzie said.

"Put on your aprons. Things might get messy!" Miss Shelly said. "We're going to use the hand mixer."
"Ooh, that looks fancy," Nina said. "Like something a real chef has! How do you use it?"
“很简单。我们把食材放在碗里。然后启动电动打蛋器。” 雪莉老师说。

“面粉、糖、发酵粉和盐。” 伊坦念道。

"What goes in first?" Jason asked.
"Flour, sugar, baking powder, and salt," Ethan read.
尼娜和莉琪量了面粉和糖。贾森量了发酵粉和盐。“打蛋器在这里！” 波比说。
伊坦用打蛋器混合干食材。
“我去预热烤箱。” 尼娜说。
Nina and Izzie measured the flour and sugar. Jason measured the baking powder and salt. "Here's a whisk!" Bobby said.
Ethan used the whisk to mix the dry ingredients.
"I'll preheat the toaster oven," Nina said.
“现在我们需要湿食材。黄油、鸡蛋、蛋黄、香草和酸奶油。” 贾森念道，“我们怎么准备蛋黄呢？” 
“把鸡蛋打到碗里。” 雪莉老师说。
"Now we need the wet ingredients. Butter, egg, egg yolks, vanilla, and sour cream," Jason read. "How do we get just egg yolks?"
"Crack them into a bowl," Miss Shelly said.
“用叉子把蛋黄舀起来。” 雪莉老师继续说。
贾森把两个鸡蛋打到碗里。然后他把蛋黄分出来。“这很简单！” 
孩子们把其他湿食材加进碗里。
"And scoop up the yolk with a fork," Miss Shelly went on.
Jason cracked two eggs into a bowl. Next he separated the yolks. "That wasn't so hard!"
The kids added the other wet ingredients to the bowl.
尼娜把湿食材倒进干食材里。他们轮流用电动打蛋器。“我们做好纸杯蛋糕了！” 尼娜大喊。
“还没有！还没烤呢！” 雪莉老师说。孩子们把面糊倒进纸杯里。他们把烤盘放进烤箱。
Nina poured the wet ingredients into the dry ingredients. They all took turns using the mixer. "We made cupcakes!" cried Nina.
"Not yet! They're not baked," Miss Shelly said. The kids filled the baking cups with batter. They put the tray in the toaster oven.
“纸杯蛋糕凉了才能放糖霜。” 雪莉老师说，“但是，我昨晚烤了一些纸杯蛋糕。” 她从桌子底下拿出纸杯蛋糕。“我们今天要装饰这些蛋糕。” 
“哇，看上去很好吃！” 伊坦说。
"You can't put icing on cupcakes until they cool," Miss Shelly said. "But I baked some cupcakes last night." She pulled out cupcakes from under the table. "We'll decorate these today."
"Wow, those look good!" Ethan said.
“你妈妈给我看了你的派对邀请。” 雪莉老师说。
“给您看了？” 伊坦惊讶地问。
“卡片很酷！” 雪莉老师笑着说。伊坦放心了。雪莉老师没有被邀请，但她并没有生气。
"Your mom showed me your party invitations," Miss Shelly said.
"She did?" Ethan asked, surprised.
"They were great!" Miss Shelly smiled. Ethan was relieved. She wasn't upset that she wasn't invited.
“这些邀请卡给了我一个想法。” 雪莉老师继续说，“这里有白色的糖霜和蓝色的食物色素。我们要给糖霜加上蓝色，这样就像大海。” 她拿起一个碗，“这是压碎的全麦饼干，它们就像沙子！” 
"They gave me an idea," Miss Shelly continued. "Here is white icing and blue food coloring. We'll dye the icing so it looks like the ocean." She held up a bowl. "These are crushed graham crackers. They look like sand!"
“还有小冲浪板！” 波比说。
伊坦把蓝色的糖霜涂在纸杯蛋糕上。他把半个蛋糕粘上全麦饼干。然后，他把冲浪板放在又蓝又甜的大海上。这个生日纸杯蛋糕真酷！
"And there are even little surfboards!" Bobby said.
Ethan spread blue icing on his cupcake. He dipped half the cupcake in the graham crackers. Then he stuck a surfboard in the blue, sugary ocean. It was one cool birthday cupcake!
需要准备：
-一杯半面粉
-一杯糖
-一勺半茶匙发酵粉
-四分之一茶匙盐
-115克黄油
-一个鸡蛋，两个蛋黄
-一勺半茶匙香草香精
-115克酸奶油
-烘焙用纸杯
-糖霜
Things You'll Need
-1 ½ cups flour
-1 cup sugar
-1 ½ teaspoons baking powder
-1/4 teaspoon salt
-115 grams butter
-1 egg plus 2 egg yolks
-1 ½ teaspoons vanilla
-115 grams sour cream
-paper baking cups
-icing
自己试试吧：
1) 混合面粉、糖、发酵粉和盐。
2) 在另一个碗里混合黄油、鸡蛋、蛋黄、香菜香精和酸奶油。把湿食材加进干食材里，用电动打蛋器混合。
3) 把纸杯放进烤盘。 把面糊倒到纸杯四分之三的地方。
4) 用177度烤20-25分钟。
5) 等纸杯蛋糕变凉。
6) 把糖霜涂在纸杯蛋糕上。
7) 品尝美食！
Do It Yourself:
1) Mix the flour, sugar, baking powder, and salt.
2) In another bowl mix butter, egg, egg yolks, vanilla, and sour cream. Add wet mixture to dry mixture and mix with a hand mixer until smooth.
3) Place baking cups in a baking tray. Fill the baking cups 3/4 full with batter.
4) Bake at 177˚C for 20-25 minutes.
5) Allow the cupcakes to cool completely.
6) Spread icing onto the cupcakes.
7) Enjoy!
今天很热。波比流着汗，走向儿童中心。
尼娜和莉琪用纸扇子互相扇风。
It was a hot day. Bobby was sweating as he walked to Kids Central.
Nina and Izzie were using paper fans to wave each other.
“今天我们做什么？” 波比问雪莉老师，“我们可以去室外吗？” 
“今天这么热，我正要带你们出去。” 雪莉老师笑着说，“拿一个水瓶，跟我走吧！” 
"What are we doing today?" Bobby asked Miss Shelly. "Please, can we go outside?"
"I wouldn't keep you inside on such a hot day." Miss Shelly smiled. "Grab a water bottle, and follow me!"
孩子们跟着雪莉老师来到足球场。“今天我们要玩儿水枪抓人游戏。” 雪莉老师说。
“水枪抓人游戏？” 莉琪说，“那是什么？” 
“一个人负责抓。” 雪莉老师说。
The kids followed Miss Shelly out to the soccer field. "Today we're going to play squirt freeze tag," she said.
"Squirt freeze tag?" Izzie repeated. "What's that?"
"One person will be 'it,'" Miss Shelly began.
“抓的人必须抓到其他所有人。 抓人需要把水喷到这个人身上。如果你被喷到了，就被‘冻住了’，不能动！所有人都被抓到以后，我们再决定谁来抓人。” 雪莉老师看着大家，“明白了吗？” 
"Whoever is 'it' must tag everyone else. You tag someone by squirting them with water. If you are tagged, You must freeze! You cannot move! After everyone is tagged, we'll choose another 'it.'" Miss Shelly looked at everyone. "Understand?"
孩子们点点头。“谁先抓呢？” 伊坦问。
雪莉老师笑了。“我在想一个1到20之间的数字。” 她说，“猜猜是什么数字。” 
“11！” 波比大喊。
The kids nodded. "Who gets to be 'it' first?" Ethan asked.
Miss Shelly grinned. "I'm thinking of a number between one and twenty," she said. "Guess what number it is."
"Eleven!" Bobby called out.
“6。” 贾森说。
“15。” 莉琪说。
“19。” 伊坦说。
“10。” 尼娜说。
"Six," said Jason.
"Fifteen," guessed Izzie.
"Nineteen," Ethan said.
"Ten," guessed Nina.
“是11。” 雪莉老师说，“波比，你来抓！” 
“耶！” 波比欢呼。大家把水瓶放下来。“我们先站成一个圆圈。波比，你站在中间。” 雪莉老师站在圆圈外面。
"It was eleven," Miss Shelly said. "Bobby, you're 'it!'"
"Yeah!" Bobby cheered. Everyone else put down their water bottles. "We'll start by standing in a circle. Bobby, you stand in the middle." Miss Shelly stood outside the circle.
“各就各位，预备，开始！” 雪莉老师吹了吹哨子。
波比去追伊坦。但是，伊坦太快了！波比决定等会儿再来抓他。他转身，看到尼娜。他快速跑向尼娜。
"On your mark, get set, go!" Miss Shelly blew her whistle.
Bobby chased after Ethan. But Ethan was fast! Bobby decided to try to catch him later. He turned around and spotted Nina. He sprinted toward her.
“啊！” 尼娜被水喷到后，尖叫了一声。
“你要冻住！” 莉琪刚好跑过，提醒她。
现在波比在追莉琪。他拿起水瓶……嗞！莉琪被冻住了。水从她的额头流下来。
"Eek!" Nina squealed as she got squirted with water.
"You have to freeze!" Izzie reminded her, running by.
Now Bobby was after Izzie. He raised his water bottle . . . Squirt! Izzie was frozen. Water dripped down her forehead.
波比追着贾森。贾森看上去又热又累。“这里有水让你凉一凉！” 波比大喊。他把水喷到贾森背后。
“哈哈！水真凉！” 贾森笑了。他被冻住了。
Bobby ran after Jason. Jason looked hot and tired. "Here's some water to cool you off!" Bobby shouted. He squirted his friend in the back.
"Ha-ha! That's cold water!" Jason giggled and then froze.
“你一定抓不到我！” 伊坦大喊。他跑过足球场。波比在后面追着他。
伊坦跑来跑去。波比靠近过一次，但伊坦躲开了！
"Bet you can't catch me!" Ethan cried. He ran across the soccer field. Bobby raced after him.
Ethan ran one way and then the other. Once, Bobby got close enough to squirt. But Ethan ducked out of the way!
“啊！” 波比突然能量爆发。他以最快的速度奔跑。伊坦的脚拌了一下！嗞！水从伊坦的背后流下来。
“你们都被冻住了！” 波比开心地喊道。
“游戏结束！” 雪莉老师说。
"Ahhh!" Bobby got a burst of energy. He ran as fast as he could. Ethan stumbled! Squirt! Water dripped down Ethan's back.
"You're all frozen!" Bobby shouted happily.
"Game over!" Miss Shelly called.
波比很热，气喘吁吁。
“真好玩儿！” 尼娜说。
“我们再来一次吧！” 伊坦看着雪莉老师。
“好。” 雪莉老师说，“波比，你来决定谁抓人。” 
Bobby was hot and breathing hard.
"That was fun!" Nina said.
"Let's play again!" Ethan looked at Miss Shelly.
"Sure," Miss Shelly said. "Bobby, please pick our next 'it.'"
“好。我在想一个1到20之间的数字。” 波比说完笑了。平时他不喜欢在抓人游戏里被抓。但是，现在被水喷到一定很凉快！
"Okay. I'm thinking of a number between one and twenty," Bobby said. He smiled. Usually he didn't like getting caught in a game of tag. But it would feel great to get squirted with water now!
需要准备：
-水瓶
-水
Things You'll Need:
-water bottles

自己试试吧：
1) 水瓶里装满水。
2) 选择一个人抓人。
3) 抓人需要喷水到这个人身上。被喷到水的人必须停住不动。每个人都被喷到后，游戏结束。

Do it Yourself:
1) Fill water bottles with water.
2) Choose one person to be "it."
3) Whoever is "it" must tag everyone else by squirting them with water. When people are tagged, they must stand still. The game is over when everyone is tagged.
4) Choose another person to be "it" and play again!
“你们会自己做午餐吗？” 雪莉老师问。伊坦、波比、贾森、莉琪和尼娜坐在地毯上。今天他们又来到了儿童中心。

Jason smiled. That would make his busy parents happy!

Nina and Ethan chose tuna salad. Jason, Bobby, and Izzie chose egg salad.
“鸡蛋沙拉组，现在要煮鸡蛋。把鸡蛋放进一锅水里。我来打开炉子。” 雪莉老师说。

Ethan picked up a can opener and placed it on the can. Twist, twist, twist. He opened his can.
"How'd you do that?" Nina asked. "I turned the handle, but nothing happened!"
“可能是刀片没有切到金属。” 伊坦说，“要这样紧紧抓住把手。” 伊坦做给她看。

"Maybe the blade didn't cut through the metal," Ethan said. "Squeeze the handles shut, like this." Ethan showed her how.

“鸡蛋好了！可以剥皮切碎了。” 波比说。

"The eggs are ready! Time to peel and chop," Bobby said.

“Be careful, Jason,” Miss Shelly warned. She watched him chop an egg. "You know, getting help is still okay sometimes," she added.
做鸡蛋沙拉的孩子们把鸡蛋和蛋黄酱混合起来。
做金枪鱼沙拉的孩子们把金枪鱼和蛋黄酱混合起来。
“我们准备好做三明治了！” 孩子们同时说。
The egg salad makers mixed their eggs with their mayonnaise.
The tuna salad makers mixed their tuna with their mayonnaise.
"We're ready to make sandwiches!" the two groups cried at the same time.
雪莉老师哈哈大笑。“小厨师们真棒！” 孩子们把沙拉涂在面包上。然后把另外一片面包放在上面。
Miss Shelly laughed. "Good work, chefs!" The kids spread their salads onto pieces of bread. Then they put another piece of bread on top.
“现在我们要把三明治包起来。你们明天可以带去作午餐！” 雪莉老师把纸分给大家。“这是一种特别的纸。它会帮三明治保鲜。” 
"Now we'll wrap your sandwiches. You can bring them for lunch tomorrow!" Miss Shelly handed out sheets of paper. "This is special paper. It will keep your sandwiches fresh."
孩子们用纸包住三明治。但是，贾森包得不太顺利。“我包不好！” 他说。

They folded the paper around the sandwiches. But Jason was having trouble. "Mine doesn't work!" he said.
"Can I help you, Jason?" Miss Shelly asked. Jason nodded. "Try putting your sandwich in the center of the paper," she said.
要回家了，贾森跑到妈妈身边。“我做了明天的午餐。全是我自己做的！” 他看了看雪莉老师。“雪莉老师帮了我。” 他补充说，“有时候，获得一点帮助也没关系。” 
When it was time to go home, Jason ran to his mom. "I made my lunch for tomorrow. All by myself!" He looked at his teacher. "But Miss Shelly helped," he added. "Sometimes a little help is okay."
需要准备：

鸡蛋沙拉
-六个煮熟的鸡蛋
-三分之一杯蛋黄酱
-两茶匙芥末酱
-四汤匙切好的黄瓜

金枪鱼沙拉
-两罐金枪鱼(每罐85克)
-四汤匙蛋黄酱
-两汤匙切好的黄瓜
-半茶匙盐
Things You'll Need:

Egg salad
-6 boiled eggs
-1/3 cup mayonnaise
-2 teaspoons mustard
-4 tablespoons chopped cucumber

Tuna salad
-2 cans (about 85 grams each) of tuna in water or oil
-4 tablespoons mayonnaise
-2 tablespoons chopped cucumber
-1/2 teaspoon salt
自己试试吧：

鸡蛋沙拉
1) 在锅里煮十分钟鸡蛋。沥干后放到冷水里。
2) 把蛋黄酱和芥末酱混合起来。加入黄瓜。
3) 剥鸡蛋，切鸡蛋。
4) 加入鸡蛋。

金枪鱼沙拉
1) 沥干一罐金枪鱼罐头。
2) 把蛋黄酱、芥末酱和黄瓜混合起来。
3) 加入金枪鱼。
Do it Yourself:

For the egg salad:
1) Boil the eggs in a pot for 10 minutes. Drain and place them in cold water to cool.
2) Mix the mayonnaise and mustard. Add cucumbers.
3) Peel eggs. Chop eggs.
4) Add the eggs.

For the tuna salad:
1) Drain the can of tuna.
2) Mix the mayonnaise, salt, and cucumber.
3) Add the tuna.
莉琪跳着去儿童中心。“呱、呱、呱。” 她呱呱叫着。她在想自己的青蛙，呱呱。呱呱今天在兽医那里。

Miss Shelly held up a beanbag. "To start, toss this beanbag onto a square. Hop to the square on one foot. If you hop on a line, you are out! When you get to the square, do the activity. If you can't do the activity, you're out."
“我先来！” 莉琪马上说。
