"Good news, sweetie. Gurpy ate five worms today. Everything is okay!" her mom said happily.
Izzie jumped up and hugged Nina. "I knew those frog jumps would work! Thanks, Nina."
需要准备：
-粉笔
-沙包，小石子或者棍子
Things You'll Need:
-chalk
-a beanbag, stone, or stick
自己试试吧：
1) 用粉笔在地板上画出跳房子游戏用的格子。
2) 在格子里写下各种好玩儿的动作。
3) 扔沙包。
4) 单脚跳到沙包掉到的格子里，做格子里写的动作。
5) 踩到线，就出局！
6) 不能完成动作，就出局！
7) 开心玩儿游戏吧！
Do It Yourself:
1) Draw a hopscotch board on the ground with chalk.
2) In the boxes write fun activities that players can do on the spot.
3) Toss the beanbag.
4) Hop on one leg to wherever it lands and do the activity.
5) If you step on a line, you're out!
6) If you can't do the activity, you're out!
7) Have fun!
尼娜很伤心。她不喜欢学校的最后一天。这意味着她会有两个月见不到朋友们了。
Nina was sad. She didn't like the last day of school. It meant she wouldn't see her friends for two months.
“我想知道今天会做什么活动。” 伊坦对尼娜说。他们往儿童中心走去。
“是啊。” 波比也加入他们，“今天是我在儿童中心的最后一天了。” 
"I wonder what we'll do today," Ethan said to Nina. They were walking to Kids Central.
"Yeah," Bobby said, joining them. "It'll be my last day of Kids Central. Ever."
“为什么？” 尼娜惊讶地问。
“这个秋天，我会加入男生足球队。放学后我需要训练。” 波比说，“再也不能玩儿四方格或者跳房子游戏了。” 他笑了，但尼娜觉得他很伤心。
"What do you mean?" Nina asked, surprised.
"In the fall I'm joining the Sunny Dale boys' soccer team. I'll have practice after school," Bobby said. "No more Four Square or hopscotch for me." He laughed, but Nina thought he looked sad.
雪莉老师把一大张纸铺在体育馆的地板上。“今天我们要画一幅特别的壁画。” 她说。
“为什么特别呢？” 贾森问。
“你们不只是画画，你们还会在画里。” 雪莉老师说。
Miss Shelly laid a huge piece of paper on the gym floor. "Today we're going to make a special mural," she said.
"What's special about it?" Jason asked.
"You won't just make it. You'll be in it," Miss Shelly said.
“在画里？” 莉琪问。
“你们要躺在纸上。你的搭档会用记号笔把你的身体描画下来。然后，我们用旧布剪出衣服，粘在上面。我们还要用线做头发！” 雪莉老师笑着说。
"In it?" Izzie asked.
"You're going to lie down on the paper. A partner will trace your body with a marker. Then we'll cut clothes from old cloth to glue on top. We even have yarn to make your hair!" Miss Shelly smiled.
“你愿意作我的搭档吗？” 尼娜问莉琪。
“当然了。” 莉琪说。
“我们一起吧。” 波比指着贾森和伊坦说。
"Will you be my partner?" Nina quickly asked Izzie.
"Of course," Izzie said.
"We're going to work together," Bobby said, pointing to Jason and Ethan.
尼娜脱下鞋子。她躺在纸上。“把我描出来吧！” 她说。莉琪开始沿着尼娜的腿和手臂描起来。“哈哈！好痒！” 莉琪画好以后，尼娜看了看画。“哇。我有那么大吗？” 
Nina took off her shoes. She lay down on the paper. "Trace me!" she said. Izzie started to trace around Nina's legs and arms. "Ha-ha! That tickles!" When Izzie was finished, Nina looked at her outline. "Wow. I'm that big?"
“轮到我了。” 莉琪说。这次，尼娜画莉琪。然后，女生们开始选布料。她们要做衣服。
“哦，这个很漂亮。” 尼娜拿起印着花的布料。
"My turn," Izzie said. This time Nina traced Izzie. Then the girls looked through the piles of cloth. They had to choose their outfits.
"Ooh, this is pretty." Nina held up some flower print cloth.
“我要用这个做我的衬衫。” 莉琪拿起带圆点的布料。
她们把布放在画上。她们开始测量。两个女生都选了蓝色的布料来做牛仔裤。
男生们在选做头发的线。
"I'll make this my shirt." Izzie held up some polka-dot cloth.
They laid the cloth on their outlines. They started to measure. Both girls chose blue cloth to make jeans
The boys were choosing yarn for their hair.
“莉琪，给你。这个很像你的头发！” 伊坦拿起一团黄色的线。
“尼娜，这个给你，接着！” 波比把一团黑色的线扔给她。
"Here, Izzie, this looks like your hair!" Ethan held up a ball of yellow yarn.
"Nina, here's one for you. Catch!" Bobby tossed her a ball of black yarn.
女生们用笔画脸，然后用线做头发。在壁画里，孩子们都笑着手拉手。
“明年我不会来儿童中心了。” 贾森突然说，“我爸爸会在家工作。” 
The girls drew their faces and glued yarn hair onto their outlines. In the mural all the kids were smiling and holding hands.
"I won't be in Kids Central next year," Jason said suddenly. "My dad is going to work from home."
“你也不来？” 尼娜简直不敢相信。今天可真是让人伤心的一天。
“我会想念儿童中心的。但是，帮我爸爸做晚饭也会很有意思。” 贾森继续说。
"You too?" Nina couldn't believe it. Today was turning into a very sad day.
"I'll miss Kids Central. But it'll be fun to help my dad cook dinner!" Jason went on.
“我们也会想你的。” 雪莉老师说，“女生们呢？” 
莉琪耸耸肩。“我还不知道，但我想来！” 
“我喜欢儿童中心。” 尼娜大声说，“明年我还想回来！” 
"We'll miss you too," Miss Shelly said. "What about you girls?"
Izzie shrugged. "I don't know yet. But I hope I'll be here!"
"I like Kids Central," Nina said a little loudly. "I want to come back next year!"
雪莉老师笑了。“很高兴你能这么说！现在我们把壁画挂到墙上吧。” 
“明年的儿童中心会完全不一样了。” 尼娜想，“但是我会记住今年，今年是最棒的一年！” 
Miss Shelly laughed. "I'm glad to hear that! Now let's hang this mural in the hall."
"Next year Kids Central will be totally different," Nina thought. "But I'll always remember this year as the best year ever!"
需要准备：
-壁画纸或牛皮纸
-记号笔
-线、布、纽扣等
-剪刀
-胶水
Things You'll Need:
-mural paper or butcher paper
-markers
-yarn, cloth, buttons, etc.
-scissors
-glue
自己试试吧：
1) 躺在纸上。
2) 请朋友用记号笔把你描画下来。
3) 用旧布剪出衣服。
4) 画脸。
5) 用线做头发。
6) 开心地完成壁画吧！
Do It Yourself:
1) Lie down on the paper.
2) Ask a friend to trace your body with a marker.
3) Cut out pieces of cloth to "dress" your outline.
4) Draw your face.
5) Use yarn to make your hair.
6) Have fun drawing the mural!
波比跟妈妈挥手说完再见，走进了学校。他觉得来学校有点别扭。他不是来上课，也不是来儿童中心，而是来儿童中心夏令营！
Bobby waved good-bye to his mom and walked inside the school. It felt a little weird to be there. He wasn't going to class. And he wasn't going to Kids Central. He was going to Kids Central summer camp!
波比在体育馆里看到了一桶水气球。一个高高的男人穿着一件T恤，上面写着 “儿童中心夏令营” 。他还戴着一顶帽子。
“你好！” 男人说，“你是波比吧？” 
In the gym Bobby saw a bucket of water balloons. A tall man was wearing a T-shirt that said: "Kids Central Summer Camp." He also had on a baseball cap.
"Welcome, camper," the man said. "Let me guess. Bobby?"
“是的。” 波比说，“您是邓恩老师吗？” 波比的妈妈说过这个夏天雪莉老师不在。
邓恩老师笑了。“是的。雪莉老师是我的朋友，她说过你会成为篮球明星。” 
"That's me," Bobby said. "Are you Mr. Dunn?" His mom had told him Miss Shelly wouldn't be teaching this summer.
Mr. Dunn smiled. "That's me. My friend Miss Shelly told me all about you. I hear you're on your way to becoming a basketball star."
波比想笑，但忍住了。“没有啦。” 他说。
突然，体育馆的门开了，两个女生冲了进来。“尼娜！莉琪！你们也来夏令营了？” 波比说。
“是啊。” 莉琪说。
Bobby tried not to grin. "Nah," he said.
Suddenly the gym door burst open and two girls rushed in. "Nina! Izzie! You guys are here for the summer too?" Bobby said.
"The whole summer," Izzie said.
“我很期待。” 尼娜说，“好想快点开始。” 两个女生咯咯笑着。她们看了看新老师。“您好，邓恩老师。” 她们说。
“你们好！” 邓恩老师说，“我们在等——” 
"I can't wait," said Nina. "Even though I'm here already." The two girls giggled. Then they looked up at their new teacher. "Hi, Mr. Dunn," they said.
"Nice to meet you," Mr. Dunn said. "We're just waiting for—"
“贾森和伊坦！” 莉琪大喊。
“对。” 邓恩老师很惊讶。
“我的意思是，贾森和伊坦来了！” 莉琪指了指正走过来的贾森和伊坦。
"Jason and Ethan!" Izzie squealed.
"That's right." Mr. Dunn looked surprised.
"No. I mean Jason and Ethan are here!" Izzie pointed as Jason and Ethan walked over to them.
“太好了。贾森、伊坦，我是邓恩老师。大家跟我出去吧。” 邓恩老师带着他们来到外面。“我们要玩儿‘认识你’扔水气球游戏，两人一组。” 
莉琪和尼娜先组成了一组。
"Great. Jason, Ethan, I'm Mr. Dunn. Everybody, follow me outside." Mr. Dunn led them to the blacktop. "We're going to have a get-to-know-you water balloon toss. Please get into pairs."
Izzie and Nina paired up first.
贾森和伊坦组成了一组。“波比，你可以作我的搭档吗？” 邓恩老师问。
波比开心起来。“当然可以！” 
“我们先面对面。” 邓恩老师说。
Then Jason and Ethan paired up. "Bobby, will you be my partner?" Mr. Dunn asked.
Bobby's face brightened. "Sure!"
"We'll start facing each other," Mr. Dunn explained.
“一个人拿着气球。扔气球时，要说一句关于自己搭档的话。我举个例子。” 邓恩老师看着波比，“波比喜欢篮球！” 他一边说，一边把水气球扔给波比。波比接到球。
"One person holds the balloon. When you toss the balloon, say something you know about your partner. For example," Mr. Dunn looked at Bobby. "Bobby likes basketball!" he said as he tossed Bobby the water balloon. Bobby caught it easily.
“接到球后，往后退一步。然后扔回给你的搭档，并说一句关于你搭档的话。明白了吗？” 邓恩老师看看大家。
“明白了！” 莉琪举起一个气球。
"When you catch the balloon, take one step back. Then toss it to your partner and say something about him or her. Get it?" Mr. Dunn looked at everyone.
"Got it!" Izzie held a balloon over her head.
“小心，莉琪。” 尼娜说，“如果气球破了，我们就出局了。” 
“尼娜说得对。” 邓恩老师说，“最后拿着气球的那一组就赢了。” 
"Be careful, Izzie," Nina said. "If you burst that balloon, we're out of the game."
"Nina's right," said Mr. Dunn. "The last pair with a water balloon is the winner."
搭档们面对面地站好了。
“贾森喜欢做饭！” 伊坦大喊着把气球扔出去。
“伊坦喜欢大海！” 贾森把气球扔回去。
“尼娜很会跳绳。” 莉琪说。
The partners lined up facing each other.
"Jason likes to cook!" Ethan called, tossing the balloon.
"Ethan likes the ocean!" Jason threw it back to his partner.
"Nina's good at jumping rope," Izzie said.
“莉琪很会逗别人笑。” 尼娜说。
波比还没有把气球扔出去。“不好了，邓恩老师。我不了解您啊！” 他说。
“你一定了解一些。” 邓恩老师说，“想一想。” 
"Izzie's good at making people laugh," Nina said.
Bobby still hadn't thrown his balloon. "Uh-oh, Mr. Dunn. I don't know anything about you," he said.
"Sure, you do," Mr. Dunn said. "Think."
“您骑自行车来夏令营！” 莉琪说。
“您喜欢园艺！” 伊坦说。
波比笑了。“您是雪莉老师的朋友！” 孩子们欢呼起来。“这个夏天一定会很有趣！” 波比想。
"You ride your bike to camp!" Izzie said.
"You like to garden!" Ethan said.
Bobby smiled. "You're friends with Miss Shelly!" The kids cheered. "This summer is going to be fun!" Bobby thought.
需要准备：
-大约12个水气球
Things You'll Need:
-about a dozen water balloons
自己试试吧：
1）在气球里装水，放在桶里或地上。
2）面对自己的搭档站着。其中一个人拿气球。
3）每次把气球扔给搭档时，说出关于他/她的事情。(不要说不友好或者不真实的话！)
4）每接到一次气球，就后退一步。
5）气球破了，那一组就出局。
6）最后拿着气球的那一组就赢了！
Do It Yourself:
1) Fill the balloons with water and place them in a bucket or on the ground.
2) Stand facing your partner. One of you holds a balloon.
3) Each time you toss the balloon to your partner, say something you know about him/her. (Make sure it's nothing mean or untrue!)
4) Each time you catch the balloon, take a step back.
5) If one of you bursts the balloon, your team is out.
6) The team that gets the farthest away from each other without breaking its balloon wins!
贾森不能集中精力。他甚至不能走路。他的腿太痒了！昨天晚上，他和爸爸在户外吃晚餐。他们回室内后，贾森的身上全是蚊子咬的包。
Jason couldn't concentrate. He couldn't even walk. His legs were so itchy! Last night he and his dad had eaten dinner outside. By the time they went inside, Jason was covered in mosquito bites.
他很痒。“我受不了了！” 贾森把腿上的包给大家看。
“哇。” 尼娜说，“看上去很痒。” 
“你应该用驱蚊水的。” 莉琪说。
Itchy, horrible mosquito bites. "I can't take it anymore!" Jason showed everyone the red spots on his legs.
"Wow," said Nina. "They look itchy."
"You should have used bug spray," said Izzie.
“我用不了驱蚊水。” 贾森说。
“为什么？” 尼娜问。
“因为我对化学药品过敏。” 贾森皱着眉头说。
“那你今天真幸运！” 邓恩老师说。
"I can't use bug spray," Jason said.
"Why not?" Nina asked.
"Because I'm allergic to the chemicals." Jason frowned.
"Well then it's your lucky day!" said Mr. Dunn.
“幸运？” 贾森说，“被蚊子咬有什么幸运的？” 
“我们今天要做驱蚊水。” 邓恩老师解释说，“是一种天然的驱蚊水。” 
“真的吗？” 贾森不敢相信，“怎么做呢？” 
"Lucky?" Jason echoed. "What's lucky about mosquito bites?"
"We're making Campers' Bug Spray today," Mr. Dunn explained. "It's all-natural bug spray."
"Really?" Jason didn't believe it. "How do you make it?"
“邓恩老师是一名化学老师。他会给我们解释的。对吗，邓恩老师？” 波比看着老师。
“是的。” 邓恩老师点了点头，“坐下吧。” 
"Mr. Dunn is a chemistry teacher. So he can explain what to do. Right, Mr. Dunn?" Bobby looked at his teacher.
"That's the plan." Mr. Dunn nodded. "Have a seat."
“这里有些瓶子里是非常浓的油，叫精油。混合几种精油，就能做出赶走蚊子的气味儿。” 邓恩老师清了清嗓子，“我是说，让蚊子飞走。” 
尼娜咯咯笑。她喜欢邓恩老师的小幽默。
"In some of these bottles are very strong oils called essential oils. By mixing certain essential oils, you can make a scent that will send mosquitoes running." Mr. Dunn coughed. "I mean, flying."
Nina giggled. She liked Mr. Dunn's silly jokes.
“气味儿会不会很难闻？” 伊坦问。
“应该不会。等一下你们就会知道了。” 邓恩老师说，“每个人都拿一个喷水瓶，写上名字。这就是你自己的驱蚊水瓶。” 
"But won't the scent make us want to run away too?" Ethan asked.
"I don't think so. But you can decide for yourself in a minute," Mr. Dunn said. "Everyone, take one of the spray bottles and write your name on it. This will be your bug spray bottle."
贾森小心地写上自己的名字。
“首先，我们要加基础油。” 邓恩老师说，“今天我们的基础油是橄榄油。先加基础油，精油才不会太浓。” 
Jason carefully wrote his name on a bottle.
"First we have to add what's called a base oil," said Mr. Dunn. "Today our base is olive oil. We'll start with that so the essential oils aren't so strong."
“而且不容易过敏，对吗？” 贾森问。
“对。有的人会因为精油太浓长小红点儿。” 邓恩老师说，“所以我们要仔细测量精油的量。” 大家把橄榄油倒进去。
"And so we won't be allergic?" Jason asked.
"Yes. Some people get a rash from too much strong essential oil," Mr. Dunn said. "So we're going to carefully measure how much we put in." Everyone poured in the olive oil.
接着，邓恩老师拿起一个瓶子。“看到这个瓶子的特殊盖子了吗？这个滴管可以一滴一滴地测量桉树油。” 邓恩老师滴了几滴在自己手上。他搓了搓手，让孩子们闻。
Next Mr. Dunn held up a bottle. "See this bottle's special top? The dropper helps us measure the eucalyptus oil one drop at a time." Mr. Dunn put a few drops in his hand. Then he rubbed his hands together and held them up for the kids to smell.
“我喜欢这个气味。” 莉琪说，“闻上去很清新。” 
伊坦闻了闻。“哇！气味儿真浓。” 
“滴二十滴到你的瓶子里。” 邓恩老师说。
贾森眯了眯眼睛。“我觉得它会刺激我的眼睛。” 他说。
"I like it," Izzie said. "It smells clean and fresh."
Ethan took a sniff. "Wow! That's strong."
"Put twenty drops into your bottle," Mr. Dunn said.
Jason squinted. "I feel like it might sting my eyes," he said.
“它确实会刺激你的眼睛！” 邓恩老师说，“所以一定要小心，弄完精油后不要碰自己的眼睛。” 
“接下来放什么呢？” 波比问。
邓恩老师拿起另一个瓶子。“香茅精油。” 
"The oil could sting your eyes!" Mr. Dunn said. "So be very careful not to touch your eyes after handling essential oils."
"What do we put in next?" Bobby asked.
Mr. Dunn held up another bottle. "Citronella essential oil."
“我们家后院有香茅蜡烛。” 尼娜说。
“香茅可以驱蚊。” 邓恩老师说，“所以，这个也加二十滴。摇一摇，就做好了！下次出去的时候，可以喷在胳膊和腿上。” 
"We have citronella candles in our backyard," Nina said.
"Citronella keeps mosquitoes away," Mr. Dunn said. "So add twenty drops of this too. Shake it up and you're done! Next time we go on a hike, you can spray it on your arms and legs."
“贾森，今晚出去的时候可以试试。应该没有蚊子咬你了。” 邓恩老师说。
“我会试试的。” 贾森说，“但是，我已经没有地方让蚊子咬了！” 
"Try this if you go outside tonight, Jason. I don't think any mosquitoes will bother you," Mr. Dunn said.
"I'll try it," Jason said. "But after last night, I have no skin left to bite anyway!"
需要准备：
-一个90毫升的喷水瓶
-两汤匙橄榄油
-桉树精油
-香茅精油
-用来测量的滴管
Things you'll need:
-a spray bottle, about 90 ml
-2 tablespoons olive oil
-eucalyptus essential oil
-citronella essential oil
-a dropper for measuring
自己试试吧：
1）把橄榄油倒入喷水瓶。
2）加20滴桉树精油。
3）加20滴香茅精油。
4）好好儿摇一摇。
5）喷在胳膊和腿上，涂抹好。
6）洗手，尽情享受户外活动吧！
Do it Yourself:
1) Pour the olive oil into the spray bottle.
2) Add 20 drops of eucalyptus essential oil.
3) Add 20 drops of citronella essential oil.
4) Shake well.
5) Spray the mixture onto your arms and legs and rub in well.
6) Wash your hands, and then enjoy being outside without getting bitten by mosquitoes!
“妈妈，再见！” 尼娜抱了抱妈妈。今天她们一起走到儿童中心夏令营。
“再见，宝贝儿。我和秀晶阿姨三点来接你。” 妈妈说。
"Bye, Mom." Nina hugged her mother. They had walked together to Kids Central Summer Camp today.
"Bye, sweetie. I'll be back with Aunt Sujong at three o'clock to pick you up," Nina's mom said.
“耶！” 今天，韩国的秀晶阿姨会来。她会在尼娜家里住一个星期。“希望今天做手工。这样我就可以送给秀晶阿姨。” 尼娜想。
"Yay!" Nina's Aunt Sujong was arriving from Korea today. She was going to stay at Nina's house for one week. "I hope we make a craft today. Then I can give it to Aunt Sujong," Nina thought.
体育馆里，邓恩老师拿着一箱草莓。莉琪在猜里面有多少个草莓。“二十二。” 莉琪说，“我猜有二十二个。” 
“你觉得呢，尼娜？” 邓恩老师问。
In the gym Mr. Dunn was holding a box of strawberries. Izzie was trying to guess how many strawberries were in it. "Twenty-two," Izzie said. "I bet there are twenty-two."
"What do you think, Nina?" Mr. Dunn asked.
尼娜看了看。“我们今天要做食物吗？” 她失望地问，“我们不做手工吗？” 
“我们要做冰沙！” 贾森猜道。
“不对。但是你们也会喜欢的。” 邓恩老师说。
Nina looked in the box. "Are we making food today?" she asked, disappointed. "We're not making a craft?"
"We're making smoothies!" Jason guessed.
"Nope. But you'll like this too," Mr. Dunn said.
“我们要做草莓酱。” 邓恩老师说，“你们做过草莓酱吗？” 
“我没做过。” 波比说，“但是我妈妈做过。” 
“很快，你就可以帮她了。很简单的。” 邓恩老师说。
"We're making strawberry jam," Mr. Dunn said. "Have any of you made jam before?"
"I haven't," Bobby said. "But my mom has."
"Soon you'll know how to help her. It's easy," said Mr. Dunn.
“首先，我们要把这些草莓洗一洗。伊坦，你可以帮忙洗吗？你还可以数一数到底有几个。” 邓恩老师说。
“三十二个！” 伊坦告诉他们。
波比笑了。“莉琪，你猜错了！” 
"First we need to wash these strawberries. Ethan, will you wash them please? You could count the berries too," Mr. Dunn said.
"Thirty-two!" Ethan announced as the kids put on their aprons.
Bobby grinned. "You weren't even close, Izzie!"
“切、切、切。” 尼娜切掉草莓的顶部。“无聊、无聊、无聊。” 她不开心地说。
切好以后，邓恩老师把草莓分到五个碗里。他拿起一些捣碎器。“每个人拿一个。” 
"Chop, chop, chop." Nina cut off green top after green top. "Boring, boring, boring," she said grumpily.
When they were done, Mr. Dunn put the strawberries into five bowls. He held up some potato mashers. "Everyone, grab one of these."
“太好了！” 伊坦欢呼道，“我们要把东西捣碎！” 
“哈哈，太好玩儿了！” 莉琪用捣碎器捣碎草莓。
“也很脏。” 尼娜指了指莉琪的胳膊。上面全是草莓汁。
"All right!" Ethan cheered. "We're mashing stuff!"
"Ha-ha. This is fun!" Izzie pressed her masher into the berries.
"And messy." Nina pointed to Izzie's arms. They were covered in strawberry juice.
“太好了。可以开始煮了。” 邓恩老师说。
“煮？要煮草莓吗？” 尼娜问。
“是的。加热可以让糖融化。” 邓恩老师解释说，“现在把碗里的草莓倒进锅里。” 
"Terrific. Those berries look ready to cook," said Mr. Dunn.
"Cook? You cook the berries to make jam?" Nina asked.
"Yes, and the heat helps to melt the sugar," Mr. Dunn explained. "Now empty your bowls into this pot."
“然后加入一杯半白糖。” 波比念道。
“加两汤匙柠檬汁。” 莉琪说。
“用小火加热到糖融化。” 贾森念道，“我们怎么知道糖融化了没有呢？” 
"Then add one and half cups of sugar," Bobby read.
"And two tablespoons of lemon juice," Izzie said.
"Heat on low until the sugar melts," Jason read. "How will we know when it melts?"
“现在糖是白色的。当它融化时，我们就看不到它了。它会变成透明的糖浆！” 邓恩老师解释说。
尼娜看着锅里。“它在融化！” 
“现在把火开大，煮沸！” 邓恩老师说。
"The sugar is white now, right? When it melts, we won't be able to see it anymore. It turns into clear liquid—syrup!" Mr. Dunn explained.
Nina peeked into the pot. "I can see it melting!"
"Now turn up that stove and let it boil!" Mr. Dunn said.
“别忘了搅拌。” 贾森把一个木头勺子给尼娜。
“颜色真好看。” 尼娜边搅拌边说。
“现在可以把酱倒进罐子里了。” 邓恩老师说，“然后，我们把它放凉，再放入冰箱。” 
"Don't forget to stir." Jason handed Nina a wooden spoon.
"It's a pretty color," Nina said, stirring.
"I think we can pour the jam into the jars now," Mr. Dunn said soon. "Then we'll let the jars cool and put them in the refrigerator."
几个小时后，邓恩老师从冰箱里拿出罐子。“这里有一些蝴蝶结和卡片。你们可以装饰罐子，然后送给别人。” 他说。
“送给别人？” 尼娜想。突然，她笑了。
A few hours later, Mr. Dunn took the jam jars out of the refrigerator. "We have some ribbons and cards. You can decorate your jar and give it to someone sweet," he said.
"Give it to someone?" Nina thought. Suddenly she smiled.
活动结束了。尼娜跑出来跟妈妈和秀晶阿姨打招呼。“秀晶阿姨！” 她大喊，“这个酱是送给您的。” 
“谢谢你，尼娜。” 秀晶阿姨抱着她说。她看了看卡片。上面写着：“甜甜的东西给甜甜的人。” 
At the end of the day, Nina ran to greet her mom and aunt. "Aunt Sujong!" she cried. "This jam is for you."
"Thanks, Nina," Aunt Sujong said, hugging her. Then she read Nina's card. It said: "Something sweet for someone sweet."
需要准备：
-四杯草莓
-一个大碗
-捣碎器或大叉子
-一杯半白糖
-两汤匙柠檬汁
-干净的罐子
Things you'll need:
-4 cups strawberries
-a large bowl
-a potato masher or a large fork
-1 ½ cups white sugar
-2 tablespoons lemon juice
-clean jam jars
自己试试吧：
1）把草莓洗干净，切掉顶部。
2）把草莓放进大碗里，用捣碎器或者叉子捣碎。
3）把草莓、白糖和柠檬汁放在锅里混合。
4）小火加热，让糖融化。
5）把火开大，煮沸。煮二十分钟，经常搅拌。
6）关火，把酱倒入干净的罐子里，放凉。
7）把罐子在冰箱里放几个小时。
8）和吐司或酸奶一起吃！
Do it Yourself:
1) Wash the strawberries and cut off the green tops.
2) Place the strawberries in a large bowl and mash them with a potato masher or a large fork.
3) Mix the strawberries, sugar, and lemon juice in a pot.
4) Heat on low until the sugar melts.
5) Turn up the heat and bring to a boil. Cook for about twenty minutes, or until the mixture thickens. Stir often.
6) Remove from heat and pour the jam into clean jam jars. Let the jars cool.
7) Place the jam jars in the refrigerator for a few hours.
8) Eat with toast or yogurt and enjoy!
莉琪在走廊里看到伊坦。她觉得伊坦比其他男生友好。她希望有一天可以和他做搭档。
体育馆里，邓恩老师坐在桌边。
Izzie saw Ethan in the hallway ahead of her. She thought he was nicer than the other boys. She hoped they could be partners at Kids Central Camp one day.
In the gym Mr. Dunn was sitting at a table.
“这些细绳是用来做什么的？” 伊坦问。
“今天我们要做友情手链。” 邓恩老师说。
“友情手链。” 莉琪想，“我可以做一个给——” 
“手链是女孩子戴的！” 波比说。
"What's the string for?" Ethan asked.
"Today we're making friendship bracelets," Mr. Dunn said.
"Friendship bracelets," Izzie thought. "I could make one for—"
"Bracelets are for girls!" said Bobby.
“不是的。” 伊坦说，“在我加利福尼亚的那个学校，每个人都戴。” 
“我姐姐和她的朋友们戴友情手链。” 波比说，“我觉得很可笑。” 
"No, they're not," Ethan said. "At my school in California everyone wore them."
"Well, my sister and her friends wear friendship bracelets," Bobby said. "I think they're goofy."
“一点儿都不可笑。” 邓恩老师说，“这是一种表达友情的方式。” 他看着波比说，“如果有朋友送你一条手链，你不能剪断它。只要你们还是朋友，就要一直戴着。” 
"They are not goofy," Mr. Dunn said. "They're part of a meaningful tradition." He looked at Bobby. "When a friend gives you a bracelet, you should never cut it off. You wear it for as long as the two of you remain friends."
“我已经等不及了！” 莉琪说。
“先选三种颜色。” 邓恩老师说。
“真好看。” 莉琪想拿蓝色的细绳，伊坦也想拿。两只手碰到了。
"I can't wait to make mine!" said Izzie.
"First choose three colors," Mr. Dunn instructed.
"This is pretty." Izzie reached for a bundle of blue thread. But her hand bumped into another hand reaching for the same one.
“对不起。” 伊坦小声说，“我选另一个吧。” 
“你们可以选同一种颜色。” 邓恩老师说，“莉琪，剪六十厘米下来，然后把剩下的给伊坦吧。” 
"Sorry," Ethan mumbled. "I'll pick a different one."
"You can choose the same color," Mr. Dunn said. "Izzie, measure out sixty centimeters, and then give Ethan the thread."
大家量好并剪下六条细绳。接着，邓恩老师告诉他们怎么做。“在一端的十厘米处打个结。接着，把这一端贴在桌子上。然后，按颜色分好细绳。每种颜色要有两条细绳。” 
Everyone measured and cut six strands of thread. Then Mr. Dunn showed them what to do. "Now tie a knot ten centimeters from one end. Next tape that end to the table. After that separate the strands by color. There should be two strands of each color."
“准备好了！” 尼娜说。
邓恩老师点了点头。“从最左边的细绳开始编。用它在每一条细绳上都打结后，再从左边开始。明白了吗？” 邓恩老师问。
"Now we're ready to weave!" said Nina.
Mr. Dunn nodded. "Start with the strand all the way to the left. Use it to tie a knot around the string next to it.
“明白了！” 莉琪说。她觉得需要编很长时间。但她想今天就编完。
Keep going all the way across. Once you've knotted each string, start again on the left. Do you understand?" Mr. Dunn asked.
"Yep!" Izzie said. This looked like it would take a while. She wanted to finish hers today.
“开始编吧！如果需要帮忙，可以叫我。” 邓恩老师说。
“我的是做给你的。” 尼娜小声对莉琪说。
莉琪看着她，咽了一口口水。“谢谢。” 然后她接着编。编呀、编呀、编呀。
"Weave away! Ask me if you need help," said Mr. Dunn.
"I'm making mine for you," Nina whispered to Izzie.
Izzie looked at her friend and swallowed. "Thanks." Then she got back to work. Knot, knot, knot. Knot, knot, knot. Start again.
她终于编好了。她感觉手很酸，脖子也很疼。但是手链看上去很不错。
“好了。该出去踢足垒球了。” 邓恩老师说。
Finally she was done. Izzie's hands were cramping and her neck hurt from bending over. But her bracelet looked great.
"Okay, campers. Time to get out into that sunshine and play some kickball," Mr. Dunn said.
“如果你的手链还没做好，可以带回家做。” 邓恩老师补充说。接着，他看到莉琪的手链。“做得好，莉琪。” 他说，“你今天非常努力。” 
“谢谢。” 莉琪说。她做好了手链，很开心。
"If you're not done with your bracelets, you can finish them at home," Mr. Dunn added. He leaned over and looked at Izzie's bracelet. "Nice job, Izzie," he said. "You worked hard today."
"Thanks," said Izzie. She was glad she was finished.
东西都整理好以后，孩子们排队准备出去。莉琪站在伊坦的后面。她看到伊坦把还没编好的手链放进口袋。
“伊坦。” 莉琪叫他。
When everything was put away, the kids lined up to go outside. Izzie was behind Ethan at the end of the line. She saw Ethan stuff his unfinished bracelet in his pocket.
"Hey, Ethan." Izzie poked his arm.
“我的手链是做给你的。你会戴吗？” 她小声说。
“当然了。谢谢你，真的很好看。” 他告诉莉琪。
“太好了。” 莉琪笑着把手链戴在他的手腕上，然后跑走了。
"I made my bracelet for you. Will you wear it?" she mumbled.
"Sure. Thanks, that's really nice," he told Izzie.
"Cool." Grinning, Izzie tied the bracelet on his wrist. Then she ran to the blacktop.
需要准备：
-三种颜色的细绳，大约六十厘米
-尺子或者卷尺
-剪刀
-强力胶带
Things you'll need:
-three different colors of embroidery thread, about 60 centimeters each
-a ruler or measuring tape
-scissors
-strong tape
自己试试吧：
1）每种颜色剪两条细绳。每条细绳六十厘米长。
2）在六条细绳的一端一起打个结。
3）把打结的一端贴在桌子或者坚硬的表面上。
4）从最左边的细绳开始，在它旁边的细绳上打结。
5）每条细绳都打结后，再从最左边开始。
6）当细绳剩下十厘米时，再把六条细绳一起打个结。
7）把友情手链送给朋友。还可以做一个一样的给自己！
Do it Yourself:
1) Cut two strands of each color of thread. Make sure each strand is 60 centimeters long.
2) Tie the six strands together by making a knot at one end.
3) Tape the knotted end to a table or hard surface.
4) Begin with the string at the left. Use it to tie a knot around the string directly to its right.
5) Repeat with each string. Then go back to the string at the left and start again.
6) When there are only 10 centimeters of loose string left, tie another knot.
7) Give your friendship bracelet to a friend. If you want, you can make a matching one for yourself!
伊坦很享受这个下午。儿童中心夏令营的孩子们走在树林里，观察大自然。伊坦喜欢树林。邓恩老师正在给他们看苔藓和各种野花。
“这是什么？” 伊坦问。
Ethan was having a great afternoon. The Kids Central campers were on a nature hike in the woods. And Ethan loved the woods. Mr. Dunn was showing them moss and different kinds of wildflowers.
"What's this?" Ethan asked, pointing to a small yellow flower.
“是毛茛花。” 尼娜说，“真可爱。” 
“今天我们什么都不摸。” 邓恩老师严厉地说，“我们只在路上观察，伊坦！” 
“哈哈，伊坦！” 波比嘲笑他说，“你有麻烦了！” 
"That's a buttercup," Nina said. "It's so cute."
"We're not touching anything today," Mr. Dunn called out sternly. "We're just observing—from the trail, Ethan!"
"Ha-ha, Ethan!" Bobby teased him. "You got in trouble!"
第二天，邓恩老师让大家画昨天看到的花。
“伊坦，你的腿怎么了？” 莉琪指着伊坦腿上的小红点说。伊坦一直在挠。
The next day Mr. Dunn asked everyone to draw a flower from the nature hike.
"Hey, Ethan. What's on your leg?" Izzie pointed to red welts on Ethan's legs. Ethan was scratching like crazy.
“我不知道。但是真的很痒。” 伊坦说。
“糟了。看上去是毒藤。” 邓恩老师说。
“我们也会被传染吗？” 贾森离伊坦远远的。
"I don't know. But it's so itchy," Ethan said.
"Uh-oh. It looks like you've got poison ivy," Mr. Dunn said.
"Are we going to get it too?" Jason backed away from Ethan.
“贾森，你不用担心。伊坦昨天离开了小路。” 邓恩老师说。
“对不起，老师。” 伊坦小声说，“我应该跟大家一起走的。” 
"Jason, you probably don't have to worry. But Ethan was wandering off the trail yesterday," Mr. Dunn said.
"Sorry, Mr. Dunn," Ethan mumbled. "I should have stayed with the rest of the group."
邓恩老师点了点头。“你的皮肤碰到了毒藤的油。” 
“油？” 贾森说，“什么油？” 
“植物有油吗？” 尼娜问。
Mr. Dunn nodded. "The oil from the poison ivy plants must have gotten on your skin."
"Oil?" said Jason. "What oil?"
"Plants have oil?" Nina asked.
“看来我们要学一学毒藤的知识了。” 邓恩老师说，“我们先去图书馆吧。我们可以在那里找关于毒藤的知识。你们等会儿再继续画画。” 邓恩老师带着孩子们走进了图书馆。
"It sounds like you campers need to learn about poison ivy," Mr. Dunn said. "Let's visit the library. We can look up facts about poison ivy. You can finish your pictures later." Mr. Dunn led the kids into the empty school library.
“我们在电脑上找！” 男生们说。
“我们在书上找！” 莉琪和尼娜说。
邓恩老师打电话给伊坦的妈妈，告诉她关于伊坦的皮疹。然后，他给伊坦一个冰袋。冰袋起了一点作用。
"We'll research on the computers!" the boys said.
"We'll look for books," Izzie and Nina said.
Mr. Dunn called Ethan's mom to tell her about the rash. Then he gave Ethan an ice pack for his itchy leg. It helped a little bit.
一个小时后，孩子们聚在地毯上。“谁来说一下自己找到的内容？” 邓恩老师问。
波比举起手。“我发现毒藤是一种带有油的植物，会引起皮疹。” 
An hour later the kids gathered on the rug. "Who wants to share what you found out?" Mr. Dunn asked.
Bobby raised his hand. "I found out that poison ivy is a plant with an oil that causes a rash."
“触摸植物或者触摸碰过植物的东西就会起皮疹。比如鞋子。” 波比说，“或者宠物。” 
“没错。” 邓恩老师说。
"You can get the rash from touching the plant or touching something that touched the plant. Like your shoes," Bobby explained. "Or your pet."
"That's absolutely right," Mr. Dunn said.
“有时，第二天才会起皮疹。” 贾森补充说。
“对。皮疹一般是12到48个小时之后出现的。” 邓恩老师说，“但并不是每一个人都这样。” 
“我们找到了一些照片。” 尼娜拿起一本书。
"You might not see the rash until the next day," Jason added.
"Right again. The rash usually doesn't appear until 12 to 48 hours later," Mr. Dunn said. "And not everyone gets it."
"We found some pictures of the rash." Nina held up a book.
“我们还找到了治疗方法。涂止痒膏和炉甘石乳液，再用燕麦洗冷水澡。” 莉琪说。
贾森在急救箱里找了找。“我找到炉甘石乳液了！” 
“我要涂这个粉色的东西吗？” 伊坦皱着眉头说。
"We also found out how to treat it. Put anti-itch cream and calamine lotion on it, and take cold, oatmeal baths," Izzie said.
Jason looked through the first aid kit. "I found calamine lotion!"
"I have to put that pink stuff on me?" Ethan said unhappily.
“这是毒藤的照片。当我们看到它时，要避开它。” 莉琪给大家看照片。
“这里有句话可以帮大家记忆：三片叶子不要碰。” 邓恩老师说。
"Here's what the poison ivy plant looks like. So we can all avoid it when we see it." Izzie showed them pictures.
"There's a special saying to help you remember: Leaves of three, let them be," Mr. Dunn said.
“我要是早点知道就好了。” 伊坦说，“我很痒。我要用燕麦洗冷水澡。还要涂粉色的乳液。唉！我再也不会走到路外边去了！” 
"Too bad I didn't know all this before," Ethan said. "I'm itchy. I have to take cold oatmeal baths. And I have to put on pink lotion—ugh! I'll stay on the trail from now on!"
需要准备：
-冰袋
-炉甘石乳液
-止痒膏
-用燕麦洗冷水澡
Things You Need:
-an ice pack
-calamine lotion
-anti-itch cream
-oatmeal bath treatment
毒藤引起的皮疹应该这样治疗：
1）用肥皂清洗手和感染部位。
2）把冰袋放在受感染的皮肤上。
3）轻轻拍干皮肤，涂上炉甘石乳液和止痒膏。
4）如果真的很痒，可以用燕麦洗冷水澡。
5）不要挠！（以后要避开长毒藤的地方！）
What to Do If You Get a Poison Ivy Rash:
1) Wash your hands and the affected area with soap and water.
2) Place an ice pack over the affected skin.
3) Pat the skin dry, and then apply calamine lotion or anti-itch cream.
4) If you're really itchy, you can take a bath in oatmeal.
5) Try not to scratch! (And in the future, do your best to avoid places where poison ivy grows!)
莉琪带着一个小桶来到体育馆。她刚度假回来。“我们要把这些藏起来吗？” 她问邓恩老师，“在大家来之前？” 
邓恩老师看了看满满一桶的贝壳。“好。走吧！” 
Izzie hurried into the gym with her beach bucket. It was her first day back at camp after vacation. "Should we hide these?" she asked Mr. Dunn. "Before everyone else gets here?"
He looked into the bucket of seashells. "Yep. Let's go!"
莉琪和邓恩老师走到操场上。他们把贝壳藏在秋千下面和球门后面。他们还把一些贝壳藏在篮球架和树的附近。其他孩子们到的时候，他们刚好藏好。
Izzie and Mr. Dunn went out to the playground. They hid Izzie's shells under the swings and behind the soccer goals. They hid more shells around the basketball nets and trees. They finished just as the other campers arrived.
邓恩老师向大家说明了今天的活动。“今天我们要寻宝。我不能告诉你们找的是什么。” 
“那我们要怎么找呢？” 波比问。
邓恩老师笑了。“我给你们一个提示。它们是来自海洋的。找到五个后，就放到桌子上。” 
On the blacktop Mr. Dunn explained the day's activity. "Today you'll hunt for secret treasures. I can't tell you what they are."
"Then how are we supposed to find them?" Bobby asked.
Mr. Dunn grinned. "I'll give you a clue.
“是的。” 莉琪补充说，“我们要做很酷的东西！” 
“祝你们好运！” 邓恩老师挥手说。
The treasures are from the sea. When you've found five items, bring them to the table."
"Yeah," Izzie added. "We're going to make something cool!"
"Good luck!" Mr. Dunn waved the hunters off.
“提示一点儿用都没有。” 贾森抱怨说。
“有用。我知道我们要找的是什么。” 波比说，“我已经想到了！” 
就在这时，尼娜大喊：“我找到了！” 
"That clue wasn't very helpful," Jason complained.
"Yes it was. I know what we're hunting for," Bobby bragged. "I figured it out!"
Just then Nina shouted, "I found something!"
男生们跑到尼娜那里。她在秋千旁边。“小心别踩到了！” 她大叫，“它们很容易碎的！” 
“是什么？” 贾森问。
尼娜伸出手。“是贝壳。” 
The boys ran to Nina, who was by the swings. "Watch where you step!" she squealed. "They're delicate!"
"What are?" Jason asked.
Nina opened up her hands. "The seashells."
大家知道了要找什么，所以贝壳很容易都被找到了。很快，大家都回到了桌子旁。
“我们找到了贝壳。” 伊坦说，“现在呢？” 
Once the campers knew what they were looking for, the seashells were easy to find. Soon they were all at the table.
"We've got our seashells," Ethan said. "Now what?"
“嗯。” 邓恩老师说，“莉琪帮我们从沙滩捡来了这些贝壳。她爸爸还在每个贝壳上打了孔。就让莉琪来说一说今天的手工吧。” 
莉琪自豪地笑了。“我们要做海风风铃。” 
"Well," Mr. Dunn said, "Izzie kindly collected these seashells from the beach for us. And her dad drilled tiny holes in each one. So I'll let her explain today's craft."
Izzie beamed proudly. "We're making sea-breeze wind chimes."
她拿起一个风铃。“我们家去年做了这个。有四个贝壳和一个海玻璃。这个是漂木。” 
“什么是漂木？” 波比问。
“在海上漂了很久的木头。” 伊坦说。
She held up a chime. "My family made this one last year. It has four shells and one piece of sea glass. And this is real driftwood."
"What's driftwood?" asked Bobby.
"Wood that's been floating in the sea for a while," said Ethan.
“我也带了一些漂木给你们。” 莉琪补充说。
“谢谢。” 尼娜说，“我们要怎么做风铃呢？” 
“很简单。你只需要把所有东西都绑在漂木上就可以了。” 莉琪说，“首先，我们要做挂钩。
"I brought you guys some driftwood too," Izzie added.
"Thanks," Nina said. "How do we make the chimes?"
"It's easy. You just have to tie everything to the wood," Izzie said. "First we have to make the hanger.
剪一条大约六十厘米的细绳。把绳子的一端绑在漂木的一端。然后把细绳的另一端绑在漂木的另一端。接着，我们就可以挂贝壳了。
Cut a piece of string about sixty centimeters long. Tie one end of the string around one end of your stick. Then tie the other end of the string to the other end of the stick. Now we're ready to attach the shells to the chime.
剪五条大约三十厘米的细绳。把绳子穿过贝壳上的孔，打个结。然后把绳子的另一端绑在漂木上。所有贝壳都用这种方法绑好。” 
Cut five pieces of string about thirty centimeters long each. Thread one string through the hole in one shell and knot it. Then tie the other end of the string to the driftwood. Keep doing this until all your shells are hanging down from the wood."
孩子们把贝壳摆好，剪绳子，开始做手工。
“要把结打紧。” 邓恩老师说。
“莉琪，谢谢。” 伊坦说，“这让我想起了加利福尼亚的海滩。” 
The campers laid out their shells, cut string, and got to work.
"Make sure the knots are tight," Mr. Dunn said.
"Hey, Izzie, thanks," Ethan said. "This reminds me of the beach in California."
“不客气。” 莉琪说。她把一个粉红色的小贝壳绑在风铃上，然后笑了。今天她把海边度假的快乐分享给了朋友们。这种感觉就和海风一样清爽！
"You're welcome," Izzie said. She tied a small pink scallop shell to her wind chime and smiled. Today she shared a fun part of her beach vacation with her friends. And that felt as cool as a sea breeze!
需要准备：
-五个打过孔的贝壳
-一根漂木或者木棍
-一条大约250厘米的细绳
-剪刀
Things you'll need:
-about five seashells with tiny holes drilled in them
-a skinny piece of driftwood or a stick
-about 250 centimeters of string
-scissors
自己试试吧：
1）从海滩上捡来贝壳，或者在手工店里购买。
2）请大人帮忙在贝壳上打孔。
3）找一根漂木或者木棍。最好是三十到四十厘米的细木棍。
4）剪一条六十厘米长的细绳做挂钩。
5）把绳子的一端绑在木棍的一端。
6）把绳子的另一端绑在木棍的另一端。
7）剪五条大约三十厘米的细绳挂贝壳。
8）绳子一端穿过贝壳的孔，另一端绑在木棍上。所有贝壳都用这种方法绑好。
9）把海风风铃挂在走廊或窗前。每当风吹动时，就想起海边！
Do it Yourself:
1) Collect seashells at the beach or purchase them from a craft store.
2) Ask an adult to drill a tiny hole in each seashell.
3) Find a piece of driftwood or a regular stick. A skinny stick about thirty to forty centimeters works best.
4) To make the chime's hanger, cut a piece of string about sixty centimeters long.
5) Tie one end of the string to one end of the stick.
6) Tie the other end of the string to the other end of the stick.
7) To hang the shells, cut five pieces of string about thirty centimeters long.
8) Thread one end through the hole in a seashell. Tie the other end around your stick. Repeat until all your seashells have been added to the chime.
9) Hang your sea-breeze wind chime on your porch or by a window. Think of the beach every time the wind blows!
儿童中心夏令营的孩子们在外面吃午餐。但是贾森没有吃。
“怎么了，贾森？” 邓恩老师问，“你今天不饿吗？” 
The Kids Central summer campers were eating lunch outside. But Jason wasn't eating.
"What's the matter, Jason?" Mr. Dunn asked. "You're not hungry today?"
“我很饿。” 贾森指着西葫芦说，“但是我不想吃西葫芦了。我家菜园里有很多西葫芦。我妈妈每天都让我吃！” 
邓恩老师很惊讶。“真的吗？你不想吃西葫芦了？” 
"I'm hungry," Jason said, poking at his zucchini. "But I'm really sick of zucchini. We have a lot of it in our garden now. My mom makes me eat it every day!"
Mr. Dunn looked shocked. "Really? You're sick of zucchini?"
“我很喜欢西葫芦。” 波比说。
“不难吃啊。” 莉琪补充说，“就吃了吧，贾森。” 
“等等！” 邓恩老师突然用手盖住贾森的西葫芦。
"I love zucchini," said Bobby.
"It's not that bad," Izzie added. "Just eat it, Jason."
"No wait—don't!" Mr. Dunn suddenly covered Jason's zucchini with his hand.
大家都看着邓恩老师。
“怎么了？” 贾森问。
“我刚想起来。” 邓恩老师说，“我们今天要做的东西可能会帮到你！” 
Everyone stared at Mr. Dunn.
"What's wrong?" asked Jason.
"I just remembered," said Mr. Dunn. "We're making something today that might help you enjoy the zucchini!"
邓恩老师收好午餐。“我要去拿些东西。” 他说。
“我可以帮忙吗？” 贾森问。
“当然了。你可以帮我拿东西。” 邓恩老师说。
Mr. Dunn started cleaning up his lunch. "I'm going to grab our supplies," he said.
"Can I help?" Jason asked.
"Sure. You can help me carry some things," Mr. Dunn said.
邓恩老师在体育馆里拿起两个袋子。他指了指桌上的插座和搅拌机。“你可以帮我拿那些吗？” 他问。
“可以。” 贾森把东西拿起来，跟着邓恩老师走。
In the gym Mr. Dunn picked up two bags. He pointed to the long extension cord and blender on the table. "Can you carry those things?" he asked.
"Sure." Jason picked them up and followed Mr. Dunn outside.
“我们要做一个神奇的蘸酱。” 邓恩老师说，“它可以让西葫芦，还有其它你不喜欢的蔬菜变得好吃。” 
伊坦皱了皱眉。“包括花菜？” 他问。
"We're going to make a magic dip," Mr. Dunn said. "It will help you eat zucchini and other vegetables you don't like."
Ethan made a sour face. "Even cauliflower?" he asked.
“当然包括花菜。” 邓恩老师回答说。
“神奇的蘸酱里有什么呢？” 伊坦问。
“贾森，请给大家看看袋子里有什么。” 邓恩老师把袋子放在桌子上。
"Absolutely cauliflower," Mr. Dunn answered.
"What's in the magic dip?" Ethan asked.
"Jason, please show us what's in the grocery bag." Mr. Dunn set the bags on the table.
“橄榄油和烤杏仁。” 贾森边说边从袋子里把东西拿出来，“柠檬和蒜。” 
“就这些？” 伊坦惊讶地问。
“不。” 贾森说，“这里还有盐和胡椒。” 
"Olive oil and roasted almonds," Jason said, pulling two items out of the bag. "A lemon and garlic cloves."
"That's it?" Ethan asked, surprised.
"Nope," said Jason. "Here's salt and pepper too."
“男生们。” 邓恩老师说，“你们可以挤出三汤匙的柠檬汁吗？女生们，你们可以量出三分之一杯的橄榄油吗？” 
"Boys," said Mr. Dunn, "can you squeeze the lemon to make three tablespoons of juice? Girls, can you measure one-third cup of olive oil?"
邓恩老师给搅拌机插上电。“我们可以把所有东西都放进去。” 他说，“烤杏仁、蒜、柠檬汁和橄榄油。” 
轰隆隆！搅拌机旋转着。“现在我们加入盐和胡椒。” 邓恩老师说。
Mr. Dunn plugged in the blender. "We can put in everything at once," he said. "Roasted almonds, garlic, lemon juice, and olive oil."
Whrr! The blender hummed and spun. "Now let's add a little salt and pepper," said Mr. Dunn.
“搅拌得很好了。” 莉琪说。
“刚好可以做蘸酱。” 邓恩老师说。他拿了一点给贾森。“再试试西葫芦。” 
大家都看着贾森。
"Nice and creamy," said Izzie.
"Perfect for our dip," said Mr. Dunn. He spooned some dip onto a plate and handed it to Jason. "Now try your zucchini."
Everyone watched Jason dip a zucchini stick into the dip.
“怎么样？” 莉琪问，“喜欢吗？” 
贾森慢慢吃着。“喜欢！” 他大喊，“很好吃。试试吧！” 他对大家说。
"Well?" Izzie burst out. "Do you like it?"
Jason squeezed his eyes as he chewed the zucchini. "Yes!" he cried at last. "It's good. Try some!" he told everyone.
“成功了！” 波比说。
“贾森，我们该叫它什么名字呢？” 邓恩老师问。
“儿童中心夏日蘸酱。” 贾森说，“我在家里也要做一次！” 
"Success!" said Bobby.
"Jason, what should we name our magic dip?" asked Mr. Dunn.
"Kids Central Summer Dip," Jason said. "But I'm going to make this at home too!"
需要准备：
-三分之一杯烤杏仁
-两块蒜
-三汤匙柠檬汁
-三分之一杯橄榄油
-一点盐和胡椒
-搅拌机
-西葫芦、胡萝卜、花菜等新鲜蔬菜
Things you'll need:
-1/3 cup roasted almonds
-2 garlic cloves
-3 tablespoons fresh lemon juice
-1/3 cup olive oil
-dash of salt and pepper
-blender
-fresh vegetables such as zucchini, carrots, and cauliflower for dipping
自己试试吧：
1）把前四种材料放进搅拌机，搅拌到均匀。
2）加一点盐和胡椒，搅拌。
3）把蘸酱放进碗里。
4）蘸你最喜欢的夏日蔬菜吃！
Do It Yourself:
1) Combine the first four ingredients in a blender and blend until smooth and creamy.
2) Add a dash of salt and pepper and stir.
3) Transfer the dip to a bowl.
4) Dip in your favorite summer vegetables, and enjoy!
